# Drill — Reward Feeling System (Main Analysis)

> **Ăn ngon → "sướng." Hiểu bài toán → "sướng." Nghe nhạc hay → "sướng."**
> **Cùng 1 từ. Cùng 1 hệ opioid. Nhưng cảm giác KHÁC NHAU.**
>
> Ăn ngon có vị, có mùi, có ấm bụng.
> Hiểu toán có "click", có nhẹ nhõm, có "đẹp quá."
> Nghe nhạc có rung, có flow, có "hay quá."
>
> Framework nói: Reward = body-base confirm signal (H10, 03-Reward.md).
> Opioid là primary, nhưng KHÔNG phải exclusive (v0.2 refined).
> CHƯA nói: tại sao 3 cái "sướng" trên KHÁC NHAU?
>
> File này drill: **"Hương vị" reward đến từ đâu?**
> Và mở rộng: Flow, eureka, psychedelics, limerence, dissociation
> — 8 mechanisms "loss of self", 6 PFC modes, abstract × body-base.
>
> **v0.3 thêm**: 2 TYPES reward signal — Type A (Evaluative, opioid)
> vs Type B (Direct State, non-opioid). PFC Control Spectrum.
> Dissociation = overcontrol. Psychedelic = undercontrol. Both = "loss of self."
>
> **v0.4 thêm**: A/B = ORTHOGONAL dimension, không phải 6th profile.
> 5 Profiles × A/B ratio. A Gates B mechanism. B = evolutionary floor.
> Preview fidelity A > B. Development lifecycle gradient (B→A→B).
>
> **v0.5 thêm**: Neonate sweet taste = Type A₀ (hardware-installed opioid).
> Type A có Complexity Gradient: A₀ (hardware binary) → A₃ (expert abstract).
>
> **v0.6 thêm**: B habituates via receptor adaptation (modality-specific), NOT VTA.
> Preview fidelity = f(cortical proportion): B ~5-15% → A₃ ~60-80%.
> A Gates B = posterior-to-anterior insula gradient process (not single locus).
>
> **v0.7 thêm**: Temporal Stack Model — onset B ~20ms → A₃ ~1-5s (layers build).
> A₃ afterglow = 4 overlapping curves (consolidation + relief + background cascade + verification).
> Compound interaction = Conditional Model: substrate overlap → subadditive (A+A) vs
> superadditive (A+B with positive gate). Relief = system-state multiplier.
> Temporal overlap determines compound quality. BFM §4 additive model → REFINED.
>
> **v0.8 thêm**: System Reconsolidation = EMERGENT from individual reconsolidation.
> Hierarchy-flat → chunk-to-chunk TOPOLOGY modifiable → lasting structural change.
> Mirror of trauma compilation (same power, opposite direction). 4 conditions.
> Strategy A→B = ESCAPE POSSIBILITY ASSESSMENT × compiled history × developmental window.
> Caregiver trauma = triple impossibility (can't fight/flee/lose attachment).
> R15↔R16 bridge: system reconsolidation can address B default at foundation level.
>
> **"Reward = body-base confirm signal. Type A evaluates (A₀→A₃ gradient).
> Type B directly confirms (non-opioid, receptor-adapted, preview-resistant).
> A modulates B via insula gradient. B persists when A fails.
> Compound = norm. Interaction = f(substrate × gate × relief × temporal overlap).
> Defense: A (fight/flee) vs B (dissociate) = f(escape × history × development)."**

```
⭐ FILE NÀY TRONG FRAMEWORK:

  DRILL FILE — không phải mechanism file, không phải observation file.
  = Ghi lại PHÁT HIỆN từ drill session, để refine sau.

  WHAT framework ĐÃ CÓ (mạnh):
    → H10: KHI NÀO reward fire (5 preconditions) — 03-Reward.md
    → 7-step: MECHANISM reward fire — Dopamine-Reward-Rejection.md
    → 4 trục: direction × magnitude × source × chunk dynamics — Body-Feedback-Mechanism.md
    → 10+ channels: NGUỒN feeling — Feeling-Sources.md
    → Quality model: f(chunk library × compile context) — Feeling.md §8

  WHAT framework THIẾU (drill này bổ sung):
    → ❶ Reward Profiles: 5 "hương vị" reward chưa formalize
    → ❷ PFC Selective Reallocation: flow ≠ PFC offline, chưa trong §7
    → ❸ Compile Context → QUALITY: P5 chưa drill sâu tới reward quality
    → ❹ 4 Mechanisms "Loss of Self": chưa so sánh tường minh
    → ❺ Developmental Path: childhood P5 → adult flow capacity chưa connect
    → ❻ Expert Phenomenology: data chưa integrate

  READING GUIDE:
    Đọc TRƯỚC: 03-Reward.md (H10), Feeling.md §6-§8, PFC-Function.md §7
    Đọc SAU: Drill-Reward-Feeling-Cases.md (expert accounts + cases)

  FILE STRUCTURE:
    §1-§3: Reward Profiles (core finding)
    §4: Compile Context → Quality (P5 extension)
    §5-§6: PFC + Flow State (mechanism finding)
    §7: Coherence Reward (specific profile analysis)
    §8: Developmental Path (childhood → adult)
    §9-§12: Cross-check, GAPs, Assessment, Refs
```

## §1 — CÂU HỎI GỐC + TÌNH TRẠNG FRAMEWORK HIỆN TẠI

### §1.1 — Câu hỏi trigger drill

```
CÂU HỎI GỐC (session 2026-05-09):

  "Tưởng tượng ăn ngon, hiểu bài toán, nhìn tranh đẹp, nghe nhạc hay,
   tưởng tượng mùi hương — cùng 1 loại reward feeling,
   hay cảm giác khác nhau?"

  "Khác nhau do nguồn gốc body-input khác nhau,
   hay còn có reward từ coherence và mix với body-input sensor?"

  "Hay là còn trục reward nào đó khác nữa?"

→ Câu hỏi CHẠM vào GAP: framework mô tả KHI NÀO reward fire (H10),
  nhưng chưa mô tả reward fire CHẤT LƯỢNG THẾ NÀO.
```

### §1.2 — Framework hiện tại cover gì

```
✅ ĐÃ CÓ — MẠNH:

  03-Reward.md §1-§3:
    → Reward = 2-level: VTA dopamine alert + opioid body-base reward
    → H10 5 preconditions: ALL 5 required cho full reward
    → P5 (chunk tag): opioid vs cortisol association → direction

  Body-Feedback-Mechanism.md §1-§2:
    → 4 trục orthogonal: Direction × Magnitude × Source × Chunk Dynamics
    → 2 input sources: Sensory-Driven vs Pattern-Driven
    → = Reward có thể từ domain stimulus HOẶC internal chunk fire

  Feeling.md §6-§8:
    → Reward happens between Step ⑤ and ⑥ (body-base check)
    → 4 eureka cases (Archimedes/Einstein/student +/-) 
    → Quality = f(chunk library × compile context × current state)

  Feeling-Sources.md:
    → 10+ channels → mỗi channel produce feeling KHÁC
    → §10: Cognitive/Prediction feelings = "rightness/wrongness"


⚠️ GAP — CHƯA CÓ:

  → Reward PROFILES không formalize: implicit hints khắp nơi, no unified model
  → PFC behavior DURING reward states: §7 chỉ có offline cases
  → Compile context → reward QUALITY: P5 nói direction (opioid vs cortisol),
    chưa nói CHẤT LƯỢNG subjective experience khác nhau thế nào
  → Flow = continuous reward: mentioned ~20+ lần nhưng no dedicated analysis
```

## §2 — 5 REWARD PROFILES: "HƯƠNG VỊ" REWARD

### §2.1 — Neuroscience foundation

```
🟢 CÙNG HỆ THỐNG, KHÁC "HƯƠNG VỊ":

  Tik, Soreq, Kounios et al. 2020 (NeuroImage):
    → Insight activates CÙNG NAcc/VTA/dopaminergic circuitry
      như food, sex, drugs
    → = CÙNG reward hardware

  Kounios & Beeman 2009:
    → Aha moment: gamma burst ở right aSTG (unique cho insight)
    → ~100ms sau: reward signal ở orbitofrontal cortex
      (cùng vùng xử lý food/social/drugs/orgasm)
    → NHƯNG chỉ ở participants with HIGH reward sensitivity

  Ultra-high-field fMRI 2018:
    → "Aha!" experience = qualitatively DISTINCT from pride/satisfaction
    → = KHÔNG chỉ "vui vì giải được" — CÓ chất lượng riêng

  → CONVERGENCE:
    Cùng NAcc/VTA (hardware) + khác activation pattern (context)
    = Cùng opioid + khác concurrent body signals
    = Cùng "ngọt" + khác "hương vị"
```

### §2.2 — 5 Reward Profiles (framework synthesis)

```
🟡 TỪ DATA + FRAMEWORK, PHÂN BIỆT ÍT NHẤT 5 REWARD PROFILES:

  Profile = Opioid (common) + Context Signals (source-specific)

  ┌────────────────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────────┐
  │ Profile                │ Components                                   │
  ├────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │                        │                                              │
  │ ① SENSORY REWARD       │ Opioid + specific receptor pathway           │
  │   (ăn ngon, mùi hương, │ Body LOCATION rõ (miệng, mũi, da, tai)     │
  │    nhạc hay, tranh đẹp)│ Duration: WHILE experiencing                │
  │                        │ Replay fidelity: ~20-60% (Imagine-Final §1) │
  │                        │ Input: Sensory-Driven (BFM §2.2)           │
  │                        │                                              │
  ├────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │                        │                                              │
  │ ② COHERENCE REWARD     │ Opioid + ACC coherence resolve              │
  │   (insight, eureka,    │   + right aSTG (unique, Kounios 2009)       │
  │    "hiểu rồi!", "đẹp  │ Body LOCATION mơ hồ ("ngực", "đầu")        │
  │    quá" toán/nghệ thuật)│ Duration: BURST then GLOW                  │
  │                        │ Unique behavior: compulsive recheck (Wiles)  │
  │                        │ Poincaré: math = art = CÙNG nature           │
  │                        │ Input: Pattern-Driven (BFM §2.3 ⓓ gap fill) │
  │                        │                                              │
  ├────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │                        │                                              │
  │ ③ SOCIAL REWARD        │ Opioid + mirror signals + status update      │
  │   (khen, connection,   │ Body: chest warmth, oxytocin contribution   │
  │    approval, belonging)│ Duration: DURING + AFTERGLOW                │
  │                        │ Input: Sensory-Driven (agent input)         │
  │                        │   + Pattern-Driven (schema match)           │
  │                        │ Connection.md: L1 SPM-owned momentary       │
  │                        │                                              │
  ├────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │                        │                                              │
  │ ④ RELIEF REWARD        │ Cortisol DROP dominant (NOT opioid-led)      │
  │   (threat resolved,    │ Body: muscle relax, breathing ease,         │
  │    "xong rồi",        │   shoulder drop                              │
  │    "thoát rồi")       │ Duration: IMMEDIATE then FADE               │
  │                        │ ≠ pleasure — = ABSENCE of pain/threat       │
  │                        │ Eureka model ① Archimedes: opioid + relief  │
  │                        │   = DOUBLE reward (Feeling.md §6.4)         │
  │                        │                                              │
  ├────────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │                        │                                              │
  │ ⑤ PREVIEW REWARD       │ Opioid REDUCED (~20-60% fidelity)            │
  │   (tưởng tượng, nhớ   │ = Replay/preview of ①②③④                    │
  │    lại, anticipation)  │ Same quality, lower intensity                │
  │                        │ BFM §2.3: ⓐ REPLAY + ⓑ PREVIEW             │
  │                        │ Animals có (hippocampal preplay)             │
  │                        │ Cần compiled chunks (prerequisite)           │
  │                        │                                              │
  └────────────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────────┘

  ⚠️ PROFILES KHÔNG LOẠI TRỪ — có thể COMPOUND:
    → Eureka sau struggle: ② coherence + ④ relief = DOUBLE (Archimedes)
    → Ăn cùng bạn bè: ① sensory + ③ social = COMPOUND
    → Được khen vì giải bài: ② coherence + ③ social = COMPOUND
    → Tưởng tượng ăn ngon: ⑤ preview OF ① sensory
```

### §2.3 — Temporal Profile khác nhau

```
🟡 THỜI GIAN REWARD KHÁC NHAU THEO PROFILE:

  ① SENSORY:   ─────████████─────  (during stimulus)
  ② COHERENCE: ─────██▓▓▒▒░░────  (burst → glow → fade)
  ③ SOCIAL:    ─────████▓▓▒▒░░──  (during + afterglow)
  ④ RELIEF:    ─────████▒░───────  (immediate → fast fade)
  ⑤ PREVIEW:   ─────▓▓▒▒░░──────  (reduced version of source)

  ████ = peak intensity
  ▓▓   = strong afterglow
  ▒▒   = moderate fade
  ░░   = trace
  ──   = baseline

  → Temporal profile = thêm 1 chiều phân biệt nữa
  → Body-Feedback-Mechanism có magnitude + direction
  → CHƯA CÓ: temporal profile per reward type
```

---

## §3 — REWARD SIGNAL LANDSCAPE (v0.2 refined)

### §3.1 — Framework abstraction level: Reward = Reward

```
⭐⭐ FRAMEWORK POSITION (v0.2 — refined từ v0.1 "opioid = sugar"):

  v0.1 NÓI: "Opioid = common denominator. Context = differentiator."
  v0.2 REFINE: Opioid là best-studied, nhưng KHÔNG PHẢI exclusive.

  FRAMEWORK ABSTRACTION LEVEL:
    → PFC giao tiếp với vô thức qua NEURON PATTERNS, không đọc hormone
    → PFC KHÔNG biết "đó là opioid hay endocannabinoid"
    → PFC chỉ thấy: body-feedback signal có HƯỚNG + MAGNITUDE + QUALITY
    → Specific hormones = implementation detail BÊN DƯỚI level of analysis

  → FRAMEWORK NÊN NÓI:
    "Reward = body-base confirm signal (approach direction)"
    "Body-base confirm signal phổ biến nhất = opioid system (🟢 Berridge)"
    "Nhưng body-feedback system RỘNG HƠN chỉ opioid"

  → "Hương vị" reward = concurrent body state + reward signal (chung)
  → KHÔNG phải hệ reward khác nhau — CÙNG hedonic hotspot circuit, KHÁC input
  → Tương tự: dissonance cũng có "hương vị" (BFM opening quote:
    "Mỗi layer chunk thêm vào = thêm 1 hương vị dissonance")
  → = Cùng principle cho CẢ 2 hướng (reward + dissonance)
```

### §3.2 — Reward Signal Landscape: Research evidence per modality

```
🟢🟡 BẰNG CHỨNG THEO TỪNG MODALITY:

  Framework không cần biết chính xác hormone nào cho mỗi loại reward.
  Nhưng CẦN biết: opioid có thật sự phổ biến không, hay chỉ sampling bias?

  ┌─────────────────┬────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────┐
  │ Loại reward     │ Evidence   │ Chi tiết                                 │
  ├─────────────────┼────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Food/sweet      │ 🟢 STRONG  │ Smith & Berridge 2007: mu-opioid hotspot │
  │ (đường, ăn ngon)│            │ DOUBLES liking reactions. Gold standard. │
  ├─────────────────┼────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Music           │ 🟢 STRONG  │ Mallik 2017: naltrexone (opioid blocker) │
  │ (nghe nhạc hay) │            │ GIẢM pleasure + facial EMG.             │
  │                 │            │ PET-fMRI 2025: mu-opioid binding TĂNG.   │
  ├─────────────────┼────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Sexual pleasure │ 🟢 STRONG  │ Review 2025 (Sex Med Rev): mu-opioid =   │
  │                 │            │ core hedonic signal. Oxytocin = bonding.  │
  ├─────────────────┼────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Spicy food      │ 🟡 VIA PAIN│ Capsaicin → TRPV1 PAIN → endorphin      │
  │ (cay vừa đủ)   │            │ release. Opioid NHƯNG qua pain pathway.  │
  ├─────────────────┼────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Pleasant touch  │ ⚠️ COUNTER │ Loseth 2019 (SCAN): naltrexone KHÔNG    │
  │ (áo mềm, vuốt) │            │ giảm touch pleasantness! C-tactile      │
  │                 │            │ afferents → posterior insula = riêng?    │
  ├─────────────────┼────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Temperature     │ 🟡 INDIRECT│ Inagaki 2015: naltrexone block           │
  │ (bóng mát, ấm) │            │ warmth→social feeling. Pure thermal     │
  │                 │            │ pleasure → ít data trực tiếp.           │
  ├─────────────────┼────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Visual beauty   │ 🟡 INDIRECT│ Ishizu & Zeki 2011: mOFC activation.    │
  │ (tranh đẹp)    │            │ mOFC CÓ hotspots. Chưa naltrexone test. │
  ├─────────────────┼────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Insight/eureka  │ 🟢 STRONG  │ Tik 2020: cùng NAcc/VTA/dopaminergic.   │
  │ (hiểu rồi!)    │            │ Kounios 2009: OFC reward ~100ms.        │
  └─────────────────┴────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────┘

  ENDOCANNABINOID = HỆ THỐNG THỨ 2, PHỤ THUỘC OPIOID:
    → Mahler 2007: anandamide ở NAcc hotspot cũng doubles liking
    → NHƯNG Stacey 2018 (Berridge lab): block opioid → endocannabinoid
      liking cũng MẤT
    → = Endocannabinoid AMPLIFY nhưng dependent on opioid
    → 🟢 Ngoại lệ quan trọng: runner's high = endocannabinoid PRIMARY
      (Fuss 2015 PNAS, Siebers 2021: naltrexone KHÔNG reduce euphoria)

  KẾT LUẬN:
    → Opioid = primary reward signal cho PHẦN LỚN modality (food, music,
      sex, insight) = 🟢 evidence strong
    → Touch = counterexample trực tiếp (Loseth 2019) → pathway riêng?
    → Runner's high = endocannabinoid dominant (Fuss 2015)
    → COMMON ELEMENT = hedonic hotspot CIRCUIT (NAcc shell, VP, mOFC)
      không chỉ 1 neurochemical
    → Framework ĐÚNG ở level: "body-base confirm signal"
      Framework cần REFINE: không commit exclusive vào "opioid"
```

### §3.3 — Tại sao opioid nổi bật (evolutionary context)

```
🟡 TẠI SAO OPIOID = BEST-STUDIED + MOST PROMINENT:

  ĂN = NHU CẦU CƠ BẢN NHẤT TẠO NÊN CƠ THỂ:
    → Thở: VTA habituate hoàn toàn (quá ổn định, zero delta)
    → Ăn: biến đổi liên tục, mỗi bữa khác nhau
    → Sensor array CỰC RỘNG: lưỡi (5 vị), mũi (hàng trăm receptor),
      mắt (màu sắc), texture, nhiệt độ, gut neurons
    → Evolutionary pressure LÂU NHẤT — mọi sinh vật đều cần ăn

  → Opioid hedonic hotspot circuit = EVOLVED CHO food reward ban đầu
  → Sau đó EXTENDED cho reward khác (neural reuse)
  → Các reward khác "plug into" circuit này + có thể dùng thêm signal khác
  → = Opioid nổi bật vì OLDEST + MOST ROBUST + MOST STUDIED
  → = Sampling bias: research food/sugar nhiều nhất → thấy opioid nhiều nhất
    → kết luận "reward = opioid" → ĐÚNG NHƯNG KHÔNG ĐỦ

  ALLIESTHESIA (Cabanac 1971, 🟢):
    → Cùng stimulus: pleasant HOẶC unpleasant tùy body state
    → Nước lạnh: pleasant khi nóng, unpleasant khi lạnh
    → Đường: pleasant khi đói, less pleasant khi no
    → = CONSISTENT với H10 P1 (schema pending) + P4 (Goldilocks)
    → Reward CÓ HƯỚNG — direction phụ thuộc body state hiện tại
```

### §3.4 — Poincaré Equivalence

```
🟡 TẠI SAO MATH = ART = "CÙNG NATURE" (Poincaré):

  Poincaré (Science and Method, 1908):
    "A mathematician experiences in his work the same impression
     as an artist; his pleasure is as great and of the same nature."

  FRAMEWORK GIẢI THÍCH:
    Math insight: abstract PATTERN coherence → Goldilocks match → reward signal
    Art beauty: sensory PATTERN coherence → Goldilocks match → reward signal

    COMMON ELEMENT = pattern match trong Goldilocks zone (H10 P4)
    → Math: input = internal chunks (pattern-driven)
    → Art: input = sensory (visual/auditory) + pattern
    → CẢ HAI: chunks fire → match ~40-70% → ACC "coherent" → reward

  → Poincaré's "same nature" = same COHERENCE REWARD profile (②)
  → Art thêm sensory component (① + ②), math thuần ② coherence
  → = Tại sao nhiều nhà toán/vật lý appreciate music
  → = KHÔNG phải trùng hợp — cùng Goldilocks mechanism

  🔴 HYPOTHESIS CẦN VERIFY:
    → Nếu đúng: expert toán + expert nhạc = CÙNG activation pattern?
    → Kounios gamma ở right aSTG — có fire cho aesthetic pleasure?
    → = Testable prediction

  ⭐ v1.0: DRILLED → see §3.19 for deep analysis.
  Zeki 2014 CONFIRMS: mOFC activation shared across math/art/music beauty.
  Beauty = H10 P4 on any domain. P2 = beauty gate. ② cross-domain priming.
```

### §3.5 — Type A / Type B: 2 loại body-base confirm signal (v0.3 new)

```
⭐⭐ REWARD SIGNAL ARCHITECTURE v0.3 — 2 TYPES:

  R9 drill (Touch: Loseth 2019) + R10 drill (Exercise: Fuss 2015)
  → reveal: KHÔNG phải mọi "feeling good" đều dùng opioid.
  → 2 loại body-base confirm signal:

  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
  │                                                                  │
  │  TYPE A — EVALUATIVE CONFIRM                                     │
  │                                                                  │
  │  Circuit: Hedonic hotspot (NAcc shell, VP, mOFC)                │
  │  Primary signal: μ-opioid                                       │
  │  Amplifier: Endocannabinoid (dependent on opioid — Stacey 2018) │
  │  H10: Full 5 preconditions required                             │
  │  Requires: Compiled chunks (P2) + body-need gap (P1)           │
  │  Learned: YES — quality depends on chunk library                │
  │  Modulated by: Alliesthesia (body state changes evaluation)     │
  │  Examples: Food, music, insight, visual beauty, sex, social     │
  │  Mechanism: Input → EVALUATE vs body-need → confirm/reject      │
  │                                                                  │
  ├──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │                                                                  │
  │  TYPE B — DIRECT STATE CONFIRM                                   │
  │                                                                  │
  │  Circuit: Interoceptive / body-state regulation (VARIES)        │
  │  Primary signal: VARIES by modality:                             │
  │    Touch: CT afferents → posterior insula (🟢 Löken 2009)       │
  │    Exercise: Endocannabinoid CB1 (🟢 Fuss 2015 PNAS)           │
  │    Temperature: thermoreceptor → hypothalamus                    │
  │  H10: Simplified (P1 basic body-need, P2-P5 reduced/N/A)       │
  │  Requires: Hardware pathways (minimal compiled chunks)          │
  │  Learned: MINIMAL — hardware from birth                         │
  │  Modulated by: Less affected by alliesthesia (🔴 prediction)    │
  │  Examples: Touch comfort, runner's high, warmth, stretching     │
  │  Mechanism: Body activity → state DIRECTLY improves → signal    │
  │                                                                  │
  ├──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │                                                                  │
  │  COMMON ELEMENT (framework level):                               │
  │  "Reward = body-base confirm signal"                             │
  │  Cả Type A VÀ Type B = body-base confirm — KHÁC mechanism       │
  │  Framework ĐÚNG ở abstraction level "body-base confirm signal"  │
  │                                                                  │
  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘


  EVIDENCE QUA NALTREXONE (opioid blocker):

    ┌──────────────┬─────────────┬──────────────────────────────────┐
    │ Modality     │ Naltrexone  │ Type                             │
    ├──────────────┼─────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┤
    │ Food/sweet   │ BLOCKS ✅    │ Type A (opioid evaluative)       │
    │ Music        │ BLOCKS ✅    │ Type A (Mallik 2017)             │
    │ Insight      │ (untested)  │ Type A (predicted)               │
    │ Touch        │ NO EFFECT ⚠️│ Type B (Loseth 2019)             │
    │ Exercise     │ NO EFFECT ⚠️│ Type B (Fuss 2015, Siebers 2021) │
    │ Temperature  │ (untested)  │ Type B (predicted)               │
    └──────────────┴─────────────┴──────────────────────────────────┘


  EVOLUTIONARY ARGUMENT:

    Type B = CỔ HƠN Type A:
    → Touch comfort: mọi sinh vật có da → benefit từ contact
      → KHÔNG CẦN circuit đánh giá phức tạp
    → Exercise: body movement → homeostatic regulation
      → Direct signal, không cần evaluation
    → Type A (evaluative): evolved CHO đánh giá phức tạp hơn
      → "Cái này ăn được không? Dinh dưỡng? Độc?"
      → Requires compiled chunks → LEARNED

    → Trẻ sơ sinh: Type B đã có NGAY (touch comfort, warmth)
    → Type A: develops with chunk compilation (taste preferences, etc.)


  H10 CHO TYPE B — SIMPLIFIED:

    P1 Schema pending: CÓ nhưng ĐƠN GIẢN (body luôn "cần" contact/movement)
    P2 Chunks base: KHÔNG CẦN nhiều (CT afferents = hardware)
    P3 VTA delta: CÓ THỂ KHÔNG CẦN (signal đi posterior insula, không qua VTA)
    P4 Goldilocks: ĐƠN GIẢN (CT optimal ~1-10cm/s = hardware preference)
    P5 Chunk tag: KHÔNG ÁP DỤNG (hardware, không compiled)
    → Type B gần hardware hơn, ít phụ thuộc compiled chunks


  EDGE CASES (spectrum, not binary):

    Spicy food: pain → compensatory opioid → compiles into Type A
    Social touch: CT afferents (B) + oxytocin bonding (→ A?)
    Music + movement: evaluative (A) + body rhythm (B?)
    → Type A/B = FRAMEWORK ORGANIZING TOOL, not brain architecture
    → Real brain = spectrum giữa 2 cực


  CROSS-CONNECTION R12 (Dissociation):
    → Dissociation = PFC suppress emotion → Type A reward BLOCKED
    → Type B (touch, CT afferents) = hardware pathway, BYPASS PFC
    → = Tại sao body-oriented therapy hiệu quả cho trauma
    → Touch = "backdoor" vào body BYPASS PFC overmodulation
    → 🟢 Van der Kolk 2014: body-oriented approaches for trauma
```

### §3.6 — Neurochemical Multi-Role Principle (v0.3 new)

```
⭐⭐ NEUROCHEMICAL FUNCTION = f(CIRCUIT, CONTEXT):

  R10 drill resolved "mâu thuẫn" endocannabinoid:
  → Stacey 2018: eCB in NAcc hotspot DEPENDS on opioid ✅
  → Fuss 2015: eCB in exercise INDEPENDENT of opioid ✅
  → KHÔNG mâu thuẫn: cùng molecule, KHÁC circuit, KHÁC function

  PRINCIPLE: Neurochemical systems = MULTI-ROLE
  Function = f(circuit × context) — NOT f(molecule alone)

  ┌─────────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────────┐
  │ Neurochemical   │ Multiple Roles                                │
  ├─────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Dopamine        │ Salience (VTA) / Motor (striatum) /          │
  │                 │ Working Memory (PFC)                          │
  ├─────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Cortisol        │ 5 roles (Cortisol-Baseline §7.7):            │
  │                 │ Compile Direction / Holding / Threat-sustained│
  │                 │ / Inertia / Silent                            │
  ├─────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Opioid          │ Pain modulation (original) /                  │
  │                 │ Hedonic evaluation (recruited) /              │
  │                 │ Social bonding (extended)                     │
  ├─────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Endocannabinoid │ Body-state regulation (original, Type B) /   │
  │                 │ Hedonic amplifier (recruited into Type A) /   │
  │                 │ Stress modulation (amygdala CB1)              │
  └─────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────────┘

  EVOLUTIONARY MECHANISM: Neural Reuse (🟢 Anderson 2010)
  → Old systems get RECRUITED into new circuits
  → eCB started as body-state regulator (homeostatic)
  → Khi hedonic hotspot evolved → eCB got recruited as amplifier
  → = Original function (body-state) + new function (amplifier)
  → = BOTH still work, in DIFFERENT circuits

  R10 STATUS: RESOLVED — reclassify từ "mâu thuẫn" → "multi-role evidence"

  FRAMEWORK IMPLICATION:
  → Framework ĐÚNG khi abstract trên hormone level
  → "Reward = body-base confirm signal" — hormone = implementation detail
  → Specific hormone × circuit = neuroscience detail DƯỚI framework scope
  → Framework CẦN note: multi-role principle khi reference hormones
```

### §3.7 — A/B × Profiles ORTHOGONAL + Edge Cases + A Gates B (v0.4 new: R1+R13 drill)

```
⭐⭐ R1+R13 DRILL — KEY FINDING: A/B = ORTHOGONAL DIMENSION

  v0.3 introduced Type A/B distinction.
  v0.4 drill RESOLVES: A/B quan hệ thế nào với 5 Profiles?

  3 khả năng đã cân nhắc:
    (a) Thêm Profile ⑥ "Homeostatic" cho Type B → REJECTED
    (b) Type A/B = meta-dimension ORTHOGONAL lên tất cả profiles → ✅ ACCEPTED
    (c) Split Profile ① thành ①a/①b → REJECTED

  TẠI SAO ORTHOGONAL:
    → A/B cắt NGANG tất cả profiles, không chỉ ①:
      Profile ① Sensory: food=A, touch=B
      Profile ③ Social: praise=A, physical proximity=B
      Profile ④ Relief: solved problem=A, pain stops=B
    → Split ① → phải split ③, ④ nữa → redundant
    → Orthogonal dimension = cleaner, more general


  5 PROFILES × A/B RATIO:

  ┌────────────────┬───────────────┬──────────────┬────────────────────┐
  │ Profile        │ Type A        │ Type B       │ Typical Ratio      │
  │                │ (evaluative)  │ (direct)     │                    │
  ├────────────────┼───────────────┼──────────────┼────────────────────┤
  │ ① SENSORY      │ Food, music,  │ Touch, warmth│ VARIES by modality │
  │                │ visual beauty │ stretching   │ Food: ~80A/20B     │
  │                │               │              │ Touch: ~20A/80B    │
  │                │               │              │ Music: ~90A/10B    │
  ├────────────────┼───────────────┼──────────────┼────────────────────┤
  │ ② COHERENCE    │ Insight,      │ (minimal)    │ ~95A/5B            │
  │                │ eureka, math  │ body relief  │                    │
  │                │ beauty        │ component    │                    │
  ├────────────────┼───────────────┼──────────────┼────────────────────┤
  │ ③ SOCIAL       │ Praise eval,  │ Physical     │ Online praise:     │
  │                │ status, belong│ proximity,   │   ~90A/10B         │
  │                │               │ co-regulation│ Mother hug:        │
  │                │               │              │   ~40A/60B         │
  ├────────────────┼───────────────┼──────────────┼────────────────────┤
  │ ④ RELIEF       │ Evaluated     │ Physical     │ Problem solved:    │
  │                │ relief (solved│ relief       │   ~70A/30B         │
  │                │ problem)      │ (pain stops) │ Pain stops:        │
  │                │               │              │   ~20A/80B         │
  ├────────────────┼───────────────┼──────────────┼────────────────────┤
  │ ⑤ PREVIEW      │ Preview of A  │ Preview of B │ Inherits source    │
  │                │ (high fidelity│ (LOW fidelity│ But B preview =    │
  │                │  ~40-60%)     │  ~10-30%? 🔴)│ fidelity DROPS     │
  └────────────────┴───────────────┴──────────────┴────────────────────┘

  ⚠️ Ratios = approximate illustration, NOT precise measurement
  ⚠️ Real brain = continuous spectrum, not discrete percentages


  TYPE A/B × BFM 2-SOURCE MAPPING:

  BFM §2 phân biệt: Sensory-Driven vs Pattern-Driven.
  Type A/B phân biệt: Evaluative vs Direct State.
  Relationship:

  ┌──────────────────┬──────────────────┬──────────────────┐
  │ BFM Source       │ Type A possible? │ Type B possible? │
  ├──────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────────┤
  │ Sensory-Driven   │ ✅ YES           │ ✅ YES           │
  │ (domain → body)  │ Food, music,     │ Touch, warmth,   │
  │                  │ visual beauty    │ exercise         │
  ├──────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────────┤
  │ Pattern-Driven   │ ✅ YES           │ ⚠️ VERY LIMITED  │
  │ (chunks → body)  │ Insight, preview,│ Preview of B     │
  │                  │ comparison       │ = LOW fidelity   │
  └──────────────────┴──────────────────┴──────────────────┘

  → Type B ≈ ALWAYS Sensory-Driven (requires actual hardware activation)
  → Type A = Sensory-Driven OR Pattern-Driven (evaluation either way)
  → Type B = "hardware-bound reward" (needs actual body-state change)
  → Type A = "evaluation-bound reward" (any input source)
```

```
⭐⭐ 6 EDGE CASES — TYPE A/B BOUNDARY (R13 drill):

  ① SPICY FOOD (ớt cay vừa đủ):
    Input: Capsaicin → TRPV1 pain → ACTUAL pain signal = B-like input
    Response: Body release endorphin compensatory → opioid = A-like reward
    → INSIGHT: Input pathway ≠ Reward pathway
    → Spicy = B INPUT → A REWARD SIGNAL (compensatory variant)
    → "Acquired taste": lần đầu chỉ pain, lần 10+ body anticipate endorphin
    → = Compile history transforms B input → A reward

  ② SOCIAL TOUCH (mẹ ôm con, bạn bè vỗ vai):
    B component: CT afferents → posterior insula (hardware)
    A component: Social evaluation — "AI đang chạm?"
    → Friend: A positive → AMPLIFY B → compound pleasant
    → Stranger: A negative → OVERRIDE B → unpleasant despite CT
    → Infant: A minimal → B raw → basic comfort (design feature)
    → Dissociation: A suppressed → B may get through → "backdoor"
    → = CT signal (B) bị GATED bởi social evaluation (A)

  ③ MUSIC + BODY MOVEMENT (nhảy, lắc lư):
    A: Music evaluation (opioid — Mallik 2017)
    B: Body movement (eCB-like? rhythmic entrainment?)
    + possible ③ Social (group dancing, synchronization)
    → Dancing = A + B + Social = compound across 3+ channels
    → Cultural universality: mọi nền văn hóa có dance
      vì compound A+B+Social = MAXIMUM reward density

  ④ MASSAGE chuyên nghiệp:
    B: CT afferents (touch pleasantness)
    A: Quality evaluation ("bấm đúng chỗ" vs "đau quá")
    + ④ Relief: muscle tension release = cortisol drop
    → 3 profiles + 2 types simultaneously
    → Bad massage: A evaluates "sai kỹ thuật" → override B

  ⑤ SEXUAL PLEASURE:
    B: Physical arousal, genital stimulation (hardware)
    A: Attractiveness evaluation, emotional context
    + ③ Social: bonding, intimacy (oxytocin)
    + ④ Relief: tension release at orgasm
    → Có thể là reward COMPOUND NHẤT trong repertoire
    → 4 profiles + 2 types ĐỒNG THỜI
    → = Tại sao sexual dysfunction multifactorial

  ⑥ ASMR (Autonomous Sensory Meridian Response):
    Response: Tingles, relaxation = body-level (B-like)
    Trigger: SPECIFIC evaluated stimuli (whispering, tapping) = A-gated
    Hardware: NOT everyone experiences → genetic variation
    → Pattern: A GATE decides WHETHER B-like response fires
    → Similar to social touch: evaluated input → body hardware response


  ⭐ 5 INSIGHTS TỪ EDGE CASES:

  Insight 1: A/B = ORTHOGONAL DIMENSIONS, NOT BINARY
    → Most rewards = compound A+B at varying ratios
    → Pure A rare (insight), Pure B rare (exercise eCB)
    → PURE B ←← MIXED →→ PURE A
      Exercise  Massage  Dancing  Music  Insight

  Insight 2: INPUT PATHWAY ≠ REWARD PATHWAY
    → Spicy food: B input (pain) → A reward (compensatory opioid)
    → Social touch: B input (CT) → A modulation → compound output
    → Type A/B nên áp dụng cho REWARD MECHANISM, not input

  Insight 3: A GATES B — evaluation CAN amplify OR suppress hardware
    → Trusted person → A amplifies B → very pleasant
    → Stranger → A overrides B → unpleasant
    → A absent (infant, dissociation) → B unmodulated (raw)

  Insight 4: A/B RATIO SHIFTS ACROSS DEVELOPMENT (§3.8 drill)

  Insight 5: "MODULATION GRADIENT" thay cho binary
    → Type B: NOT modulated by compiled chunks, PFC state
    → Type A: FULLY modulated by chunks, PFC state, evaluation
    → Mixed: degree of modulation = f(A/B ratio)
```

```
⭐⭐ A GATES B — EVALUATION MODULATES HARDWARE SIGNAL:

  MECHANISM (3 bước):

  Step 1: B SIGNAL FIRES (hardware, automatic)
    → CT afferents detect touch → posterior insula receives
    → Timing: immediate (ms)
    → KHÔNG cần evaluation, KHÔNG cần compiled chunks

  Step 2: A EVALUATION RUNS (parallel, slightly slower)
    → Context evaluation: WHO/WHAT/WHERE
    → Compiled chunks activate: friend? stranger? threat?
    → Timing: 100-500ms (needs chunk matching)

  Step 3: INTEGRATION → A MODULATES B
    → Integration hub: anterior insula? ACC? (🔴 exact locus unclear)
    → A result MODULATES B signal:

    ┌──────────────────────┬──────────────────────────────────┐
    │ A Evaluation Result  │ Effect on B Signal               │
    ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┤
    │ A positive           │ AMPLIFY B → compound pleasant    │
    │ (trusted person)     │ B + A = more than either alone   │
    ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┤
    │ A negative           │ SUPPRESS/OVERRIDE B              │
    │ (stranger, threat)   │ A negative > B positive → net    │
    │                      │ unpleasant despite CT pleasant   │
    ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┤
    │ A absent             │ B RAW (unmodulated)              │
    │ (infant, dissociation│ Basic pleasant from hardware     │
    │  PFC offline)        │ = "pure Type B experience"       │
    ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┤
    │ A conflicted         │ AMBIGUOUS signal                 │
    │ (attracted stranger) │ Body confused → arousal + caution│
    └──────────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────┘


  EVOLUTIONARY LOGIC (🟡):

  Tại sao B KHÔNG hoạt động đơn lẻ ở adult?
    → Pure B = dangerous (snake touch = CT pleasant but DANGER)
    → A GATE evolved to provide CONTEXT for B signals
    → = Safety filter ON TOP OF hardware pleasure

  Tại sao infant KHÔNG CÓ A gate đầy đủ?
    → Infant chưa có compiled chunks → A evaluation LIMITED
    → B dominant at birth = DESIGN FEATURE (needs unconditional touch)
    → A gate develops GRADUALLY with chunk compilation
    → = "Trust the world first, learn to evaluate later"

  Therapeutic implication:
    → Trauma (dissociation) = A gate stuck at "suppress everything"
    → Body-oriented therapy = deliberately activate B pathway
    → B bypasses stuck A gate → body registers "safe"
    → Gradual: B exposure → A gate loosens → emotions return
    → = Van der Kolk 2014 mechanism explained at circuit level


  H10 × TYPE A/B — PRECONDITIONS REFINED:

  ┌──────────────────┬─────────────────┬────────────────┬──────────────────┐
  │ Precondition     │ Type A          │ Type B         │ Compound A+B     │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────┼────────────────┼──────────────────┤
  │ P1 Schema        │ REQUIRED —      │ SIMPLIFIED —   │ Either can       │
  │    pending       │ specific gap    │ body-need      │ satisfy          │
  │                  │                 │ always present │ independently    │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────┼────────────────┼──────────────────┤
  │ P2 Chunks base   │ REQUIRED —      │ MINIMAL —      │ A limited by P2  │
  │                  │ compiled for    │ hardware paths │ B NOT limited    │
  │                  │ evaluation      │ from birth     │                  │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────┼────────────────┼──────────────────┤
  │ P3 VTA delta     │ REQUIRED —      │ UNCERTAIN —    │ B may fire       │
  │                  │ novelty/change  │ may bypass VTA │ WITHOUT VTA      │
  │                  │                 │ (→ posterior   │ = "always-on     │
  │                  │                 │  insula path)  │   background"    │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────┼────────────────┼──────────────────┤
  │ P4 Goldilocks    │ REQUIRED —      │ HARDWARE —     │ A: complexity    │
  │                  │ ~40-70% match   │ CT ~1-10cm/s   │ B: fixed optimal │
  │                  │                 │ = fixed range  │ range            │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────┼────────────────┼──────────────────┤
  │ P5 Chunk tag     │ REQUIRED —      │ N/A —          │ A affected by    │
  │                  │ opioid/cortisol │ hardware, no   │ compile history  │
  │                  │ tag direction   │ tag needed     │ B = safe baseline│
  └──────────────────┴─────────────────┴────────────────┴──────────────────┘


  ⭐ B = "SAFE BASELINE REWARD" (evolutionary floor):

    Type B KHÔNG bị block bởi P2, P3, P5 failures:
    → Không cần compiled chunks → infant CAN experience
    → Không cần VTA novelty → habituate CHẬM hơn (🔴 R20)
    → Không bị cortisol-tag → KHÔNG associated với threat

    → Type B = RELIABLE, ALWAYS-AVAILABLE baseline reward
    → Type A = RICH, VARIABLE, but CONDITIONAL on P1-P5
    → Loss of A (burnout, anhedonia) → B remains ("touch still good")
    → Loss of B (neuropathy) → A remains ("can still enjoy music")
    → Loss of BOTH → severe anhedonia (rare, devastating)
    → = "Last resort" reward cho trauma, depression, burnout:
      Type A blocked (P5 cortisol tag, P2 insufficient, etc.)
      → Type B VẪN accessible vì hardware-based


  🔴 PREVIEW FIDELITY × A/B — TESTABLE PREDICTION (R17):

    Type A preview fidelity = HIGHER (~40-60%):
    → Compiled chunks fire → evaluation runs → mini-opioid
    → 🟢 Kosslyn 1994: visual imagery uses visual cortex
    → 🟢 Jeannerod 1995: motor imagery uses motor cortex
    → Both = cortical simulation = Type A territory

    Type B preview fidelity = LOWER (~10-30%?):
    → CT afferents = peripheral nerves, NEED actual skin contact
    → Preview misses hardware component → fidelity drops
    → "Nhớ vị chocolate rõ hơn nhớ cảm giác được massage"

    Implication:
    → Type A CAN drive wanting from PREVIEW (anticipation)
    → Type B NEEDS actual experience to reward
    → Type B resistant to "tưởng tượng cho sướng"
    → Infants: CẦN actual touch, không thể preview
```

---

### §3.8 — A/B Development Gradient Lifecycle (v0.4 new)

```
🟡 A/B RATIO SHIFTS ACROSS DEVELOPMENT:

  STAGE 1 — Neonate (0-3 months): A/B ≈ 5/95
    Type B dominant: touch, warmth, sucking, vestibular
    Type A minimal: sweet preference emerging (🔴 R19: A or B?)
    → Body = nearly pure hardware-driven reward
    → = Tại sao neonatal care = primarily physical contact

  STAGE 2 — Infant (3-18 months): A/B ≈ 20/80
    Type B still dominant: touch, co-regulation, warmth
    Type A growing: food preferences, familiar faces, object exploration
    → A gate forming: stranger anxiety (~8 months) = A starts evaluating
    → = "Trust the world" shifting to "evaluate the world"

  STAGE 3 — Child (2-7 years): A/B ≈ 40/60
    Type A expanding: music preference, food pickiness, coherence (puzzles)
    Type B maintained: still NEEDS touch, warmth, physical comfort
    → A can now OVERRIDE B: "don't touch me!" (stranger evaluation)
    → Play = primary A reward mechanism (Goldilocks challenges)

  STAGE 4 — Adolescent (12-18): A/B ≈ 60/40
    Type A dominant: social evaluation INTENSE, aesthetic developing
    Type B maintained but SOCIALLY CONSTRAINED:
      → Touch acceptable only in specific contexts
      → "Embarrassed by parent hug" = social A gate VERY strong

  STAGE 5 — Adult (25+): A/B ≈ 70/30 (varies enormously)
    Type A: full range (mastery, aesthetic, social, coherence)
    Type B: persists but often NEGLECTED:
      → "Quá bận để tập" (exercise B neglected)
      → "Không ai ôm" (touch B neglected)
      → Body-Base deficit ACCUMULATES silently
    → Expert in domain: A SO compiled → feels automatic like B

  STAGE 6 — Elderly: A/B potentially shifts BACK toward B
    → Cognitive decline reduces A capacity
    → Physical touch becomes MORE valuable again
    → "Bà chỉ cần con cháu tới, nắm tay bà" = B prominence returns

  LIFECYCLE ARC:
    B dominant → A builds → A peaks → A may decline → B persists
    → B NEVER reaches zero — hardware PERSISTS
    → = Evolutionary CIRCLE: hardware first and last


  CROSS-REFERENCE:
    → Child-Dev/Attachment: early B = foundation for later A
    → Compile-Taxonomy §3: 4 pathways = HOW A develops differently
    → Feeling-Sources §2 L1: interoceptive = Type B territory
    → Feeling-Sources §5: agent input = social B (co-regulation)
    → Education/Mechanism: pedagogy should respect A/B ratio per age
```

### §3.9 — 3 Types State Dependence: Alliesthesia Refined (v0.4 new: R14 drill)

```
⭐⭐ R14 DRILL — ALLIESTHESIA × TYPE A/B:

  Cabanac 1971 (🟢): "Alliesthesia" = cùng stimulus, khác hedonic value
  tùy body state. Framework mapped vào H10 P1 (schema pending).

  v0.3 prediction: "Type B LESS affected by alliesthesia."
  v0.4 drill reveals: prediction ĐÚNG nhưng cần precision.
  Cabanac GỘP ít nhất 2 mechanisms khác nhau thành 1 concept.
  Framework REFINES: 3 TYPES state dependence, ở 3 LEVELS khác nhau.


  ❶ SENSOR-LEVEL STATE DEPENDENCE (hardware / physics):

    Definition: Physical state changes SENSOR OUTPUT itself.
    Signal varies because PHYSICS changes, not opinion.

    Temperature:
      → Thermoreceptors detect delta from homeostatic setpoint
      → Moving TOWARD setpoint = pleasant signal
      → Moving AWAY from setpoint = unpleasant signal
      → = PHYSICS built into sensor, not evaluation
      → Nước lạnh khi nóng = pleasant (toward setpoint) ✅
      → Nước lạnh khi lạnh = unpleasant (away from setpoint) ✅

    CT afferents:
      → Optimal ~1-10 cm/s = hardware property (🟢 Löken 2009)
      → Too fast or too slow = less pleasant
      → = FIXED optimal range, not evaluation-dependent

    Exercise eCB:
      → Release = f(exercise duration, intensity) = metabolic computation
      → Exhaustion = body systems at limit → eCB insufficient
      → = HARDWARE constraint (metabolic), not evaluation constraint

    Characteristics:
      → CANNOT override by PFC (physics, not opinion)
      → Present from BIRTH (hardware)
      → Type B territory primarily
      → DETERMINISTIC: same physical input = same output


  ❷ EVALUATION-LEVEL STATE DEPENDENCE (classical alliesthesia):

    Definition: Body-need state changes EVALUATION OUTCOME.
    Same signal, different hedonic value — via evaluation circuit.

    Food:
      → Đói → chocolate = "fit body-need" → opioid → pleasant
      → No → chocolate = "no body-need" → no opioid → neutral
      → Mechanism: P1 (schema pending) modulates evaluation result
      → 🟢 Cabanac 1971: gustatory alliesthesia

    Music:
      → Mood modulates appreciation depth
      → Depression → music less rewarding (evaluation capacity reduced)
      → But: music CŨNG có Type B component (rhythm, body response)

    Insight:
      → Pending gap (P1) modulates reward magnitude
      → No pending → insight less rewarding
      → = P1 × schema depth = evaluation variables

    Characteristics:
      → CAN partially override by PFC (force-eat when full → possible but unpleasant)
      → Develops with CHUNK COMPILATION (evaluation needs chunks)
      → Type A territory primarily
      → = H10 P1 mechanism


  ❸ GATE-LEVEL STATE DEPENDENCE (A modulates B experience):

    Definition: Social/emotional context modulates EXPERIENCE of
    hardware signal — B signal constant, A gate varies.

    Touch:
      → CT afferents fire SAME regardless of social state
      → But EXPERIENCE varies:
        Lonely → A gate AMPLIFIES B → touch more valued
        Touch-saturated → A gate NEUTRAL on B → touch baseline
        Stranger → A gate SUPPRESSES B → touch uncomfortable
        Dissociation → A gate BLOCKS B → touch may not register
      → = B signal constant, A evaluation MODULATES experience

    Characteristics:
      → B signal NOT changing — A modulation changing
      → Develops with A gate formation (infant → adult, §3.8)
      → Interaction territory (A × B)
      → = "A Gates B" mechanism (§3.7) applied to state dependence


  COMPARISON TABLE:

  ┌──────────────────┬──────────────────┬──────────────┬─────────────────┐
  │ Dimension        │ ❶ Sensor-level   │ ❷ Evaluation │ ❸ Gate-level    │
  ├──────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────┼─────────────────┤
  │ What changes     │ Sensor output    │ Eval result  │ A modulation    │
  │                  │ itself           │              │ of B signal     │
  ├──────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────┼─────────────────┤
  │ Mechanism        │ Physics of       │ Body-need    │ Social/emotional│
  │                  │ receptor         │ (P1) changes │ context changes │
  │                  │                  │ evaluation   │ A gate setting  │
  ├──────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────┼─────────────────┤
  │ PFC override?    │ NO (physics)     │ PARTIAL      │ PARTIAL         │
  │                  │                  │ (can force)  │ (therapy)       │
  ├──────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────┼─────────────────┤
  │ From birth?      │ YES (hardware)   │ NO (needs    │ NO (needs       │
  │                  │                  │ chunks)      │ A gate)         │
  ├──────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────┼─────────────────┤
  │ Type territory   │ Type B           │ Type A       │ A × B           │
  │                  │                  │              │ interaction     │
  ├──────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────┼─────────────────┤
  │ Examples         │ Temp setpoint,   │ Food hunger, │ Touch lonely    │
  │                  │ CT speed range,  │ music mood,  │ vs stranger,    │
  │                  │ exercise fatigue │ insight gap  │ dissociation    │
  ├──────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────┼─────────────────┤
  │ Intervention     │ Change PHYSICAL  │ Change BODY- │ Change SOCIAL/  │
  │                  │ state (cool body,│ NEED state   │ EMOTIONAL       │
  │                  │ rest muscles)    │ (eat, rest,  │ context (safe   │
  │                  │                  │ resolve gap) │ person, therapy)│
  └──────────────────┴──────────────────┴──────────────┴─────────────────┘
```

```
⭐ TEMPERATURE PARADOX — CABANAC REFINED:

  Cabanac INCLUDED temperature in alliesthesia concept (1971).
  Framework REFINES: temperature = sensor-level mechanism
  MASQUERADING as evaluation-level alliesthesia.

  Observable: Cold person → warm water = pleasant
              Warm person → warm water = unpleasant
  Looks like: evaluation-level alliesthesia (same as food)
  Actually is: sensor-level (thermoreceptor delta from setpoint)

  Proof:
  → PFC CANNOT override: "I WANT to enjoy this hot bath" when overheated = FAILS
  → Evaluation-level CAN be partially overridden: force-eat when full = POSSIBLE
  → Temperature state dependence = ABSOLUTE, non-negotiable
  → Food state dependence = PARTIAL, overridable

  → = Same OBSERVATION (changed hedonic value)
  → = Different MECHANISM (sensor logic vs evaluation circuit)
  → = Framework contribution: distinguishes mechanism levels
       that Cabanac's concept conflated


  v0.3 PREDICTION REFINED:

  v0.3: "Type B LESS affected by alliesthesia"

  v0.4: "Type B SIGNAL is not affected by evaluation-level alliesthesia.
         Type B SIGNAL has its own sensor-level state dependence.
         Type B EXPERIENCE is affected by A-gate modulation.
         Classical alliesthesia (Cabanac) = evaluation-level = Type A specific."

  → Không phải B "less affected" — B affected BY DIFFERENT MECHANISM
  → 3 mechanisms, 3 levels, 3 intervention strategies
  → Framework ADDS precision to Cabanac's unified concept


  🔴 TESTABLE PREDICTIONS:

  P-R14a: Touch pleasantness does NOT change with hunger state
    → CT afferents independent of digestive state
    → Measurable: pleasant touch ratings before/after meal
    → Expected: no significant difference

  P-R14b: Touch pleasantness DOES change with social isolation
    → BUT: this is A-gate modulation, not B signal change
    → Under naltrexone: isolation effect should REDUCE
      (blocks opioid component of social evaluation)
    → Without naltrexone: isolation effect present
    → = Distinguishes B signal from A-gate modulation

  P-R14c: Temperature state dependence CANNOT be overridden by PFC
    → Warm water when overheated = unpleasant REGARDLESS of desire
    → Food state dependence CAN be partially overridden
    → = Distinguishes sensor-level from evaluation-level

  P-R14d: Elderly with cognitive decline: PRESERVED sensor-level
    but REDUCED evaluation-level alliesthesia
    → Temperature responses maintained (hardware)
    → Food hedonic modulation by hunger may decrease
    → Touch pleasantness maintained (B hardware)
    → Social modulation of touch may simplify (A gate declines)
    → = Tests developmental gradient (§3.8) × state dependence


  CROSS-REFERENCES:
    → §3.3 Alliesthesia original mention → REFINED here
    → §3.7 A Gates B → applied to state dependence (gate-level)
    → §3.8 Development Gradient → mapped onto 3 types
    → 03-Reward.md §3.2 P1 → = evaluation-level mechanism
    → Feeling-Sources.md §2 L1 → interoceptive = sensor-level territory
    → Body-Coupling.md → coupling may modulate A-gate per entity
```

### §3.10 — Type A Complexity Gradient: A₀→A₃ (v0.5 new: R19 drill)

```
⭐⭐ R19 DRILL — NEONATE SWEET TASTE: A or B?

  QUESTION:
  Neonates prefer sweet > bitter (🟢 established). Sweet taste in neonates
  là Type A (evaluative, opioid) hay Type B (direct state, non-opioid)?

  TENSION:
  Framework v0.4 define:
    Type A = evaluative + opioid + cần compiled chunks
    Type B = direct state + non-opioid + hardware from birth

  Neonate sweet taste:
    → Hardware from birth (mọi trẻ sơ sinh) → ĐẶC TÍNH B
    → Opioid-mediated (naltrexone blocks) → ĐẶC TÍNH A
    → = CROSS-CUTS A/B binary!


  EVIDENCE:

  🟢 Steiner 1973, 1979: Gustofacial reflexes — neonates show
    distinct expressions: sweet (tongue protrusion, relaxation)
    vs bitter (gag, rejection). REFLEXIVE, no cortical processing.

  🟢 Blass & Hoffmeyer 1991: Sucrose trên pacifier giảm khóc
    ở neonates. Calming effect well-established.

  🟢 Blass & Ciaramitaro 1994: Naltrexone (opioid blocker)
    GIẢM hiệu quả calming của sucrose ở neonates.
    → Opioid mediation CONFIRMED cho neonate sweet taste.

  🟢 Berridge 2003: Rats decorticated (không cortex) VẪN show
    hedonic reactions tới sucrose → subcortical, không cần PFC.

  🟢 Anencephalic infants (sinh ra không có cortex) VẪN có
    gustofacial responses tới sweet → definitively subcortical.


  CROSS-CUT ANALYSIS:

  ┌──────────────────┬──────────────┬──────────────┬──────────────────┐
  │ Đặc tính         │ Type A       │ Type B       │ Neonate Sweet    │
  ├──────────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────────┤
  │ Neurochemical    │ Opioid       │ Non-opioid   │ OPIOID ✅A       │
  │ Learning req.    │ Compiled     │ Hardware     │ HARDWARE ✅B      │
  │ PFC needed?      │ Yes          │ No           │ NO ✅B            │
  │ Naltrexone       │ Blocks       │ No effect    │ BLOCKS ✅A        │
  │ From birth?      │ No           │ Yes          │ YES ✅B           │
  │ Evaluation?      │ Yes (complex)│ None         │ YES (binary) ✅A  │
  └──────────────────┴──────────────┴──────────────┴──────────────────┘

  → Sweet taste = hardware + opioid = KHÔNG FIT vào A hay B!
  → Resolution cần: refine Type A definition.
```

```
⭐⭐ RESOLUTION: TYPE A CÓ COMPLEXITY GRADIENT

  A/B distinction KHÔNG phải binary ở A-end.
  Type A có SPECTRUM of evaluation complexity:


  TYPE A — COMPLEXITY GRADIENT:

  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
  │                                                                  │
  │  A₀ — HARDWARE-INSTALLED EVALUATION (simplest):                 │
  │    Mechanism: Taste receptor → brainstem → opioid                │
  │    Chunks needed: NONE — evolution PRE-COMPILED                  │
  │    Evaluation: BINARY (sweet receptor fires → "caloric" → opioid)│
  │    From birth: YES                                               │
  │    Examples: Sweet taste, bitter aversion, (possibly umami)      │
  │    Naltrexone: BLOCKS ✅                                         │
  │    = "Evolution đã compile sẵn evaluation đơn giản nhất"         │
  │                                                                  │
  │  A₁ — BASIC COMPILED EVALUATION:                                │
  │    Mechanism: Sensory → compiled chunks → hedonic hotspot → opioid│
  │    Chunks needed: SOME (learned food preferences, 2-6 yrs)       │
  │    Evaluation: MULTI-FACTOR (taste + texture + memory + social)   │
  │    From birth: NO — develops with chunk compilation               │
  │    Examples: Learned food preferences, familiar music             │
  │    = "Food pickiness ở trẻ 3 tuổi"                               │
  │                                                                  │
  │  A₂ — COMPLEX COMPILED EVALUATION:                              │
  │    Mechanism: Rich pattern matching → multi-chunk → opioid       │
  │    Chunks needed: RICH library (years of exposure)               │
  │    Evaluation: RICH (pattern matching + emotional history)        │
  │    Examples: Music appreciation, aesthetic judgment, wine tasting │
  │    = "Phân biệt Beethoven hay hơn background music"              │
  │                                                                  │
  │  A₃ — DEEP COMPILED EVALUATION:                                 │
  │    Mechanism: Abstract schema fit → coherence → opioid           │
  │    Chunks needed: EXPERT-LEVEL (years/decades)                   │
  │    Evaluation: ABSTRACT (schema fit + coherence + elegance)      │
  │    Examples: Mathematical beauty, expert insight, scientific fit  │
  │    = "Einstein thấy equations fit → heart palpitations"           │
  │                                                                  │
  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘


  TẠI SAO A₀ VẪN LÀ TYPE A (KHÔNG PHẢI TYPE B):

  ① Opioid pathway: Sweet → brainstem hedonic circuit → μ-opioid.
    CÙNG pathway với adult food reward, music reward.
    Naltrexone blocks → confirmed. Type B = non-opioid → sweet ≠ B.

  ② Evaluation EXISTS — dù đơn giản nhất:
    Taste receptor fires → "match template: caloric, beneficial" → reward.
    Đây IS evaluation, chỉ là binary.
    Type B = NO evaluation at all (CT afferents → state change, no matching).

  ③ Contrast trực tiếp:
    Touch (Type B): CT afferents → posterior insula → state change.
      Naltrexone = NO EFFECT (Loseth 2019). Non-opioid. No evaluation.
    Sweet (Type A₀): Taste receptors → brainstem → opioid.
      Naltrexone = BLOCKS (Blass 1994). Opioid. Binary evaluation.
    → Qualitatively DIFFERENT pathways → different types.


  ⭐ A₀ = EVOLUTIONARY SHORTCUT:

  WHY evolution PRE-INSTALLED A₀:

    Type B sufficient cho survival AFTER contact made:
      → Touch = "safe contact" (CT afferents)
      → Warmth = "temperature OK" (thermoreceptors)
      → Vestibular = "motion OK"

    But infant ALSO needs to EVALUATE food — LIFE OR DEATH:
      → Breast milk (sweet, caloric) vs toxic substance (bitter)
      → CANNOT wait for compiled chunks — infant starves/poisons
      → Solution: PRE-INSTALL binary evaluation for taste
      → Sweet → opioid → approach → survive
      → Bitter → aversion → reject → survive

    = A₀ = evolution's shortcut:
      "We can't wait for learning. Install the simplest evaluation NOW."

    Bitter aversion also = A₀ (hardware-installed evaluation).
    Possibly: umami (protein/amino acid signal) also = A₀.
    (🔴 Hypothesis — umami receptor từ birth chưa confirmed Type A₀)
```

```
⭐ DEVELOPMENT GRADIENT REFINED (§3.8 enriched):

  Neonate (0-3 months): A/B ≈ 5/95
    → 5% = A₀ (hardware-installed opioid: sweet, bitter)
    → 95% = B (non-opioid hardware: touch, warmth, vestibular)
    → A₀ = evolutionary SEED cho toàn bộ Type A system

  Development:
    A₀ PERSISTS underneath → AS chunks compile:
    → Sweet + mẹ cho bú → sweet + warmth + social → COMPOUND
    → A₀ enriched by associations → A₁ (learned food preferences)
    → A₁ enriched by experience → A₂ (aesthetic appreciation)
    → A₂ enriched by expertise → A₃ (expert coherence)

    → Adult still likes sweet = A₀ + compiled layers on top
    → Expert wine tasting = A₀ + A₁ + A₂ (STACKING, not replacing)

  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
  │  Birth:   A₀ only (sweet/bitter binary)                      │
  │     ↓                                                        │
  │  1-2yr:   A₀ + A₁ emerging (food preferences compile)       │
  │     ↓                                                        │
  │  5-10yr:  A₀ + A₁ + A₂ emerging (music, aesthetics)         │
  │     ↓                                                        │
  │  Expert:  A₀ + A₁ + A₂ + A₃ (abstract beauty, coherence)    │
  │                                                              │
  │  B = parallel track, independent, ALWAYS present             │
  │  A₀ = foundation, NEVER lost, layers BUILD on top            │
  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

  → A₀ = FOUNDATION. A₁-A₃ = LAYERS built on foundation.
  → Each layer ADDS evaluation complexity, opioid pathway shared.
  → B = SEPARATE system. Non-opioid. No evaluation at all.


  🔴 TESTABLE PREDICTIONS:

  P-R19a: Sweet taste pleasantness in neonates REDUCED by naltrexone
    → Blass 1994 already suggests this (partial confirmation)
    → Full dose-response curve in neonates = stronger test

  P-R19b: Touch comfort in neonates NOT reduced by naltrexone
    → If A₀/B distinction correct: sweet (opioid) blocked,
      touch (non-opioid) not blocked
    → Direct comparison in same infants = powerful test
    → Prediction: naltrexone blocks sweet calming, NOT touch calming

  P-R19c: Sweet taste pleasantness INCREASES with chunk compilation
    → Neonate: simple pleasant (A₀ only)
    → Child: richer pleasant (A₀ + learned preferences A₁)
    → Expert chef: complex pleasant (A₀ + A₁ + A₂ + A₃)
    → Measurable: hedonic vocabulary richness grows with age/expertise

  P-R19d: Anencephalic infants show sweet preference BUT NOT food pickiness
    → A₀ (subcortical) present → sweet preference YES
    → A₁+ (cortical, compiled) absent → food pickiness NO
    → = Demonstrates A₀ ≠ A₁ (hardware vs compiled evaluation)


  CROSS-REFERENCES:
    → §3.5 Type A/B distinction → REFINED: A has gradient
    → §3.7 H10 × A/B → A₀ bypasses P2/P5 like B but USES opioid like A
    → §3.8 Development Gradient → enriched: neonate A₀ as seed
    → 03-Reward.md §3.6 P5 → A₀ = pre-installed "opioid tag"
    → Compile-Taxonomy.md → A₀ → A₁ transition = earliest compile
    → Body-Coupling.md → A₀ for breast milk → mother coupling seed
```

### §3.11 — B Habituation: Receptor Adaptation vs VTA (v0.6 new: R20 drill)

```
⭐⭐ R20 DRILL — B HABITUATION RATE vs A:

  QUESTION: Does Type B habituate at the same rate as Type A?
  ANSWER: NO. They habituate through DIFFERENT MECHANISMS.


  TYPE A HABITUATION = VTA HABITUATION (central, uniform):

  Mechanism:
    → VTA detects prediction delta → habituates to baseline → delta → 0
    → 🟢 Schultz 1997: reward prediction error signal disappears when expected
    → Location: CENTRAL (VTA, midbrain)
    → What changes: DETECTION SYSTEM habituates (sensor output unchanged)
    → Speed: moderate (sessions → days)
    → ALL Type A rewards habituate this way — universal mechanism

  Example:
    → Chocolate lần 1: VTA delta LỚN + opioid = wow
    → Chocolate lần 50: VTA delta ~0 + opioid (if P1 met) = still good, not wow
    → = "Boring but still tastes good" = VTA habituated, receptor intact


  TYPE B HABITUATION = RECEPTOR ADAPTATION (peripheral, modality-specific):

  Key insight: Type B likely bypasses VTA (§3.5: P3 UNCERTAIN for B).
  → If B bypasses VTA → B signals NOT "baseline-adjusted" by VTA
  → B ONLY habituates at peripheral RECEPTOR level
  → Each modality has ITS OWN adaptation curve

  ┌──────────────────┬─────────────────┬──────────────────────────────────┐
  │ B Modality       │ Adaptation Rate │ WHY                              │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┤
  │ CT touch         │ SLOW (dynamic)  │ CT afferents DESIGNED for         │
  │ (dynamic stroke) │                 │ sustained contact (~1-10 cm/s)   │
  │                  │                 │ 🟢 Löken 2009                    │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┤
  │ CT touch         │ FAST (static)   │ CT responds to MOVEMENT, not     │
  │ (static pressure)│                 │ sustained position → adapts fast │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Temperature      │ FAST            │ Thermoreceptor adaptation =       │
  │                  │ (~5-10 min)     │ physics (well-established 🟢)    │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Exercise eCB     │ SLOW            │ Metabolic process, CB1 receptor  │
  │                  │ (weeks/months)  │ desensitization possible but slow│
  └──────────────────┴─────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────┘

  ⭐ KEY: KHÔNG CÓ "B habituation rate" chung.
  CÓ nhiều rates, mỗi modality khác nhau.
  "Does B habituate slower?" = WRONG QUESTION.
  "Which B modalities habituate at what rate?" = RIGHT QUESTION.


  TYPE B DOES NOT UNDERGO VTA HABITUATION:

  Nếu B bypasses VTA:
    → Mỗi lần CT fires → signal tới posterior insula → pleasant
    → KHÔNG CÓ "VTA đã quen, lần này ít hơn"
    → Each dynamic stroke ≈ "as good as the first"
    → = Type B MORE RESISTANT to experiential flattening

  Contrast:
    → Type A: "boring but still good" (VTA habituated, receptor intact)
    → Type B: "NOT boring AND still good" (no VTA, receptor designed for sustained)

  Evolutionary design:
    → Body needs SUSTAINED RELIABLE reward for basic regulation
    → If B habituated fast → infant loses comfort → dangerous
    → SLOW B adaptation = DESIGN FEATURE for survival


  COMFORT OBJECTS EXPLAINED:

  Child carries same blanket for YEARS. Tại sao không habituate?

    B components (PERSIST):
      → CT afferents: fire during handling (dynamic touch) → SLOW adaptation
      → Thermal: body heat warms fabric → re-warms each re-grip

    A components (habituated but still works):
      → A₁ compiled "safe" schema → A-gate AMPLIFIES B consistently
      → Olfactory association → A₁ (compiled, habituated but gate intact)
      → Novelty = ZERO (VTA completely habituated)

    → B component PERSISTS (no VTA habituation)
    → A-gate PERSISTS (deeply compiled, no delta needed for gate)
    → = "Boring but comforting" — VTA: "nothing new", body: "still good"

    Adult equivalents:
      → Spousal touch 20 years: ZERO novelty, STILL comforting
      → Same coffee every morning: A habituated, B (warmth) persists
      → Favorite old shirt: ZERO novelty, STILL comfortable


  HEDONIC TREADMILL × A/B:

  "Hedonic treadmill" (🟢 Brickman & Campbell 1971):
    → Adaptation to new circumstances → return to baseline

  Framework refines:
    → Hedonic treadmill = VTA HABITUATION applied to life events
    → = PRIMARILY Type A phenomenon

    Type A: luxury food, fancy music, status → TREADMILL
    Type B: basic touch, movement, warmth → RESISTANT

    → B = "hedonic FLOOR" (v0.4 "safe baseline reward" CONFIRMED)
    → "Rich or poor, a hug still feels the same" — B is democratic

  Therapeutic:
    → Burnout/anhedonia: Type A rewards exhausted (VTA habituated)
    → Type B: still accessible as FLOOR
    → Body-oriented therapy: deliberately activate B pathways
    → = Van der Kolk (🟢) mechanism: B pathway → recovery


  🔴 TESTABLE PREDICTIONS:

  P-R20a: CT pleasantness does NOT decrease across repeated daily sessions
    → Contrast: food pleasantness DOES decrease with same-food daily
    → Protocol: 30-day study, hedonic ratings
    → Expected: food habituation curve, touch FLAT

  P-R20b: Comfort object seeking NOT blocked by naltrexone
    → If primarily Type B: opioid blocker should NOT reduce seeking
    → Partial reduction = compound (A + B) confirmed

  P-R20c: Type B rewards less vulnerable to "hedonic treadmill"
    → Cross-SES study: touch/exercise satisfaction vs food/status satisfaction
    → Rich vs poor: B satisfaction similar, A satisfaction differs

  P-R20d: Temperature habituation FAST (~5 min), touch SLOW (~30+ min)
    → Both Type B, DIFFERENT adaptation rates
    → = B habituation modality-specific, NOT uniform


  CROSS-REFERENCES:
    → §3.5 H10 × A/B → P3 VTA uncertain for B → explains no VTA habituation
    → §3.7 B = "safe baseline reward" → CONFIRMED: B resists hedonic treadmill
    → §3.10 A₀→A₃ → A habituation via VTA, B via receptor = DIFFERENT mechanisms
    → Novelty.md §1 → VTA habituation mechanism = A-specific
    → Body-Feedback-Mechanism.md §3.2 → Chunk-Miss = VTA negative delta → A territory
    → Body-Coupling.md → spousal touch persists = B component not habituated
```

### §3.12 — Preview Fidelity Gradient (v0.6 new: R17 drill)

```
⭐⭐ R17 DRILL — PREVIEW FIDELITY × A/B REFINED:

  v0.4 prediction: "A ~40-60% vs B ~10-30%"
  v0.6 drill: ĐÚNG HƯỚNG nhưng A is NOT monolithic.
  Preview fidelity follows A₀→A₃ gradient.


  CORE PRINCIPLE: Preview fidelity = f(cortical proportion)

  Preview = cortical SIMULATION of reward experience.
  Preview activates: CORTICAL representations (chunks, schemas).
  Preview CANNOT activate: PERIPHERAL hardware (receptors, afferents).

  → More cortical pathway = higher preview fidelity
  → More peripheral/hardware pathway = lower preview fidelity

  🟢 Kosslyn 1994: visual imagery activates visual cortex (~30% overlap)
  🟢 Jeannerod 1995: motor imagery activates motor cortex
  🟢 Damasio 1994: somatic marker = body responds to simulation "as if" real
  🟢 Gilbert 2007: affective forecasting biased but REAL


  PREVIEW FIDELITY GRADIENT:

  ┌──────────────────┬─────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────┐
  │ Type             │ Est. Fidelity│ WHY                                  │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ B (pure hardware)│ ~5-15%      │ Peripheral only. CT, eCB, thermo-    │
  │ Touch, exercise  │             │ receptors unreachable by cortical    │
  │                  │             │ simulation. Preview misses hardware.  │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ A₀ (hw-installed)│ ~15-25%     │ Brainstem opioid partially simulable │
  │ Sweet taste      │             │ via gustatory cortex. Taste RECEPTORS│
  │                  │             │ not activated in preview.             │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ A₁ (basic comp.) │ ~25-40%     │ Compiled food/music chunks fire.     │
  │ Food preferences │             │ Partial evaluation. Actual sensory   │
  │                  │             │ component missing.                    │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ A₂ (complex comp)│ ~40-60%     │ Rich compiled chunks fire. Pattern   │
  │ Music, aesthetics│             │ matching mostly cortical.             │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ A₃ (deep comp.)  │ ~60-80%     │ PURELY cortical. Abstract schema fit │
  │ Math beauty,     │             │ = fully simulable internally.         │
  │ expert coherence │             │ No peripheral component needed.       │
  └──────────────────┴─────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────┘

  ⚠️ Percentages = ILLUSTRATIVE, not measured.
  But GRADIENT direction = strong framework prediction.


  "NHỚ VỊ CHOCOLATE RÕ HƠN NHỚ CẢM GIÁC MASSAGE":

  Chocolate memory (A₁, ~30-40%):
    → Compiled taste chunks fire → gustatory cortex (partial)
    → Mini-opioid from evaluation pathway
    → PFC: "tôi nhớ vị đó" → RELATIVELY VIVID

  Massage memory (mostly B, ~10-15%):
    → Compiled "relaxing" schema fires → generic
    → CT sensation COMPLETELY ABSENT (peripheral)
    → PFC: "tôi biết nó dễ chịu" → CONCEPTUAL, not vivid

  → "Nhớ rõ hơn" = higher cortical proportion = more simulable
  → NOT about memory quality — about SIMULABILITY of reward type

  Expert exception:
    → Wine expert "nhớ vị Bordeaux" = ~50-60% (rich compiled chunks)
    → Pianist "nghe Chopin trong đầu" = ~60-70% (auditory cortex richly compiled)
    → = Preview fidelity INCREASES with compile depth WITHIN A level


  WANTING × PREVIEW — ADDICTION VULNERABILITY:

  Berridge (🟢): Wanting = dopamine (anticipation). Liking = opioid (actual).
  Preview primarily activates WANTING.
  High preview fidelity → strong wanting → drive to seek.

    A₃: "Obsessively thinking about solving problem" → intense wanting
      → Einstein "could not eat, could not sleep"
    A₁: "Food craving from thinking about food" → moderate wanting
    B: "I know I need a hug but don't CRAVE it" → weak wanting
      → Touch craving = STATE-DRIVEN (loneliness), not PREVIEW-DRIVEN

  → Type A more vulnerable to CRAVING (preview-driven wanting)
  → Type B resistant to craving (needs actual experience)
  → Marketing: food ads (A₁) effective, massage ads (B) less effective


  ⚠️ "APPARENT B PREVIEW" CAVEAT:

  "Remember massage → body relaxes"
  This LOOKS like B preview. But it's NOT:
    → What fires: compiled schema [massage → relax → safe → parasympathetic]
    → Body responds to SCHEMA (A evaluation component)
    → CT sensation = ABSENT
    → = Preview of "B CONTEXT" (through A pathway) ≠ Preview of "B SENSATION"

  Test: naltrexone should REDUCE schema-associated relaxation
    → If genuine B preview: naltrexone would NOT affect
    → = Distinguishes "schema preview of B" from "actual B preview"


  🔴 TESTABLE PREDICTIONS:

  P-R17a: Imagined food pleasantness > imagined touch pleasantness
    → Rate "how vivid is the pleasure?" for food vs touch
    → Expected: food ~30-40%, touch ~10-15% of actual

  P-R17b: Expert preview > novice preview WITHIN same modality
    → Wine expert vs novice imagining wine
    → Pianist vs non-musician imagining Chopin
    → Expert has richer chunks → more cortical activation

  P-R17c: A₃ preview fidelity > A₁ preview fidelity
    → Mathematician imagining proof completion vs imagining chocolate
    → COUNTERINTUITIVE but: A₃ = purely cortical → fully simulable

  P-R17d: "Apparent B preview" reduced by naltrexone
    → Schema-based relaxation response blocked → confirms A pathway


  CROSS-REFERENCES:
    → §3.7 "nhớ vị chocolate rõ hơn massage" → EXPLAINED by cortical proportion
    → §3.10 A₀→A₃ → preview fidelity maps DIRECTLY onto gradient
    → §3.11 R20 → B no VTA habituation + low preview = "in the moment" reward
    → Feeling-Sources.md §8 → Imagine-Final preview = somatic marker (Damasio)
    → Liking-Wanting.md → Wanting = dopamine → preview drives wanting for A, not B
    → BFM §2.3 → preview fidelity ~20-60% → refined to per-type gradient
```

### §3.13 — A Gates B Neural Process: Insula Gradient (v0.6 new: R18 drill)

```
⭐⭐ R18 DRILL — A GATES B INTEGRATION LOCUS:

  QUESTION: WHERE does A evaluation modulate B signal?
  ANSWER: NOT a single location. A Gates B = GRADIENT PROCESS
  through the posterior-to-anterior insula.

  🟢 Craig 2002, 2013: posterior insula → mid-insula → anterior insula
  = progressively context-enriched interoceptive representation.
  Framework's A Gates B = EXACTLY this gradient applied to Type B signals.


  5-STEP NEURAL PROCESS:

  STEP 1 — POSTERIOR INSULA: B arrives (~0-50ms)
    → CT afferents → lamina I → posterior insula
    → RAW, UNMODULATED first-order representation
    → SAME signal regardless of WHO touches
    → 🟢 Craig 2002: posterior insula = primary interoceptive cortex

  STEP 2 — A EVALUATION fires in parallel (~50-200ms)
    → Context chunks activate: WHO/WHAT/WHERE
    → Social schemas: friend? stranger? threat?
    → Amygdala: rapid threat assessment (LeDoux fast path)
    → = A produces CONTEXT SIGNAL (positive/negative/absent)

  STEP 3 — ANTERIOR INSULA: B + A INTEGRATE (~100-300ms)
    → B signal PROPAGATES anteriorly
    → A context signal arrives TOP-DOWN
    → Anterior insula: INTEGRATES both = EXPERIENCED SIGNAL
    → 🟢 Craig 2009: anterior insula = "seat of subjective awareness"
    → = WHERE "friend touch" DIFFERS from "stranger touch"

  STEP 4 — ACC: CONFLICT CHECK (~200-400ms)
    → ACC monitors: B and A AGREE or CONFLICT?
    → B positive + A positive → silent (smooth)
    → B positive + A negative → FIRES (flags attention)
    → 🟢 Botvinick et al. 2004: ACC conflict monitoring
    → = ALARM, not judge — flags mismatch, doesn't resolve

  STEP 5 — OFC/vmPFC: VALUE ASSIGNMENT (~300-500ms)
    → Final value computation
    → Integrates: insula output + ACC flag + PFC evaluation
    → = NET: approach or avoid?
    → 🟢 Damasio 1994: vmPFC somatic marker


  FLOW:

  B signal → posterior insula (raw)
              → mid-insula (context begins)
                 → anterior insula (B + A = EXPERIENCE)
                    → ACC (conflict?) + OFC/vmPFC (value)


  4 OUTCOMES × NEURAL PROCESS:

  ① A positive (friend):
    → Posterior: CT pleasant (same as any touch)
    → A eval: [trusted, safe] → facilitate
    → Anterior insula: A AMPLIFIES B → compound pleasant
    → ACC: silent (no conflict)
    → = Warm, connected, pleasant

  ② A negative (stranger):
    → Posterior: CT pleasant (SAME signal as friend!)
    → A eval: [unknown, possible threat] → suppress
    → Anterior insula: A SUPPRESSES B
    → ACC: FIRES (B positive + A negative = conflict)
    → = Uncomfortable, want to withdraw DESPITE CT pleasant

  ③ A absent (infant, dissociation):
    → Posterior: CT pleasant
    → A eval: MINIMAL (infant: chunks not compiled)
    → Anterior insula: B propagates near-UNMODULATED
    → ACC: nothing to compare → silent
    → = Basic, raw comfort (infant touch)

  ④ A conflicted (attracted stranger):
    → Posterior: CT pleasant
    → A eval: MIXED (attraction + unfamiliar)
    → Anterior insula: MIXED signal
    → ACC: FIRES STRONGLY (multiple conflicts)
    → = "Electrically charged" — excited + cautious


  INSULA GRADIENT × DEVELOPMENT (§3.8 connection):

  Neonate: posterior functional, anterior IMMATURE
    → B propagates unmodulated → all touch accepted
    → = A gate NOT YET FORMED

  ~8 months: anterior DEVELOPING → stranger anxiety emerges
    → A gate FORMING → stranger touch → suppress begins
    → = Stranger anxiety ≈ anterior insula maturation

  Adult: anterior fully FUNCTIONAL → full A Gates B
    → Touch experience highly context-dependent

  Elderly (cognitive decline): anterior may SIMPLIFY
    → A gate LOOSENS → touch more valued in simpler way
    → = "Bà chỉ cần nắm tay" = B re-emerging

  → Insula maturation curve MIRRORS A/B development gradient
  → NOT coincidence — insula gradient IS the A gate mechanism


  ⚠️ FRAMEWORK SCOPE BOUNDARY:

  Framework scope = mechanism at CONCEPT level:
    "A evaluation modulates B hardware signal"
  Neural mapping = INFORMATIVE but below framework abstraction:
    "This happens via posterior-to-anterior insula gradient"
  Framework NOTES mapping for verification anchors.
  Framework does NOT commit to sub-region claims as FRAMEWORK claims.


  🔴 TESTABLE PREDICTIONS:

  P-R18a: Posterior insula activation SAME for friend vs stranger touch
    → Raw B signal → no context effect at posterior
    → Anterior insula activation DIFFERENT → A modulation visible
    → fMRI: posterior ROI no difference, anterior ROI significant difference

  P-R18b: ACC activation HIGHEST during stranger touch
    → B positive + A negative = maximum conflict
    → Higher than friend (no conflict) or object (no B)
    → Measurable: ACC BOLD signal during social touch paradigm

  P-R18c: Anterior insula lesion → touch pleasant regardless of context
    → A gate damaged → B propagates unmodulated
    → = Similar to infant's raw B experience
    → Case study prediction: reduced social gating of touch

  P-R18d: Stranger anxiety onset correlates with anterior insula maturation
    → Before: B dominant, no A gate → accepts all touch
    → After: A gate forming → stranger touch rejected
    → Measurable: infant anterior insula development imaging


  CROSS-REFERENCES:
    → §3.7 A Gates B → NEURAL IMPLEMENTATION specified here
    → §3.8 Development Gradient → MIRROR of insula maturation
    → §3.9 3-type state dependence → Gate-level = anterior insula modulation
    → Feeling.md §4.1 → 3 integration hubs: anterior insula + ACC + vmPFC
    → Feeling-Sources.md §0 → integration hub = where feeling emerges
    → 04-Right-Wrong-Vague.md → ACC conflict detection at varying intensities
    → 🟢 Craig 2002, 2009, 2013 — interoception posterior-to-anterior gradient
    → 🟢 Botvinick et al. 2004 — ACC conflict monitoring
    → 🟢 Damasio 1994 — vmPFC somatic marker
    → 🟢 Singer et al. 2004 — anterior insula in empathy for pain
```

### §3.14 — Temporal Stack Model (v0.7 new: R5 drill)

```
⭐⭐ R5 DRILL — TEMPORAL PROFILES: PRECISION

  QUESTION: §2.3 has temporal sketch (5 ASCII curves) but notes
  "CHƯA CÓ: temporal profile per reward type."
  What determines onset latency, peak duration, and afterglow?

  ANSWER: Temporal profiles follow A₀→A₃ gradient (onset),
  mechanism type (decay), and compound layering (total envelope).


  ❶ ONSET LATENCY = f(EVALUATION COMPLEXITY):

  R19 (A₀→A₃ gradient) + R18 (insula process) → onset prediction:

  ┌──────────────────┬─────────────┬──────────────────────────────────┐
  │ Type             │ Onset       │ WHY                              │
  ├──────────────────┼─────────────┼──────────────────────────────────┤
  │ B (hardware)     │ ~20-100ms   │ Peripheral → posterior insula.   │
  │                  │             │ NO evaluation. Shortest path.    │
```
