### §3.19 — Poincaré Equivalence: Beauty = H10 P4 on Any Domain (v1.0 new: R3 drill)

```
⭐⭐ R3 DRILL — COHERENCE REWARD: MATH × ART EQUIVALENCE:

  QUESTION (from §10):
  "Poincaré claim 'same nature' — cần neuroscience confirm."

  ANSWER: CONFIRMED. 🟢 Zeki et al. 2014 — math beauty activates SAME
  mOFC region as visual/musical beauty. Framework adds: beauty = H10 P4
  operating on ANY domain's chunks. P2 = beauty gate. ② transfers across
  domains via domain-general ACC coherence sensitivity.


  ❶ NEUROSCIENCE CONFIRMATION — mOFC CONVERGENCE:

  🟢 Zeki, Romaya, Benincasa & Atiyah 2014 (Frontiers Human Neuroscience):
    → 15 mathematicians rated 60 formulas for beauty
    → Beautiful equations → medial OFC area A1 ACTIVATED
    → SAME mOFC region also activates for:
      Visual beauty (🟢 Ishizu & Zeki 2011)
      Musical beauty (🟢 Blood & Zatorre 2001)
      Facial beauty (🟢 O'Doherty et al. 2003)

  Framework interpretation:

    Math beauty ───→ abstract chunks (A₃) → ACC coherence ─┐
    Art beauty ────→ sensory chunks (A₁-A₂) → ACC coher. ──┤→ mOFC → opioid
    Musical beauty ─→ auditory chunks (A₂) → ACC coherence ─┘

  = CONVERGENT PIPELINE: different inputs → SAME integration → SAME reward
  = Poincaré's "same nature" = CONFIRMED at neural endpoint


  ❷ BEAUTY = H10 P4 OPERATING ON ANY DOMAIN:

  ⭐ Beauty is NOT a separate aesthetic faculty.
  Beauty = the FEELING of Goldilocks-level pattern coherence.
  = H10 P4 experienced phenomenologically.

  Beauty REQUIRES 3 SIMULTANEOUS CONDITIONS:

    ① Sufficient COMPLEXITY (P4 floor): too simple → no beauty
       1+1=2 → no beauty (trivial, no VTA delta)
       Euler's e^(iπ)+1=0 → beauty (5 constants, unexpected unity)

    ② Sufficient SURPRISE (P3 delta): expected → no beauty
       Known proof 100th time → no beauty (habituated)
       First seeing proof → beauty (novel coherence → VTA delta)

    ③ Sufficient COHERENCE (P4 ceiling): chaotic → no beauty
       Random number string → no beauty (no pattern detected)
       Mandelbrot set → beauty (infinite complexity + underlying order)

  = Beauty = OPTIMAL coherence-to-complexity ratio
  = Goldilocks for pattern recognition
  = SAME mechanism across ALL domains


  ❸ SAME vs DIFFERENT — FRAMEWORK ADDS TO POINCARÉ:

  SAME (confirming Poincaré):
  ┌────────────────┬──────────────────┬──────────────────┬────────────────┐
  │ Dimension      │ Math Beauty      │ Art Beauty       │ Evidence       │
  ├────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────────┼────────────────┤
  │ Reward endpoint│ mOFC → opioid    │ mOFC → opioid    │ 🟢 Zeki 2014   │
  │ Mechanism      │ H10 P1→P5       │ H10 P1→P5       │ 🟡             │
  │ Profile        │ ② Coherence      │ ② Coherence      │ 🟡             │
  │ Goldilocks     │ ~40-70% match    │ ~40-70% match    │ 🟡             │
  │ ACC detection  │ Coherence signal │ Coherence signal │ 🟢 Botvinick   │
  └────────────────┴──────────────────┴──────────────────┴────────────────┘

  DIFFERENT (framework ADDS what Poincaré couldn't articulate):
  ┌────────────────┬──────────────────┬──────────────────┬────────────────┐
  │ Dimension      │ Math Beauty      │ Art Beauty       │ Implication    │
  ├────────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────────┼────────────────┤
  │ Input pathway  │ Pattern-Driven   │ Sensory+Pattern  │ Different road │
  │                │ (internal chunks)│ (external+intern)│ same city      │
  │ Chunk level    │ A₃ (expert)      │ A₁-A₃ (varies)  │ Math = deeper  │
  │ A/B ratio      │ ~95A/5B          │ ~70-90A/10-30B   │ Art has body B │
  │ Body location  │ Diffuse          │ Partly localized │ Different sig. │
  │ Compound       │ Nearly pure ②    │ ①sensory + ②     │ Art = richer   │
  │ Motor response │ Urgency (R4)     │ Mostly savoring  │ Math = fragile │
  │ Temporal       │ Burst (A₃)       │ Sustained        │ R5 stack diff  │
  │ P2 gate        │ Very narrow      │ Wider (hardware) │ Math excludes  │
  └────────────────┴──────────────────┴──────────────────┴────────────────┘


  ❹ P2 AS BEAUTY GATE — WHY NOT EVERYONE SEES MATH BEAUTY:

  ⭐ P2 = chunk base requirement = BEAUTY GATE.
  No chunks in domain → P4 Goldilocks CANNOT fire → no beauty experience.

  ACCESSIBILITY GRADIENT (inversely proportional to P2 requirement):

    Visual beauty (A₁, hardware-aided) ─── MOST ACCESSIBLE
    Musical beauty (A₁-A₂, partial hardware) ── BROADLY ACCESSIBLE
    Literary beauty (A₂, language chunks) ─── MODERATELY ACCESSIBLE
    Mathematical beauty (A₃, expert abstract) ── LEAST ACCESSIBLE
    Physics beauty (A₃, expert + domain-specific) ── VERY NARROW

  → Visual cortex already extracts symmetry → P2 broadly met → most people
    can experience visual beauty
  → Music: auditory system has hardware pitch/rhythm → P2 partially met
  → Math: requires YEARS of abstract chunk compilation → P2 met for FEW
  → = "Tại sao không phải ai cũng thấy toán đẹp"
    = P2 gate highest for math, not lack of aesthetic sense

  Evidence: Zeki 2014 used MATHEMATICIANS, not general population.
  Prediction: non-mathematicians would NOT show mOFC for same equations.


  ❺ "SUBLIMINAL SELECTION BY BEAUTY" — FRAMEWORK MECHANISM:

  Poincaré (1908): "math solutions selected by subliminal self
  on the basis of mathematical beauty."

  Framework translation:
    "Subliminal self" = body-base (B+C areas, NOT PFC)
    "Selected on basis of beauty" = H10 operating in background:

    Step 1: Schema pending (P1) = mathematical gap active
    Step 2: Background processing (Background-Pattern.md)
    Step 3: Chunks that match coherently → ACC fires → opioid
    Step 4: THAT solution gets body-base CONFIRM → reinforced
    Step 5: PFC observes reward → "that's the one!" → articulation

  → Body "selects" elegant solutions BEFORE PFC articulates
  → = Penrose case: "high spirits but couldn't work out why"
  → Body rewarded insight BEFORE PFC saw it

  WHY ELEGANT solutions win (not just correct ones):
    Correct but inelegant: resolves P1 → moderate opioid
    Correct AND elegant: resolves P1 + P4 optimal + P3 high
    → MORE opioid → STRONGER reinforcement → body selects THIS one
    → Beauty is NOT decoration — beauty is SIGNAL of optimal coherence


  ❻ CROSS-DOMAIN ② PRIMING — EINSTEIN'S MUSIC MECHANISM:

  Einstein: "I often think in music. I live my daydreams in music.
  The theory of relativity occurred to me by intuition, and music
  is the driving force behind this intuition."

  Framework mechanism:
    Step 1: Play violin (music ② active)
      → ACC coherence detection = WARM (recently exercised)
      → ② reward pathway = recently active
      → dlPFC in ⑦ Loose Hold mode

    Step 2: Physics chunks also activate (background P1)
      → Already-warm ACC detects coherence MORE EASILY
      → Spreading activation BROADER (music ↔ physics chunks)

    Step 3: Insight probability ↑
      → NOT because music "teaches" physics
      → Because music PRIMES the ② detection mechanism
      → = "Driving force behind intuition" = ② pathway warmed by music

  8 HISTORICAL FIGURES — CROSS-DOMAIN PATTERN:
  ┌────────────┬──────────────────┬──────────────────────────────┐
  │ Figure     │ Primary domain   │ Cross-domain ② hobbies       │
  ├────────────┼──────────────────┼──────────────────────────────┤
  │ Einstein   │ Physics          │ Violin (Mozart), sailing     │
  │ Feynman    │ Physics          │ Bongos, drawing, safecracking│
  │ Heisenberg │ Physics          │ Piano (Beethoven), hiking    │
  │ Hamilton   │ Mathematics      │ Poetry (befriended Wordsworth│
  │ Darwin     │ Biology          │ Beetle collecting, pigeons   │
  │ Tesla      │ Engineering      │ Walking 8-10 miles daily     │
  │ Poincaré   │ Mathematics      │ Geological walks             │
  │ Ramanujan  │ Mathematics      │ Virtually NONE (math = sole) │
  └────────────┴──────────────────┴──────────────────────────────┘

  PATTERN: ALL hobbies = ② coherence activities in other domains.
  Music = temporal pattern ②. Drawing = spatial pattern ②.
  Poetry = linguistic ②. Collecting = taxonomic ②.
  Walking = Background-Pattern facilitator.
  = Body seeks ② across domains, not random pleasure.


  ❼ 4-FACTOR INDIVIDUAL ② PROFILE MODEL:

  ⭐⭐ Individual ② Profile = f(Hardware × Childhood × Exposure × Balance)

  ① HARDWARE (sets CEILING + BIAS):
    → ACC coherence detection sensitivity
    → DRD4 (VTA delta threshold → pattern novelty sensitivity)
    → COMT (dlPFC clear speed → pattern linking speed)
    → Unusual capacities: Tesla (eidetic imagery), Poincaré (forced
      internal visualization by poor eyesight)
    → = CANNOT train — genetic variation
    → Evidence: Gauss prodigy at 3, Ramanujan ② extreme without training

  ② CHILDHOOD COMPILATION (sets DIRECTION + MOMENTUM):
    → First ② experience = P5 SEED for entire trajectory
    → Einstein: compass at 5 → first coherence GAP → physics seed
    → Feynman: father's pattern-teaching → deliberate ② training
    → Darwin: beetle collecting → pattern-observation micro-rewards
    → Hamilton: 13 languages → linguistic ② → loss to Colburn → math redirect
    → = CAN be influenced by education, parenting, exposure
    → = SNOWBALL: seed → approach → more ② → deeper → stronger → ...

  ③ DOMAIN EXPOSURE (determines WHERE ② expresses):
    → P2 domain-specific → must have chunks to detect patterns
    → Cross-domain: ② sensitivity transfers, P2 does NOT
    → More domains exposed → more channels for ② reward
    → Feynman: broadest exposure → broadest ② expression
    → Ramanujan: narrowest exposure → narrowest ② (but deepest)

  ④ CHANNEL BALANCE (determines HOW DOMINANT ② becomes):
    → Other channels available → ② = one of many (balanced)
    → Other channels reduced → ② = dominant BY DEFAULT
    → 3 variants:
      Hardware constraint (Poincaré: poor eyesight → ① reduced)
      Environmental constraint (Ramanujan: poverty → ③ reduced)
      Personality/choice (Einstein: "horse for single harness")

  INTERACTION PATTERNS:
    High HW + early seed + reduced channels = EXTREME ②
      (Ramanujan, Tesla)
    High HW + early seed + balanced channels = BROAD ②
      (Feynman, Einstein)
    Moderate HW + strong seed + forced adaptation = DEEP ②
      (Poincaré, Darwin)

  ⚠️ IMPORTANT: causality UNCLEAR in many cases.
  "Reduced social" might be CONSEQUENCE of ② dominance, not cause.
  Biographical data = retrospective + selection bias + hagiography.
  N=8 historical figures ≠ representative sample.
  Hardware vs compilation = cannot distinguish from biography alone.
  Snowball effect = hard to falsify (explains any trajectory post-hoc).


  ❽ BRIDGE INSIGHTS (R3 ↔ framework):

  R3 ↔ R8 (Individual differences — PENDING):
    → 4-factor model BRIDGES R3 into R8
    → Hardware factor = R8 core question
    → Childhood compilation = Education/ files territory
    → Channel balance = connects to mental health

  R3 ↔ R2 (PFC mapping):
    → Beauty endpoint = mOFC (= OFC in §3.18 sub-region mapping)
    → OFC = 5/24 functions → VALUE COMPUTER → beauty evaluation
    → ACC = coherence detection → beauty DETECTION
    → = Beauty = ACC detect + OFC value + opioid release

  R3 ↔ R5 (Temporal Stack):
    → Math beauty = A₃ burst (brief, intense, afterglow)
    → Art beauty = A₁-A₂ sustained (ongoing sensory input)
    → Different temporal stacks → different "flavors" of beauty

  R3 ↔ §4 P5 (Compile Context):
    → P5 opioid tag → approach → ② seed → snowball
    → P5 cortisol tag → avoidance → ② blocked
    → = Childhood compile context DETERMINES ② trajectory


  🔴 TESTABLE PREDICTIONS:

  P-R3a: mOFC activation should correlate with subjective beauty rating
    across BOTH math AND art in SAME individuals (P2 met in both domains).
    → Testable: cross-domain fMRI in math+art experts
    → Expected: shared mOFC correlation if P2 met in both

  P-R3b: Non-experts should NOT show mOFC for "beautiful" equations.
    → Testable: mathematician vs non-mathematician mOFC for equations
    → Expected: mOFC ONLY in mathematicians (P2 gate)
    → Zeki 2014 consistent (used only mathematicians)

  P-R3c: Domain training should INCREASE beauty appreciation WITHOUT
    explicit aesthetic instruction (P2 deepens → P4 accessible).
    → Testable: longitudinal math training → beauty rating changes
    → Expected: beauty ∝ domain expertise

  P-R3d: Cross-domain ② correlation (math↔music) should be positive
    but imperfect — moderated by P2 level in each domain.
    → Testable: math beauty × music beauty in experts + ACC baseline
    → Expected: positive r, not perfect (domain-general + domain-specific)

  P-R3e: ② priming: ② activity in one domain should INCREASE ②
    performance in another domain shortly after (priming effect).
    → Testable: music listening → math insight task performance
    → Expected: recent ② activity → faster insight (ACC pre-warmed)


  CROSS-REFERENCES:
    → §3.4 Poincaré Equivalence (original brief analysis → NOW confirmed)
    → §2 Profile ② Coherence — beauty = Profile ② at maximum
    → §7 Coherence Reward — ACC → opioid pipeline = beauty mechanism
    → §8 Developmental Path — childhood P5 → adult ② capacity
    → §4 Compile Context → P5 as beauty trajectory determinant
    → §6 Flow — flow = sustained ②, beauty = peak ② burst
    → Drill-Reward-Feeling-Cases.md §1 — 8 expert accounts (biographical data)
    → Background-Pattern.md — "subliminal selection" mechanism
    → Domain-Mapping-Drive.md — Zone 2 = Goldilocks = beauty zone
    → Feeling.md §8 — feeling quality = f(chunk library) → beauty quality
    → PFC-Hardware.md — DRD4/COMT → hardware factor
    → 🟢 Zeki et al. 2014 — mathematical beauty and mOFC
    → 🟢 Ishizu & Zeki 2011 — visual beauty and mOFC
    → 🟢 Blood & Zatorre 2001 — musical chills and ventral striatum
    → 🟢 O'Doherty et al. 2003 — facial beauty and OFC
    → 🟢 Poincaré 1908 — Science and Method (primary source)
```

### §3.20 — 5 Forces Holding Model: Sustaining Long Creative Arcs (v1.1 new: R3 extended)

```
⭐⭐ R3 EXTENDED — WHY GENIUSES PERSIST WHEN COST > REWARD:

  QUESTION (emerged from R3 analysis):
  Einstein 1907-1915: 8 years. Phases stuck. Cost > reward for long stretches.
  ② micro-rewards ALONE insufficient to hold through years of frustration.
  WHAT mechanism HOLDS through extended creative arcs?
  And WHY contribute to COLLECTIVE rather than keep for personal use?

  ANSWER: 5 FORCES compound holding. Trust thái độ = prerequisite
  for collective contribution. SAME ② mechanism can serve opposite
  directions depending on childhood compilation of collective valence.


  ❶ 5 FORCES HOLDING MODEL (compound, not single):

  ┌─────────────────────┬────────────────────────────────────────────┐
  │ Force               │ Mechanism                                   │
  ├─────────────────────┼────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ F1: MEANING         │ Life-level Anchor-Schema (Meaning.md §1)   │
  │ (Life Anchor)       │ = "Tôi LÀ physicist" compiled deep         │
  │                     │ → CONTINUOUS background identity-coherence  │
  │                     │ → Hold qua dissonance: "khó nhưng ĐÚNG"    │
  │                     │ → Absent: "để làm gì?" → break dễ          │
  ├─────────────────────┼────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ F2: GAP-DIRECTION   │ Persistent P1 at life scale (Gap-Dir.md)   │
  │ (Zeigarnik life)    │ = "Newton + Maxwell XUNG ĐỘT" → ACC fire  │
  │                     │ → PFC ⑧ Active Lock — CANNOT release       │
  │                     │ → "Nghỉ một thời gian → lại bị thôi thúc" │
  │                     │ → Background-Pattern CONTINUES during rest  │
  │                     │ → Absent: có meaning nhưng không biết hướng │
  ├─────────────────────┼────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ F3: ② MICRO-REWARDS │ Intermittent reinforcement (§6-§7)         │
  │ (Intermittent ②)    │ = Mỗi sub-insight → opioid → "đúng hướng" │
  │                     │ → Intermittent = STRONGEST reinforcement    │
  │                     │   (🟢 Skinner variable ratio schedule)      │
  │                     │ → ALONE insufficient for years-long arcs    │
  │                     │ → But NECESSARY as periodic confirmation    │
  ├─────────────────────┼────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ F4: TRUST THÁI ĐỘ   │ Body-base smooth with collective (NEW)     │
  │ (Collective trust)  │ = DEFAULT valence toward humanity = APPROACH│
  │                     │ → Willingness to CONTRIBUTE, chịu cost      │
  │                     │ → = GATE deciding WHO benefits from ②       │
  │                     │ → Absent: solve for self only (free-rider)  │
  │                     │ → Inverted: use intelligence AGAINST (⬇)    │
  ├─────────────────────┼────────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ F5: RECOGNITION     │ Status/peer acknowledgment (Status.md)      │
  │ (Social ③)          │ = "Được công nhận" = status → resource map  │
  │                     │ → CAN override material deficit             │
  │                     │ → Absent: F1+F2+F3 must hold alone          │
  │                     │ → Paradox: pre-fame = most creative (⬇)     │
  └─────────────────────┴────────────────────────────────────────────┘

  5 FORCES = COMPOUND — mỗi force hold 1 tầng:
    F1 = WHY (identity direction)
    F2 = WHERE (specific gap direction)
    F3 = CONFIRMATION (am I progressing?)
    F4 = FOR WHOM (self vs collective)
    F5 = VALIDATION (does collective acknowledge?)

  INSUFFICIENT forces → characteristic failures:
    Missing F1: "talented but directionless" (no anchor)
    Missing F2: "meaningful life but stuck" (no gap direction)
    Missing F3: "persistent but unrewarded" (burnout risk)
    Missing F4: "brilliant but selfish" (no collective contribution)
    Missing F5: "contributing but unacknowledged" (Van Gogh risk)


  ❷ TRUST THÁI ĐỘ — NEW DISTINCTION (CHƯA FORMALIZE):

  Collective-Body.md §5: "Trust = ONLY bridge individual ← collective"
  NHƯNG: §5 nói về trust NỘI DUNG. Còn thiếu trust THÁI ĐỘ.

  ┌──────────────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────┐
  │ TRUST NỘI DUNG       │ TRUST THÁI ĐỘ                            │
  │ (Collective-Body §5) │ (NEW — chưa formalize)                    │
  ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ "Chain dài collective │ "Con người NÓI CHUNG là tích cực"        │
  │  hold HOẠT ĐỘNG"     │ = Body-base DEFAULT = APPROACH toward     │
  │                      │   humanity, not avoidance                 │
  │ = COGNITIVE trust    │ = BODY-BASE trust                         │
  │ = Tin hệ thống      │ = CẢM THẤY smooth với mọi người          │
  │                      │                                           │
  │ Source: evidence,    │ Source: CHILDHOOD COMPILATION              │
  │ institution track    │ = [người → ấm → safe] compiled DEEP       │
  │                      │ = Attachment pattern (🟢 Bowlby/Ainsworth) │
  │                      │                                           │
  │ CÓ THỂ có mà không  │ CÓ THỂ có mà không có Loại 1:            │
  │ có Loại 2:           │ "Yêu mọi người nhưng không tin            │
  │ "Biết hệ thống ok,  │  hệ thống nào cả"                         │
  │  nhưng ghét mọi ng." │ = Hippie, artist, anarchist pattern       │
  │ = Free-rider pattern │                                           │
  └──────────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────┘

  CHILDHOOD MECHANISM:
    Secure attachment (🟢 Bowlby 1969, Ainsworth 1978):
      → Caregiver consistent → [người → safe] compiled deep
      → DEFAULT: encounter stranger → APPROACH
      → SPM fire rộng → willing to help, contribute
      → Trust thái độ HIGH

    Insecure/avoidant/disorganized:
      → [người → unsafe / unpredictable] compiled
      → DEFAULT: people = caution/avoidance
      → SPM restricted → help only trusted few
      → Trust thái độ LOW or INVERTED


  ❸ CONTRAST CASE: SERIAL KILLER IQ CAO vs CREATIVE GENIUS:

  ⚠️ NOTE: case examples from public criminal psychology literature.
  Simplified for framework analysis. Individual cases far more complex.
  Biographical data = retrospective + clinical interpretation.

  ┌──────────────┬──────────────────────┬──────────────────────────┐
  │ Force        │ Creative Genius      │ High-IQ Serial Killer    │
  ├──────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┤
  │ F1: Meaning  │ "Hiểu vũ trụ / Tạo  │ "Kiểm soát / Trả thù /  │
  │              │  cho thế giới"       │  Chứng minh power"       │
  │              │ Direction: CONTRIBUTE│ Direction: DOMINATE      │
  ├──────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┤
  │ F2: Gap-Dir. │ Collective-gap:      │ Personal-gap:            │
  │              │ "physics còn thiếu"  │ "phải control mọi thứ"   │
  │              │ Scale: COLLECTIVE    │ Scale: PERSONAL          │
  ├──────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┤
  │ F3: ② Reward │ Insight micro-reward │ Planning micro-reward    │
  │              │ Content: beauty      │ Content: control         │
  │              │ = SAME H10 mechanism │ = SAME H10 mechanism     │
  ├──────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┤
  │ F4: Trust-C. │ HIGH: smooth with    │ INVERTED: hostile toward │
  │              │ humanity → contribute│ humanity → use as objects│
  ├──────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┤
  │ F5: Recognit.│ Peer acknowledgment  │ "Getting away with it"   │
  │              │ = validation         │ = superiority confirm    │
  └──────────────┴──────────────────────┴──────────────────────────┘

  ⭐ KEY: F3 (② mechanism) = IDENTICAL. F4 (trust thái độ) = INVERTED.
  → CẢ HAI dùng CÙNG H10, gap-direction, persistence, ② reward
  → F4 = GATE deciding WHERE intelligence POINTS
  → Reward mechanism = AMORAL — H10 fires for coherence bất kể moral content
  → P5 tag determines direction: childhood compilation decides

  Serial killer reward mechanism (framework terms):
    → Planning complex attack: ② coherence (problem-solving)
    → Executing: ④ relief (cortisol drop) + power (Status.md primitive)
    → Escaping: ② coherence (prediction confirmed)
    → = COMPOUND ②+④+status → intense → REINFORCING
    → Childhood: [người → threat/object] compiled under trauma
    → = P5 cortisol-tagged toward people → approach = predatory

  ⚠️ This is FRAMEWORK-LEVEL mechanism analysis.
  NOT clinical diagnosis. Individual cases involve many more factors
  (genetics, neurological damage, substance abuse, specific triggers).
  Framework identifies mechanism TYPE, not individual causation.


  ❹ RECOGNITION CAN EXCEED MATERIAL COMFORT:

  "Reward từ 'được công nhận' > 'ăn ngon mặc đẹp'?"

  Framework: CÓ THỂ. Không phải hijack — là EVOLUTION DESIGN.

    ① Status.md: recognition = RESOURCE ACCESS MAP node
       → "Được công nhận" = predict FUTURE resource access
       → Body compile: [recognized → future safe → approach]
       → Body evaluate "recognized" = HIGHER survival value
         than "ăn ngon RIGHT NOW" (aggregate over time)

    ② Collective-Body.md: chain dài sống ở collective
       → "Ăn ngon" = short chain (immediate body-base)
       → "Được công nhận" = access collective resource network
       → LONGER chain, HIGHER expected value (aggregate)

    ③ Meaning.md: Life-level anchor > daily anchor
       → "Ăn ngon" = daily satisfaction → minutes
       → "Được công nhận cho công trình" = life-level → YEARS
       → Life-level OVERRIDE daily-level discomfort
       → = DESIGNED: short pain acceptable if life-anchor satisfied

    "PFC không check lại à?"
    → PFC KHÔNG CẦN check — body-base ALREADY evaluated:
      recognition > food AT BODY LEVEL (not PFC override)
    → PFC confabulate: "tôi hi sinh vì khoa học"
    → Body truth: [recognized → status → resource access → safe]
    → = RATIONAL at body-base, not "hijack" or "delusion"

    ⚠️ GIỚI HẠN: L0 survival FLOOR
    → Malnutrition → L0 signal OVERRIDE status reward
    → Tesla cuối đời: health COLLAPSE despite meaning intact
    → = Body-Base.md L0 = ultimate constraint


  ❺ HISTORICAL CASES × 5 FORCES:

  ⚠️ NOTE: biographical data = retrospective + selection bias.
  Framework mapping = INTERPRETATION, not established fact.
  Historical figures' inner states = inferred from writings + behavior.

  TESLA (chết nghèo, bị exploit):
    F1: ⭐⭐ CỰC MẠNH — "tạo tương lai cho nhân loại"
    F2: ⭐ Persistent — electromagnetic gaps liên tục
    F3: ⭐ STRONG — eidetic visualization = rich ② feedback
    F4: PARTIAL — trust HUMANITY abstract, distrust specific people
    F5: COLLAPSED — early recognition → later ignored
    → F1 HELD alone after F5 collapsed → SUSTAINABLE nhưng
      without F5 reality-check → distorted over time
      (pigeon love, death ray claims, increasingly grandiose)
    → = F1 without F5 = meaning holds but may DRIFT (1B, not 1A)

  VAN GOGH (không được công nhận, tự sát):
    F1: ⭐⭐ Compulsive — "tôi PHẢI vẽ" (override survival)
    F2: ⭐ Visual-aesthetic gaps = persistent
    F3: ⭐⭐ Art ② STRONG — mỗi stroke = visual micro-feedback
         (art ② > theoretical science ② vì ① sensory compound)
    F4: THẤP — isolated, mental illness, few connections
         BUT: Theo = 1 DEEP trust proxy → channel to collective
    F5: NEAR ZERO — chỉ bán 1 tranh khi sống
    → F3 strongest force (art has immediate sensory ② feedback)
    → F5 absent → F1+F3 hold alone → fragile → breakdown
    → Art/music domain: F3 CÓ THỂ sufficient intermittently
      vì sensory compound reward (khác theoretical domains)

  EINSTEIN (pre-fame vs post-fame):
    F1: ⭐ STRONG — "hiểu cách vũ trụ vận hành"
    F2: ⭐ CLEAR — Newton-Maxwell conflict = specific direction
    F3: ⭐ Frequent — thought experiments = rich ② source
    F4: MODERATE-HIGH — tin physics community, later: humanitarian
    F5: Pre-fame LOW → post-1919 EXTREME
    → MOST creative period = BEFORE fame (1905-1915)
    → Post-fame: F5 amplifies BUT expectations → pressure → cortisol
    → Unified field theory: STUCK 25 years (F5 + F2 nhưng F3 dried up)

    ⭐ RECOGNITION PARADOX:
    → Pre-fame: F1+F2+F3 = pure ② → maximum creativity
    → Post-fame: F5 adds → sustaining BUT constraining
    → = Recognition SUSTAINS but can REDUCE creativity
    → = Expectation pressure → cortisol → ② pathway disrupted
    → = WHY "sophomore slump" exists across creative domains


  ❻ COLLECTIVE-LEVEL: "CHO ĐI VÔ TƯ" = RATIONAL AT SCALE:

  Einstein không thể "ăn" E=mc² (non-rivalrous knowledge).
  Share → collective improve → collective serve Einstein BETTER.

  Gap-Direction.md §10.5 + Connection.md §8:
    → "Cây xoài chín sai trĩu quả — ăn 1 mình không hết"
    → Knowledge = ZERO marginal cost to share + POSITIVE collective return
    → Collective improvement → individual benefit (indirect, distributed)
    → Body compile SHORT: [share → recognition → ấm]. Done.
    → Full chain lives at CẤP 2 collective, cá nhân trust.

  F4 (trust thái độ) = PREREQUISITE for this to work:
    → Without F4: "có knowledge, giữ cho mình" = rational at individual
    → WITH F4: "có knowledge, share" = rational at collective+individual
    → F4 = GATE enabling collective knowledge sharing
    → = WHY attachment style → collective contribution pattern


  🔴 TESTABLE PREDICTIONS:

  P-R3f: Secure attachment (childhood) should correlate with
    willingness to contribute to collective goods (volunteer, share,
    open-source) — controlling for other variables.
    → Testable: attachment style × prosocial behavior survey
    → Expected: secure > insecure for unpaid contribution

  P-R3g: Recognition (F5) should show DIMINISHING returns for
    creativity in high-recognition individuals (recognition paradox).
    → Testable: fame timeline × creative output in scientists/artists
    → Expected: peak creativity BEFORE or DURING early recognition

  P-R3h: Artists/musicians should show HIGHER persistence than
    theoretical scientists at EQUAL recognition levels, due to
    stronger F3 (sensory ② compound > pure abstract ②).
    → Testable: persistence rates × domain × recognition level
    → Expected: art/music persist longer with low recognition


  CROSS-REFERENCES:
    → §3.19 R3 Poincaré Equivalence — parent analysis
    → Meaning.md v2.0 §1 — life-level Anchor-Schema = F1
    → Gap-Direction.md v1.0 — gap has direction = F2
    → Status.md v2.0 — Resource Access Map, recognition = F5
    → Connection.md v3.1 §3 — 3 Generative Primitives, ❸ Per-Agent Valence
    → Collective-Body.md v1.1 §5 — trust = bridge (content trust, NOW + attitude trust)
    → Empathy.md v2.0 — SPM wide/narrow = trust thái độ expression
    → Body-Base.md §3 — L0 ultimate constraint (recognition FLOOR)
    → §3.17 R16 Strategy A→B — childhood compilation → defense strategy
    → 🟢 Bowlby 1969 — attachment theory (trust thái độ foundation)
    → 🟢 Ainsworth 1978 — attachment styles
    → 🟢 Skinner — variable ratio schedule (intermittent reinforcement)
    → ⚠️ Serial killer analysis = framework-level, NOT clinical diagnosis
    → ⚠️ Biographical data = retrospective + hagiography risk
    → ⚠️ "Recognition paradox" = observed pattern, causality unclear
```

### §3.21 — Developmental Data: Childhood P5 → Adult Reward Capacity (v1.2 new: R6 drill)

```
⭐⭐ R6 DRILL — DEVELOPMENTAL DATA: LONGITUDINAL EVIDENCE:

  QUESTION (from §10):
  "Childhood P5 → adult flow = theoretical chain, cần data."
  §8.1-§8.2 already has framework chain. R6 asks: IS THERE EVIDENCE?

  ANSWER: YES — multiple converging longitudinal + experimental sources.
  Chain is NOT just theoretical. P5 mechanism maps onto 5 established
  research programs. + Compound Tag Accumulation Model formalizes
  how individual tags → domain schemas → lifetime trajectory.


  ❶ RESEARCH FOUNDATION — 6 CONVERGING EVIDENCE LINES:

  🟢 Ryan & Deci SDT (2000, 2020) — LONGITUDINAL:
    → Autonomy-supportive environments PRESERVE intrinsic motivation
    → Controlling feedback UNDERMINES intrinsic motivation
    → Children in supportive environments → adults who self-select challenges
    → = P5 approach tag preserved when compile context = novelty-path
    → SDT "intrinsic motivation" = framework's "approach-tagged chunks"

  🟢 Harter (1981, 1992) — LONGITUDINAL:
    → Intrinsic vs extrinsic motivation orientation MEASURED
    → Intrinsic orientation in elementary school → predicts academic
      persistence YEARS later
    → = P5 tag direction in childhood → PREDICTS adult behavior pattern
    → Widely replicated, established instrument

  🟢 Lepper, Greene & Nisbitt (1973) — EXPERIMENTAL:
    → Children draw freely → give expected reward → drawing DROPS
    → = Overjustification effect: extrinsic reward OVERWRITES P5 tag
    → Mechanism: body-state shifts from curiosity+opioid to instrumental
    → P5 tag CHANGES from "approach (intrinsic)" to "instrumental"
    → Remove reward → no P5 driver → activity drops
    → = P5 tag VULNERABILITY to pathway shift
    → Classic study, highly replicated

  🟢 Mueller & Dweck (1998) — EXPERIMENTAL:
    → Praise type → behavior change:
      "You're smart" → avoidance of challenge (fear of disproving)
      "You worked hard" → approach challenge (effort = learnable)
    → = Praise type → P5 tag direction for ENTIRE domain
    → "Smart" praise = threat-path: performance anxiety → avoidance tag
    → "Effort" praise = novelty-path: process valued → approach tag
    → Robust across cultures

  🟢 Sroufe et al. (2005) — Minnesota Longitudinal Study:
    → 30+ YEARS following same cohort from infancy
    → Attachment quality at 12 months → predicts:
      competence, relationships, psychopathology ACROSS development
    → = Closest longitudinal evidence for childhood P5 → adult capacity
    → Framework mapping:
      Secure attachment = B FLOOR solid → curiosity enabled
      → approach P5 tags accumulate → adult: flow accessible
      Insecure avoidant = B FLOOR disrupted → reduced exploration
      → avoidance/neutral P5 tags → adult: relief-only, flow harder
      Disorganized = B FLOOR chaotic → inconsistent P5 tags
      → adult: unpredictable reward response

  🟢 Bowlby (1969) + Ainsworth (1978) — FOUNDATIONAL:
    → Secure attachment → exploration (secure base phenomenon)
    → = Body-base safety (B floor) → enables curiosity (A exploration)
    → = Approach P5 tags accumulate ONLY when B floor present
    → Without secure base → exploration inhibited → fewer approach tags

  🟡 Oudeyer et al. (2016) — COMPUTATIONAL:
    → "Learning progress ITSELF generates motivation"
    → = H10 micro-reward chain: learn → opioid → want more → learn more
    → Early disruption → impair SELF-REINFORCING CYCLE
    → = Once P5 approach tags begin accumulating → SNOWBALL
    → Once disrupted → recovery requires EXTERNAL intervention


  ❷ 4-PATHWAY × P5 TAG MODEL (Compile-Taxonomy §3 integrated):

  ⭐ Compile-Taxonomy identifies 4 pathways. EACH creates DIFFERENT P5 tags:

  ┌────────────────────────┬──────────────────────┬──────────────────────┐
  │ Pathway                │ Body State at Compile│ Adult Reward Profile  │
  ├────────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┤
  │ ① Hardware Fit         │ Dopamine/opioid      │ ② coherence natural  │
  │   (body tự reward)     │ (APPROACH tag)       │ flow ACCESSIBLE      │
  │                        │                      │ sustainable decades  │
  ├────────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┤
  │ ② Trust Install        │ Trust-warmth         │ Depends on collective│
  │   (nghe mẹ → compile)  │ (moderate APPROACH)  │ chain holding. If    │
  │                        │                      │ chain breaks → drift │
  ├────────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┤
  │ ③ Social Default       │ Neutral-conformity   │ ④ relief dominant    │
  │   (mọi người đều đi)   │ (weak/NEUTRAL tag)   │ (obligation fulfill) │
  │                        │                      │ "xong rồi" > "hay"  │
  ├────────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┤
  │ ④ Threat Avoidance     │ Cortisol-NE          │ ④ relief ONLY        │
  │   (sợ bị mắng)         │ (AVOIDANCE tag)      │ burnout trajectory   │
  │                        │                      │ "giỏi MÀ không thích"│
  └────────────────────────┴──────────────────────┴──────────────────────┘

  ⭐ KEY INSIGHT: Adult reward capacity = NOT random trait.
  = Accumulated P5 tags through childhood × pathway used.
  = "Talent" = early opioid-tagged exposure + hardware fit + years
  = NOT random "talent gene" (hardware SEED có vai trò nhưng KHÔNG quyết định)


  ❸ SENSITIVE PERIODS — 4 WINDOWS (not critical periods):

  §3.8 Development Gradient + Child-Dev-Mechanism §3:

  WINDOW 1 — Foundation (0-3 tuổi):
    A/B ≈ 5-20% / 95-80%. Type B dominant.
    P5 tags primarily from BODY experience: touch, warmth, co-regulation.
    → Body-base FOUNDATION forming.
    → Attachment quality = P5 FOUNDATION tag (🟢 Sroufe 2005).
    → Tag type: [người → safe] vs [người → unsafe]
    → This tag PERSISTS deepest (first compiled, most repeated).

  WINDOW 2 — Exploration (3-7 tuổi):
    A/B ≈ 40/60. Type A expanding rapidly.
    P5 tags from PLAY + exploration. THE WINDOW where approach/avoidance
    tags for DOMAINS compile en masse.
    → "Piano" example (Child-Dev §3.2): 2 cách dạy → 2 tags → 2 trajectories
    → Emotional peak tags weight MOST here (single-shot compile §2.1 kênh ②)
    → 1 STRONG avoidance tag can override many mild approach tags

  WINDOW 3 — Deepening (7-12 tuổi):
    A/B ≈ 50/50. Domain-specific P5 tags deepening.
    School begins → threat vs novelty pathway DIVERGES sharply.
    → "Ghét toán" or "thích toán" compiled here → persists decades.
    → Education system = MASS P5 TAG INSTALLATION mechanism
    → Threat-path education → avoidance tags for ENTIRE domains

  WINDOW 4 — Identity (12-18 tuổi):
    A/B ≈ 60/40. Social evaluation INTENSE.
    P5 tags COMPOUND with social (③) tags. Identity formation.
    → P5 tags consolidate into Anchor-Schema (Meaning.md)
    → "Tôi là người thích X" = accumulated approach tags → identity chunk
    → "Tôi ghét Y" = accumulated avoidance tags → identity chunk
    → Reconsolidation still possible but harder (deeper compilation)

  🟡 NOT "critical period" (Lorenz binary):
    Sensitive period = compile EASIER, tag ATTACHES STRONGER.
    Later reconsolidation possible (§3.16 R15, §3.17 R16).
    But HARDER — requires destabilization of compiled foundation.


  ❹ COMPOUND TAG ACCUMULATION MODEL:

  ⭐ HOW individual tags → domain schemas → lifetime trajectory:

  Each domain accumulates tags over years:

    Domain X: [approach₁ + approach₂ + ... + avoidance₁ + neutral₃ + ...]
    NET tag direction = Σ(approach) - Σ(avoidance) × f(peak_weight)

  Where peak_weight = emotional peak tags weighted MORE:
    → Single-shot compile (kênh ②) = 1 event STRONG tag
    → Repetition compile (kênh ①) = many events MODERATE tags
    → PEAK NEGATIVE > PEAK POSITIVE per event (asymmetry):
      Miss threat = death, miss reward = next time
      → Evolution: negative peak tags STRONGER per event
      → = "1 lần bị mắng khi giải toán sai > 20 lần giải toán êm ả"

  Net tag → schema:
    → Strong net approach → schema "domain X = enjoy" → ② accessible
    → Strong net avoidance → schema "domain X = threat" → ④ only
    → Weak net → schema "domain X = neutral" → no strong reward either way

  Schema → trajectory:
    → Approach schema → seek domain → compile deeper → ② stronger → SNOWBALL
    → Avoidance schema → avoid domain → no new compilation → tag FROZEN

  ⭐ SNOWBALL BIDIRECTIONAL:
    Approach snowball: approach → seek → compile → more approach → seek more
    Avoidance snowball: avoidance → avoid → no compile → tag stays → avoid more
    → BOTH are self-reinforcing loops
    → BREAKING avoidance loop requires EXTERNAL intervention
      (safe context + guided re-exposure + reconsolidation window)


  ❺ OVERJUSTIFICATION = P5 TAG OVERWRITE:

  🟢 Lepper et al. 1973:
    Free drawing → expected reward → drawing DROPS

  Framework mechanism:
    Phase 1: Draw freely → body state: curiosity + opioid → P5 approach tag
    Phase 2: Expected reward announced → body state SHIFTS:
      now [draw → get sticker] = INSTRUMENTAL, not curiosity
    Phase 3: P5 tag OVERWRITES from "approach (intrinsic)" to
      "instrumental (extrinsic)" = Pathway ④ territory
    Phase 4: Remove reward → no P5 driver → activity drops
    Phase 5: Tag persists → child now "less interested" than before experiment

  → P5 tag is VULNERABLE to pathway shift
  → Pathway ① → ④ shift = DESTRUCTIVE (intrinsic → extrinsic)
  → Reverse (④ → ①) much HARDER (need new approach experiences
    strong enough to overwrite instrumental tag)

  IMPLICATION FOR EDUCATION:
    → Reward PROCESS (effort, exploration) not OUTCOME (grade, completion)
    → Mueller & Dweck 1998: "effort praise" = novelty-path P5 tag
    → "Smart praise" = performance-contingent = threat-path risk
    → Framework adds mechanism: praise type → body-state-at-compile → P5 tag


  🔴 TESTABLE PREDICTIONS:

  P-R6a: Autonomy-supportive childhood → higher adult flow frequency
    → Measurable: SDT questionnaire childhood × adult flow frequency
    → Expected: positive correlation, STRONGER than IQ correlation
    → Mechanism: approach P5 tags → ② accessible → flow prerequisite met

  P-R6b: Emotional peak negative tag → domain avoidance persists DECADES
    → Measurable: trauma in specific domain (fear of water) × adult behavior
    → Expected: single negative peak → avoidance >20 years without intervention
    → 🟢 Partially supported: phobia literature (specific phobias persist lifelong)

  P-R6c: Pathway ④ compilation → adult relief-only pattern
    → Children who learn through punishment → adults who feel relief at
      completion but NO enjoyment of process
    → Measurable: childhood discipline style × adult work satisfaction profile
    → Expected: punitive → relief-only; supportive → approach + coherence

  P-R6d: Attachment security → adult reward RANGE (not just magnitude)
    → Secure → broader reward profile (all 5 profiles accessible)
    → Insecure → narrower profile (primarily ④ relief + limited ①)
    → Measurable: attachment interview × reward profile breadth
    → Expected: secure → broader, insecure → narrower
    → 🟢 Partially supported: Sroufe 2005 (competence breadth)


  CROSS-REFERENCES:
    → §8.1-§8.2: Development chain — NOW has research backing + mechanism
    → §3.8: Development Gradient — average trajectory (R6 adds individual paths)
    → §3.19 R3: 4-factor ② model — "Childhood Compilation" = Axis ② = P5 tags
    → §3.20 R3 Extended: F4 Trust thái độ = childhood attachment → P5 FOUNDATION
    → §3.17 R16: Caregiver trauma → triple impossibility → B → avoidance P5
    → §3.16 R15: System reconsolidation — window for P5 tag modification
    → Compile-Taxonomy.md §3: 4 pathways = 4 ways P5 tags differ
    → Child-Dev-Mechanism.md §3: approach/avoidance tags = P5 at compile level
    → Education/Mechanism.md: pedagogy implications of P5 mechanism
    → 🟢 Ryan & Deci 2000, 2020 — SDT (autonomy-supportive environments)
    → 🟢 Harter 1981, 1992 — intrinsic motivation orientation (longitudinal)
    → 🟢 Lepper, Greene & Nisbitt 1973 — overjustification effect
    → 🟢 Mueller & Dweck 1998 — praise type → behavior change
    → 🟢 Sroufe et al. 2005 — Minnesota Longitudinal Study (30+ years)
    → 🟡 Oudeyer et al. 2016 — learning progress = motivation (computational)
    → ⚠️ "Sensitive period" ≠ "critical period" — reconsolidation still possible
    → ⚠️ Tag asymmetry (negative > positive) = evolutionary reasoning, not measured
    → ⚠️ Compound Tag Accumulation = framework formalization, interaction weights unknown
    → ⚠️ 4-Pathway × P5 mapping = framework synthesis from Compile-Taxonomy
```

### §3.22 — Individual Differences: Hardware × Reward Profile Sensitivity (v1.2 new: R8 drill)

```
⭐⭐ R8 DRILL — INDIVIDUAL DIFFERENCES IN REWARD:

  QUESTION (from §10):
  "Hardware × reward profile sensitivity"

  R8 PARTIALLY PRE-ANSWERED by:
    R3 §3.19: 4-factor ② model (HW × Childhood × Exposure × Balance)
    R3 Extended §3.20: Trust thái độ = childhood compilation
    PFC-Hardware.md: COMT, DRD4 (Hypothesis D), MAO-A, NE α2/α1
    §3.8: Development Gradient (A/B ratio shifts)
    R6 §3.21: P5 tags × 4 pathways

  ANSWER: Individual reward profile = EMERGENT from 5 independent axes.
  R3's 4-factor model GENERALIZED from ② to ALL 5 profiles.
  Hardware affects Type A MUCH MORE than Type B.
  B = evolution's EQUALIZER ("democratic reward").
  COMT × DRD4 interaction creates specific reward PATTERNS.


  ❶ 5-AXIS MODEL — INDIVIDUAL REWARD PROFILE:

  R3 §3.19: 4 factors for ② specifically.
  R8 GENERALIZES to ALL 5 reward profiles:

  ┌──────────────────────┬──────────────────────┬─────────────────────┐
  │ Axis                 │ What It Determines   │ Changeable?          │
  ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼─────────────────────┤
  │ ① Hardware           │ Reward CEILING +     │ NO (genetic)         │
  │   Architecture       │ BIAS toward profiles │ COMT, DRD4, MAO-A,  │
  │                      │                      │ NE, opioid density   │
  ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼─────────────────────┤
  │ ② Childhood          │ Reward DIRECTION +   │ VERY HARD (deepest   │
  │   Compilation        │ P5 tags (R6 §3.21)   │ chunks, reconsolid.  │
  │                      │                      │ possible but costly) │
  ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼─────────────────────┤
  │ ③ Domain Exposure    │ WHERE reward         │ YES (education +     │
  │                      │ expresses (P2 met)   │ experience)          │
  ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼─────────────────────┤
  │ ④ Channel Balance    │ HOW DOMINANT one     │ PARTIALLY (lifestyle │
  │                      │ profile becomes      │ choices, culture)    │
  ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼─────────────────────┤
  │ ⑤ Current State      │ Reward ACCESSIBILITY │ YES (most malleable) │
  │                      │ right now            │ Cortisol, sleep,     │
  │                      │                      │ social context       │
  └──────────────────────┴──────────────────────┴─────────────────────┘

  PARALLEL to PFC-Hardware.md §2:
    Observed Capacity = Hardware × Chunks × Cortisol × Context
    Observed Reward = Hardware × Childhood × Exposure × Balance × State

  ⭐ KEY INSIGHT: "Reward sensitivity" is NOT a single trait.
  = 5-axis EMERGENT property. 2 people can be "equally sensitive"
  but in COMPLETELY DIFFERENT profiles.


  ❷ HARDWARE AXIS — 4 RECEPTOR SYSTEMS × REWARD PROFILES:

  PFC-Hardware.md: 4 receptor systems. Each affects profiles DIFFERENTLY:

  ┌──────────────┬──────────────┬──────────────┬──────────────┬─────────────┐
  │ Receptor     │ ① Sensory    │ ② Coherence  │ ③ Social     │ ④ Relief    │
  │ System       │   Reward     │   Reward     │   Reward     │   Reward    │
  ├──────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ COMT         │ Low impact   │ HIGH: clear  │ Moderate     │ Low impact  │
  │ (PFC clear   │ (sensory =   │ speed → ②    │ (social eval │ (cortisol   │
  │  speed)      │ below PFC)   │ develop speed│ = PFC-partly)│ system)     │
  ├──────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ DRD4         │ Low impact   │ HIGH: chunk  │ Moderate     │ Low impact  │
  │ (Hypothesis  │ (sensory not │ threshold →  │ (social cues │ (not VTA-   │
  │  D threshold)│ VTA-gated)   │ "AHA" vs "ồ" │ = VTA delta) │ gated)      │
  ├──────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ MAO-A        │ Moderate     │ Moderate     │ HIGH: mood   │ HIGH: base  │
  │ (mood global │ (sensory     │ (sustained   │ stability →  │ cortisol ↔  │
  │  stability)  │ valence)     │ affect mood) │ social resil.│ relief mag. │
  ├──────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ NE α2/α1     │ Low impact   │ HIGH: PFC    │ HIGH: threat │ HIGH: NE ↔  │
  │ (circuit     │              │ stability →  │ assessment → │ cortisol →  │
  │  breaker)    │              │ flow access  │ social threat│ relief sens.│
  ├──────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────┼──────────────┼─────────────┤
  │ μ-Opioid     │ HIGHEST      │ HIGH         │ HIGH         │ Moderate    │
  │ receptor     │ (A₀-A₃ all   │ (coherence   │ (social bond │ (relief =   │
  │ density      │ opioid)      │ → opioid)    │ opioid-aided)│ cortisol    │
  │              │              │              │              │ primarily)  │
  └──────────────┴──────────────┴──────────────┴──────────────┴─────────────┘

  ⭐ TYPE B (touch, warmth, exercise) = LESS affected by these receptor systems:
    B = non-opioid, non-PFC, hardware pathways
    → B reward = MORE EGALITARIAN across individuals
    → Hardware individual differences = primarily TYPE A variation
    → B = evolution's EQUALIZER ("democratic reward" — §3.11)

  ⚠️ μ-opioid receptor density = 🟡 consistent with pharmacological
  literature but individual variation in density poorly mapped.
  Table = framework synthesis, NOT established receptor-by-profile mapping.


  ❸ COMT × REWARD PROFILE — IMPROVISER vs SPECIALIST REWARD:

  PFC-Hardware §3: COMT Val/Val (clear fast) vs Met/Met (clear slow).
  PFC-Hardware discusses COMT for COGNITION (draft management).
  R8 EXTENDS to REWARD patterns:

  ┌──────────────────────┬──────────────────────────────────────────┐
  │ Val/Val (Improviser) │ Met/Met (Specialist)                      │
  ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ ② MANY shallow       │ ② FEWER but DEEPER insights              │
  │ insights → MANY      │ → FEWER but STRONGER rewards             │
  │ micro-rewards        │                                          │
  ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Afterglow: SHORT     │ Afterglow: LONG                          │
  │ (draft clears →      │ (draft persists → re-derive →            │
  │  next topic)         │  additional opioid pulses)               │
  ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Cross-domain ②:      │ Cross-domain ②: HARDER                   │
  │ NATURAL (workspace   │ (workspace occupied → new domain         │
  │  clears → new domain)│  blocked by existing draft)              │
  ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Flow: HARDER to      │ Flow: EASIER to sustain                  │
  │ sustain (draft clears│ (draft persists → continuous             │
  │ during flow →        │  coherence stream)                       │
  │ interruption)        │                                          │
  ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Compound: MORE VARIED│ Compound: LESS varied but DEEPER         │
  │ (many domains)       │ (same domain = deep stack)               │
  ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────────────────────┤
  │ Risk: "dopamine      │ Risk: "stuck in rut"                     │
  │ chasing" — jump to   │ (can't escape domain even when           │
  │ next novelty before  │  diminishing returns)                    │
  │ depth compiles       │                                          │
  └──────────────────────┴──────────────────────────────────────────┘

  Val/Met Heterozygous (~50% population):
    Context-dependent switching → FLEXIBLE reward pattern.
    Can flow AND explore depending on state.

  🟡 FRAMEWORK INSIGHT:
    "Improviser gets BORED not because reward is LOW — because DRAFT CLEARS
    before depth compiles. Specialist gets STUCK not because curiosity is
    LOW — because draft WON'T CLEAR for new domain."
    → ≠ personality trait → = HARDWARE managing DRAFTS differently


  ❹ DRD4 HYPOTHESIS D × REWARD (extending PFC-Hardware §4.3):

  DRD4-7R = HIGH chunk threshold (detects LARGE chunks only).
  DRD4-4R = LOW chunk threshold (detects small chunks).

  Extension to REWARD patterns:

    7R: ② rewards RARE but INTENSE ("AHA!" — Ramanujan type)
        Sensory: need STRONGER stimulus for same pleasure (prediction)
        Flow: once IN flow MORE intense, getting INTO flow HARDER
        Domain: NEEDS deep chunk library → shallow domain = frustrate
        Risk: "can't find anything interesting" if domain wrong

    4R: ② rewards FREQUENT but MILD ("ồ..." — steady accumulation)
        Sensory: mild stimulus sufficient
        Flow: easier entry, less intense peak
        Domain: satisfies across breadth → less domain-dependent
        Risk: "content with surface" → may not develop depth

  ⚠️ DRD4 = Hypothesis D (framework 🔴), NOT established.
  BUT consistent with observed individual differences in reward intensity.
  AND: Type B = hardware → NOT affected by DRD4 (B below VTA threshold system).


  ❺ INTERACTION EFFECTS — WHY "TYPE" DESCRIPTIONS FAIL:

  Simple trait psychology: "extrovert = high reward sensitivity."
  Framework: reward sensitivity = 5-axis emergent →
  trait descriptions = LOSSY COMPRESSION.

  COMT × DRD4 INTERACTION:

  ┌────────────────────┬──────────────────────┬──────────────────────┐
  │ Combination        │ Reward Pattern       │ Popular Label        │
  ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┤
  │ Val/Val + 7R       │ Clear fast + high    │ "Thrill seeker"      │
  │                    │ threshold = NEED     │ Jumps to big novel   │
  │                    │ novel BIG experiences│ experiences           │
  ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┤
  │ Met/Met + 4R       │ Clear slow + low     │ "Obsessive expert"   │
  │                    │ threshold = SATISFY  │ Deep within single   │
  │                    │ within single domain │ domain               │
  ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┤
  │ Val/Val + 4R       │ Clear fast + low     │ "Social butterfly"   │
  │                    │ threshold = many     │ Many small rewards   │
  │                    │ small rewards, none  │ from many domains    │
  │                    │ deep                 │                      │
  ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┤
  │ Met/Met + 7R       │ Clear slow + high    │ "Frustrated genius   │
  │                    │ threshold = draft    │  or true genius"     │
  │                    │ stuck + needs BIG    │ BIMODAL: highest     │
  │                    │ chunks              │ genius OR highest    │
  │                    │                      │ frustration          │
  └────────────────────┴──────────────────────┴──────────────────────┘

  COMT × CHILDHOOD COMPILATION:

  ┌────────────────────┬──────────────────────┬──────────────────────┐
  │ Combination        │ Reward Life          │ Implication          │
  ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┤
  │ Met/Met + approach │ DEEP FLOW expert     │ Best case for ②      │
  │ childhood          │ (draft stays +       │ Sustainable decades  │
  │                    │ approach-tagged)      │                      │
  ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┤
  │ Met/Met + avoidance│ RIGID ANXIETY        │ Draft stuck +        │
  │ childhood          │ (cannot escape +     │ threat-tagged =      │
  │                    │ threat-tagged domain)│ worst combination    │
  ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┤
  │ Val/Val + approach │ CREATIVE EXPLORER    │ Breadth + approach   │
  │ childhood          │ (jumps freely +      │ = versatile joy      │
  │                    │ approach-tagged)      │                      │
  ├────────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┤
  │ Val/Val + avoidance│ SCATTERED ANXIETY    │ Jump + avoid = chaos │
  │ childhood          │ (drafts clear +      │ Nothing feels safe   │
  │                    │ threat-tagged)        │ or deep enough       │
  └────────────────────┴──────────────────────┴──────────────────────┘

  ⭐ SAME hardware, DIFFERENT childhood = COMPLETELY DIFFERENT reward life.
  → Hardware sets RANGE. Childhood sets DIRECTION within range.
  → = "Nature sets the instrument. Nurture plays the tune."


  ❻ TYPE A/B RATIO × INDIVIDUAL VARIATION:

  §3.8 shows A/B ratio shifts with age. But individual variation ENORMOUS:

  WHY some adults ~80A/20B, others ~50A/50B:

    ① Hardware: opioid receptor density → A capacity (μ-opioid → A)
       CT afferent density → B capacity (varies less across individuals)
    ② Childhood: touch-rich environment → B strongly compiled → maintained
    ③ Culture: some cultures SUPPRESS physical contact → B neglected
    ④ Domain: some domains = nearly pure A (math), others = rich B (dance)
    ⑤ Cortisol: chronic stress → A capacity impaired → B relatively MORE
       important (but also HARDER to access under stress)

  "Body-base deficit" (§3.8 Stage 5 note) = INDIVIDUAL DIFFERENCE:
    → Some adults: B RICH (exercise, touch, body care) → A+B compound available
    → Some adults: B NEGLECTED → A-only reward → FRAGILE
       (A depends on cortisol state, compile quality, context fit)
    → "Burnout" often = A exhausted + B neglected → BOTH down →
       hedonic emptiness with no floor to recover from


  ❼ DEVELOPMENT GRADIENT × INDIVIDUAL DEPARTURE PATTERNS:

  §3.8 gives AVERAGE trajectory. Individual variation creates 4 DEPARTURES:

  ┌──────────────────┬──────────────────────┬──────────────────────────┐
  │ Pattern          │ Description          │ Mechanism                │
  ├──────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┤
  │ ① Precocious A   │ A develops EARLY     │ High PFC quality +       │
  │                  │ (child prodigy)      │ Hardware Fit + early     │
  │                  │                      │ approach-tagged exposure │
  ├──────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┤
  │ ② Extended B     │ B stays dominant     │ Touch-rich environment + │
  │                  │ LONGER than average  │ B-domain culture         │
  │                  │                      │ (athletes, craftsmen)    │
  ├──────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┤
  │ ③ Arrested A     │ A STOPS developing   │ Threat-path education →  │
  │                  │ at Stage 3-4         │ avoidance tags BLOCK     │
  │                  │                      │ A growth in domains      │
  ├──────────────────┼──────────────────────┼──────────────────────────┤
  │ ④ Reversed A/B   │ A declines           │ Chronic stress →         │
  │                  │ prematurely          │ cortisol → A capacity    │
  │                  │                      │ eroded (McEwen 2007      │
  │                  │                      │ dendrite retraction)     │
  └──────────────────┴──────────────────────┴──────────────────────────┘

  Pattern ③ = MOST COMMON education failure:
    → Child in threat-path school → domain-specific avoidance tags
    → A capacity EXISTS (hardware ok) but BLOCKED by avoidance tags
    → Adult "I can't do math" = NOT hardware limitation
      = accumulated avoidance tags (R6 §3.21 mechanism)
    → Intervention: reconsolidation window (R15 §3.16) + safe re-exposure

  Pattern ④ = burnout mechanism:
    → Chronic stress → sustained cortisol → dlPFC dendrite retraction
    → A capacity physically REDUCED (not just blocked)
    → Recovery requires: cortisol reduction + time + B floor restoration
    → = Body-Base.md circuit breaker engaged


  ❽ 3-VARIABLE SHORTHAND FOR INDIVIDUAL PROFILES:

  Full model (5 profiles × 5 axes = 25 cells) = too complex for practical use.
  COMPRESSED DESCRIPTION uses 3 variables:

    ① A/B Ratio:
       Where on spectrum (pure A → balanced → pure B)
    ② Dominant Profile:
       Which of 5 profiles is STRONGEST (①②③④⑤)
    ③ Breadth:
       How many profiles ACTIVE (narrow specialist → broad generalist)

  EXAMPLES:

    Einstein: High A (90/10), Dominant ②, Moderate breadth (②+③+④)
      → Intense coherence seeker, some social/relief reward, very little B
    Chef: Balanced A/B (60/40), Dominant ①, Narrow (①+④)
      → Sensory-driven, relief from completion, significant body reward
    Therapist: Moderate A (55/45), Dominant ③, Broad (①②③④⑤)
      → Social reward primary, but accesses ALL profiles
    Athlete: Low A (30/70), Dominant B+④, Narrow
      → Body-driven, relief from exertion, minimal coherence/social

  → "Personality" re: reward = this 3-variable profile
  → "Compatibility" in relationships = OVERLAP (not identity)
  → = Why simple "extrovert/introvert" fails to predict reward behavior


  🔴 TESTABLE PREDICTIONS:

  P-R8a: COMT Val/Val → SHORTER flow episodes, MORE domain-switches
    → Met/Met → LONGER flow, FEWER domain switches per unit time
    → Measurable: COMT genotype × flow duration × domain-switch frequency
    → Expected: Val/Val shorter+more, Met/Met longer+fewer

  P-R8b: Type B reward sensitivity has LOWER individual variance than Type A
    → Measurable: SD of touch/warmth pleasure ratings across population
      vs SD of insight/music pleasure ratings
    → Expected: B SD < A SD (B = hardware, A = compilation-dependent)
    → = B = "democratic reward" quantified

  P-R8c: Individual reward profile STABILITY across timescales
    → Short-term fluctuation → Axis ⑤ (cortisol, sleep)
    → Year-level stability → Axes ③④ (exposure, balance)
    → Decade-level stability → Axes ①② (hardware + childhood)
    → Measurable: test-retest reward profile at 1 week / 1 year / 10 years
    → Expected: ⑤ explains short, ①② explains long

  P-R8d: Met/Met + 7R = HIGHEST variance in life satisfaction
    → If domain RIGHT: deepest flow, strongest ② → most satisfied
    → If domain WRONG: draft stuck + no big chunks → most frustrated
    → Measurable: COMT × DRD4 × domain fit × life satisfaction
    → Expected: Met/Met+7R = BIMODAL distribution (very high OR very low)


  CROSS-REFERENCES:
    → §3.19 R3: 4-factor ② model — R8 GENERALIZES to all 5 profiles
    → §3.20 R3 Extended: F4 Trust thái độ = Axis ② for collective direction
    → §3.21 R6: P5 tags × 4 pathways = Axis ② mechanism
    → §3.8: Development Gradient — average trajectory (R8 = departures)
    → §3.11 R20: B habituation modality-specific → B individual diff = per-modality
    → §3.12 R17: Preview fidelity → individual craving vulnerability
    → PFC-Hardware.md §1-§6 — COMT, DRD4, MAO-A, NE (Axis ① specifics)
    → PFC-Hardware.md §2 — Observed Capacity formula (PARALLEL for reward)
    → Body-Base.md v2.0 — circuit breaker, B floor
    → Cortisol-Baseline.md v2.0 — chronic stress → A capacity erosion
    → 🟢 Egan et al. 2001 — COMT Val/Val vs Met/Met fMRI (well-replicated)
    → 🟢 PFC-Hardware.md evidence — Cowan 2001, Haier 1992, Pietschnig 2015
    → 🟡 DRD4 Hypothesis D — framework 🔴, consistent but not established
    → ⚠️ Receptor × Profile table = framework synthesis, NOT established mapping
    → ⚠️ COMT × Reward extension = inferred from COMT × Cognition (PFC-Hardware)
    → ⚠️ COMT × DRD4 interaction patterns = framework reasoning, not tested
    → ⚠️ COMT × Childhood combinations = framework synthesis, observational consistency
    → ⚠️ 4 departure patterns = framework organizing from developmental literature
    → ⚠️ 3-variable shorthand = practical compression, loses interaction detail
    → ⚠️ Individual profile examples (Einstein, etc.) = illustrative, not measured
```

---

## §4 — COMPILE CONTEXT → REWARD QUALITY (P5 EXTENDED)

### §4.1 — P5 hiện tại: direction (opioid vs cortisol)

```
✅ ĐÃ CÓ (03-Reward §3.6):

  P5 = Chunk Association Tag
  → Chunks compiled under curiosity → opioid-tagged → approach
  → Chunks compiled under threat → cortisol-tagged → avoidance
  → "Math learned under fear → adult retrieval fires discomfort"

  = Direction: opioid (approach) vs cortisol (avoidance)
  = Đã formalize, đã có examples
```

### §4.2 — Extension: P5 quyết định REWARD PROFILE nào fire

```
🟡 P5 EXTENDED — KHÔNG CHỈ DIRECTION, CÒN PROFILE:

  CÙNG EVENT: giải được bài toán. KHÁC COMPILE CONTEXT:

  Student A — curiosity compile (Pathway ①: Hardware Fit):
    → Math chunks opioid-tagged (P5 MET fully)
    → Giải được → Profile ② COHERENCE REWARD dominant
    → = "À hiểu rồi!" + ACC resolve + opioid burst
    → = Hamilton's "intellectual want relieved"
    → APPROACH reward → muốn giải thêm → POSITIVE LOOP

  Student B — threat compile (Pathway ④: Threat Avoidance):
    → Math chunks cortisol-tagged (P5 FAILED partially)
    → Giải được → Profile ④ RELIEF REWARD dominant
    → = Cortisol DROP → "xong rồi, nhẹ người"
    → = KHÔNG phải "sướng" — là "hết đau"
    → AVOIDANCE reward → KHÔNG wanting giải thêm → NO LOOP

  ⭐ KEY INSIGHT:
    → Cả 2 activate NAcc/VTA (cùng hardware)
    → Nhưng: Student A → opioid dominant → Profile ②
    → Student B → cortisol drop dominant → Profile ④
    → = KHÁC CHẤT, không chỉ khác LƯỢNG

  REFERENCES:
    → Compile-Taxonomy.md §2.1 (Loại A): [học → mẹ khen → ấm] vs
      [không học → mẹ mắng → đau] = approach vs avoidance
    → Compile-Taxonomy.md §3 (4 pathways): Hardware Fit / Trust Install /
      Social Default / Threat Avoidance
    → 03-Reward §3.6 (P5): chunk association tag → direction
```

### §4.3 — Post-reward chain compile

```
🟡 POST-REWARD CONTEXT CÓ THỂ MODIFY FUTURE REWARD:

  Case X: [giải toán → thường đi chơi sau]
    → Body compile chain: [giải → TIẾP THEO → vui/tự do]
    → Over time: [giải toán] trigger PREVIEW [đi chơi]
    → = Profile ② (coherence) + Profile ⑤ (preview of autonomy)
    → = Compound reward amplified

  Case Y: [giải toán → mẹ mang đồ ăn]
    → Body compile chain: [giải → TIẾP THEO → ăn ngon]
    → = Profile ② (coherence) + Profile ⑤ (preview of sensory)
    → + Social approval (mẹ chăm sóc) = ③ social bonus

  → POST-REWARD CONTEXT compile thành ANTICIPATORY CHAIN
  → Mỗi lần giải toán → body PREVIEW rewards tiếp theo → amplify
  → = "Điều kiện hóa" nhưng framework-specific: compile chain + preview

  ⚠️ DATA LIMITATION: case studies BỊA (theoretical prediction)
  → Cần real data để verify
  → Khó lấy data vì: trẻ không introspect, retrospective = confabulation
```

---

## §5 — PFC + LOSS OF SELF: 8 MECHANISMS (v0.2 expanded)

### §5.1 — Research foundation

```
🟢 PFC TRONG FLOW KHÔNG TẮT — CHUYỂN CHẾ ĐỘ:

  Limb & Braun 2008 (jazz improvisation fMRI — landmark study):
    → DLPFC (self-monitoring, explicit control) → DEACTIVATE
    → Medial PFC (internally motivated processing) → ACTIVATE focal
    → = Dissociated pattern: 1 phần PFC TẮT, 1 phần PFC BẬT

  Perico et al. 2022 (systematic review):
    → Lateral frontoparietal network (task-relevant attention) → TĂNG
    → Medial PFC (self-referential, mind-wandering) → GIẢM
    → Default Mode Network (DMN) → SUPPRESSED

  Katahira et al. 2018 (EEG):
    → Flow = increased frontal theta + moderate frontocentral alpha
    → = Focused attention with reduced cortical arousal
    → ≠ blanket suppression

  Dietrich 2003, 2004 (transient hypofrontality):
    → Original: PFC giảm đồng loạt
    → Later research refined: SELECTIVE reallocation, not blanket suppression
    → Prerequisite: skills in IMPLICIT system (compiled expertise)

  → CONVERGENCE: flow = PFC SELECTIVE REALLOCATION
  → KHÔNG phải "PFC tắt" — là "PFC chuyển sang serve task"
```

### §5.2 — 8 Mechanisms "Loss of Self" (v0.2 — expanded từ 4)

```
⭐⭐ "QUÊN BẢN THÂN" = ÍT NHẤT 8 MECHANISMS KHÁC NHAU (v0.2):

  v0.1 có 4: Flow, Threat, Limerence, Meditation.
  v0.2 thêm 4: Psychedelic, Exercise, Hypnosis, Dissociation.

  ┌──────────────┬────────────────┬────────────┬──────────┬───────────────────────┐
  │ State        │ PFC Mode       │ DMN        │ Amygdala │ Primary Mechanism     │
  ├──────────────┼────────────────┼────────────┼──────────┼───────────────────────┤
  │ ① Flow       │ Selective      │ Suppressed │ Normal   │ Task-driven           │

  │              │  breaker)      │            │          │ over                  │

  ├──────────────┼────────────────┼────────────┼──────────┼───────────────────────┤

  │              │ SUPPRESSION    │            │ (unique!)│ neurochemical         │

  │ ④ Meditation │ TRAINED        │ Suppressed │ Reduced  │ Voluntary attention   │
  │              │ SUPPRESSION    │ (gradual)  │          │ training              │
  │              │                │            │          │ 🟢 Brewer 2011 PNAS   │
  ├──────────────┼────────────────┼────────────┼──────────┼───────────────────────┤

  │   (ego       │ mPFC ↓ nhưng  │ (within-   │          │ → DMN breakdown       │
  │   dissolut.) │ dlPFC-DMN      │  network   │          │ + global integration  │
  │              │ connectivity ↑ │  collapse) │          │ 🟢 Carhart-Harris 2012│

  ├──────────────┼────────────────┼────────────┼──────────┼───────────────────────┤

  │   (runner's  │ (resource      │            │          │ + endocannabinoid     │
  │    high)     │  competition)  │            │          │ 🟢 Dietrich 2006      │
  │              │                │            │          │ 🟢 Fuss 2015 PNAS    │
  ├──────────────┼────────────────┼────────────┼──────────┼───────────────────────┤

  │              │ dACC dampened  │            │          │ redirects PFC         │

  │              │ DLPFC-DMN ↓    │            │          │    Raz 2005           │

  │ ⑧ Dissociat. │ HYPERACTIVATED │ Variable   │ OFF      │ Defensive             │
  │   (trauma)   │ vmPFC + ACC    │            │ (over-   │ overmodulation        │
  │              │ SUPPRESS       │            │  modul.) │ 🟢 Lanius 2010        │
```

### §5.2b — 3 Loại "Loss of Self" (v0.2 key insight)

```
⭐⭐ "QUÊN BẢN THÂN" THỰC RA LÀ 3 HIỆN TƯỢNG KHÁC NHAU:

  ❶ Loss of self-MONITORING = DLPFC off → không tự đánh giá mình
     → Flow ①, Exercise ⑥
     → "Tôi không nghĩ về mình" — vì PFC busy với task/motor
     → Valence: positive (productive states)

  ❷ Loss of self-REFERENCE = DMN off → không còn "tôi" narrative
     → Meditation ④, Psychedelic ⑤
     → "Ranh giới tôi và thế giới mờ đi" — DMN = self-narrative
     → Valence: neutral-transcendent

  ❸ Loss of self-JUDGMENT = evaluative PFC off → không phán xét
     → Limerence ③, Hypnosis ⑦
     → "Tôi không critical nữa" — judgment system suppressed
     → Valence: variable (vulnerable state)

  DISSOCIATION ⑧ = OPPOSITE: không phải "mất" mà "THỪA"
     → PFC hyperactivated → suppress emotion quá mạnh → tê liệt
     → "Mất bản thân" kiểu KHÁC: quá nhiều control → cảm giác trống rỗng
     → Lanius 2010: NGƯỢC với acute threat (threat = PFC thua amygdala /
       dissociation = PFC thắng quá mạnh, amygdala bị đè)

  ACUTE THREAT ② = PFC GONE (khác cả 3 loại trên)
     → Không phải mất monitoring/reference/judgment
     → Mà PFC HOÀN TOÀN OFFLINE → subcortical run everything
     → = Design feature cho survival

  → Framework implication: PFC-Function §7 cần thêm nhiều modes
    không chỉ "offline" — có Reallocation, Reconfiguration,
    Disintegration, Hyperactivation
```

### §5.2c — 6 PFC Modes (v0.2 spectrum model)

```
🟡 PFC KHÔNG PHẢI ON/OFF — CÓ ÍT NHẤT 6 MODES:

  ① NORMAL        = Default waking. DMN active. Self-referential on.
  ② REALLOCATION  = Task-serving. DLPFC→task. DMN suppressed. (Flow)
  ③ RECONFIGURED  = Re-routed by suggestion/training. (Hypnosis, partial Meditation)
  ④ DISCONNECTED  = Circuit breaker. PFC fully offline. (Acute threat, alcohol)
  ⑤ HYPERACTIVATED= PFC suppress subcortical quá mạnh. (Dissociation)
  ⑥ DISINTEGRATED = DMN network collapse + global integration. (Psychedelic)

  ┌──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
  │  DISCONNECT ← ← ← NORMAL → → → HYPERACTIVATE                      │
  │       ④                ①              ⑤                              │
  │  (PFC gone)       (default)      (PFC overdrive)                    │
  │                       ↓                                              │
  │              ┌─ REALLOCATION ② (task-serving)                        │
  │              ├─ RECONFIGURED ③ (suggestion/training)                 │
  │              └─ DISINTEGRATED ⑥ (pharmacological)                    │
  └──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

  → PFC-Function §7 hiện tại chỉ có mode ④ (offline cases)
  → CẦN bổ sung: modes ②③⑤⑥ = Gap cho refine PFC-Function.md
  → 🟡 6-mode spectrum = framework synthesis từ research data
```

### §5.3 — PFC Functions × Flow State

```
🟡 MAP PFC-FUNCTION.MD 24 FUNCTIONS VÀO FLOW:

  TRONG FLOW — CÁI GÌ ON, CÁI GÌ OFF:

  ON (task-serving):
    ✅ PFC directed attention → fully engaged on task domain
    ✅ PFC domain-check → continuous verify smooth vs reality
    ✅ PFC hold → task chunks in working memory (~4 slots)
    ✅ PFC compression → compile task patterns real-time

  OFF (self-referential):
    ❌ PFC self-monitor → "tôi đang thế nào?" → KHÔNG slot
    ❌ PFC time-track → "mấy giờ rồi?" → KHÔNG slot
    ❌ PFC multi-option → "nên làm cái khác?" → KHÔNG slot
    ❌ PFC social-evaluate → "người khác nghĩ gì?" → KHÔNG slot

  → ≠ PFC "full allocation" (model sơ bộ ban đầu)
  → = PFC SELECTIVE REALLOCATION (refined by neuroscience data)
  → = Specific PFC SUB-REGIONS on/off, NOT uniform

  🔴 HYPOTHESIS CẦN VERIFY:
    → Framework dùng "24 functions" — nhưng chưa map sub-regions
    → DLPFC vs medial PFC vs OFC — mỗi cái serve functions nào?
    → Limb & Braun 2008 data → CÓ THỂ map, nhưng cần cẩn thận
```
