## §5b — PFC CONTROL SPECTRUM (v0.3 new: R11+R12 synthesis)

### §5b.1 — 2 Taxonomy Orthogonal

```
⭐⭐ DRILL R11+R12 REVEAL: 2 TAXONOMY KHÁC NHAU, ORTHOGONAL:

  Drive.md §2 — PFC PARTICIPATION (activation level):
    Mode 1-6: Absent → Monitor → Spinning → Resolve → Strategic → Override
    = TRỤC: PFC bận CỠ NÀO? (0% → 95%)
    = QUANTITATIVE (how much)

  Drill §5.2c — PFC CONFIGURATION (qualitative mode):
    6 modes: Normal → Reallocation → Reconfigured → Disconnected →
             Hyperactivated → Disintegrated
    = TRỤC: PFC wired/routed THẾ NÀO?
    = QUALITATIVE (what kind)

  → 2 TAXONOMY ORTHOGONAL — BỔ SUNG, KHÔNG cạnh tranh:

    Flow        = Mode 2/4 (Resolve)   + Config: Reallocation ②
    Acute Threat = Mode 1 (Absent)      + Config: Disconnected ④
    Dissociation = Mode 6 (Override)    + Config: Hyperactivated ⑤
    Meditation  = Mode 5 (Strategic)    + Config: Reconfigured ③
    Psychedelic = N/A (modes break down)+ Config: Disintegrated ⑥
```

### §5b.2 — PFC Control Spectrum

```
⭐⭐ DISSOCIATION + PSYCHEDELIC = 2 CỰC ĐỐI DIỆN:

  PFC CONTROL SPECTRUM:

  OVERCONTROL ←←←←←← BALANCED →→→→→→ UNDERCONTROL
       ⑤                  ①                  ⑥
  Dissociation         Normal          Psychedelic
  PFC suppress       PFC coordinate    PFC disintegrate
  emotion              processing        hierarchy

  ┌──────────────────┬────────────────┬──────────────────┐
  │ DISSOCIATION     │ NORMAL         │ PSYCHEDELIC      │
  ├──────────────────┼────────────────┼──────────────────┤
  │ Emotion: NUMB    │ Emotion: FELT  │ Emotion: FLOOD   │
  │ Self: EMPTY      │ Self: PRESENT  │ Self: DISSOLVED  │
  │ Perception: intact│ Perception:   │ Perception:      │
  │  but colorless   │  normal        │  altered/intense │
  │ vmPFC ↑↑ suppress│ Balance        │ 5-HT2A disrupt   │
  │  amygdala        │                │  Layer V pyramids│
  │ Drive Mode: 6    │ Drive Mode:    │ Drive Mode: N/A  │
  │  (auto)          │  1-6           │  (modes break)   │
  │ Duration: chronic│ Duration:      │ Duration: hours   │
  │                  │  default       │                  │
  │ Therapeutic:     │                │ Therapeutic:     │
  │  re-connect body │                │  schema destabil.│
  │  (somatic therapy)│               │  + guided recomp.│
  └──────────────────┴────────────────┴──────────────────┘

  → Dissociation: QUÁ NHIỀU control → emotional emptiness
  → Psychedelic: QUÁ ÍT control → emotional flood
  → Normal PFC: CÂN BẰNG giữa 2 cực
  → = PFC = NOT just "on/off" — PFC = complex system with
    CONTROL DIMENSION + CONFIGURATION DIMENSION + PARTICIPATION DIMENSION
```

### §5b.3 — Dissociation = Drive Mode 6 weaponized (R12 key insight)

```
⭐ DISSOCIATION = MODE 6 OVERRIDE BỊ WEAPONIZE:

  Drive.md Mode 6 (Override) bình thường:
  → Deliberate (PFC chọn override)
  → Costly nhưng có mục đích
  → Temporary (kết thúc khi đạt mục tiêu)

  Dissociation = Mode 6 AUTOMATIC:
  → Body tự kích hoạt (không chọn)
  → Cost CỰC CAO (mất emotional processing)
  → CÓ THỂ CHRONIC (stuck in override)

  2 CHIẾN LƯỢC PHÒNG THỦ:
    Strategy A — Active (Fight/Flight):
      NE flood → PFC offline → amygdala rules → escape
      = PFC mode ④ Disconnected. 500M+ years.

    Strategy B — Passive (Freeze/Dissociate):
      PFC ramp up → suppress amygdala → disconnect from pain
      = PFC mode ⑤ Hyperactivated. Khi A fails (inescapable).

  LANIUS 2010 🟢: 2 trauma subtypes:
    → Re-experiencing: PFC hypoactive, amygdala hyperactive (Strategy A)
    → Dissociative: PFC hyperactive, amygdala suppressed (Strategy B)
    → Dissociative subtype MORE COMMON in early childhood trauma
    → = Strategy A failed (inescapable) → Strategy B compiled as default
```

### §5b.4 — Psychedelic = Schema Destabilization (R11 key insight)

```
⭐ PSYCHEDELIC STATE × FRAMEWORK:

  REBUS MODEL (Carhart-Harris & Friston 2019, 🟢):
  → "Relaxed Beliefs Under Psychedelics"
  → Normal brain: top-down priors CONSTRAIN bottom-up signals
  → Psychedelic: RELAX priors → bottom-up gets MORE weight
  → = Framework: compiled schemas temporarily LOSE constraint power

  DMN DISINTEGRATION:
  → DMN = "hệ điều hành của cái tôi" (self-schema + narrative + simulation)
  → Meditation: DMN SUPPRESSED → self-narrative quiets → peaceful
  → Psychedelic: DMN DISINTEGRATED → self-narrative dissolves → ego dissolution
  → = Qualitatively different: suppress (intact but quiet) vs disintegrate (collapse)

  CHUNK DYNAMICS CHẠY WILD:
  → Chunk-Shift: valence re-evaluate HÀNG LOẠT (schemas destabilized)
  → Chunk-Miss: baseline patterns fire KHÁC → continuous miss signals
  → Chunk-Gap: ACC detects EVERYWHERE (all patterns disrupted)
  → PFC coordination disrupted → 3 dynamics UNCOORDINATED
  → = TẠI SAO psychedelic = INTENSE (body-feedback overwhelm)

  THERAPEUTIC POTENTIAL:
  → Negative schemas (depression, addiction) temporarily lose constraint
  → New patterns CAN compile mà bình thường bị suppress
  → = "System reconsolidation" — schema landscape temporarily malleable
  → 🟢 Griffiths 2006: single session → lasting personality change
  → Set & setting: giữ destabilization trong Goldilocks zone (P4)

  TYPE A × PSYCHEDELIC: AFFECTED (evaluation disrupted, signals flood)
  TYPE B × PSYCHEDELIC: LESS AFFECTED (hardware-level, below disruption)
  → Touch, exercise = potentially STABLE across PFC states
```

---

## §6 — FLOW = H10 CONTINUOUS + LOẠI B + ZONE 2

### §6.1 — Flow prerequisites (framework terms)

```
⭐ FLOW = INTERSECTION CỦA NHIỀU PRECONDITIONS:

  ① LOẠI B COMPILED EXPERTISE (Compile-Taxonomy §2.2):
     → 10,000+ giờ → chunks compiled SÂU → run implicit
     → Expert KHÔNG CẦN PFC cho basic execution → PFC freed
     → Dietrich 2004: "skills in implicit system knowledge base"
     → = Prerequisite KHÔNG negotiate
     → Beginner KHÔNG THỂ flow (PFC busy với basic execution)

  ② ZONE 2 DISSONANCE (Domain-Mapping-Drive §3.1):
     → Goldilocks: challenge ~40-70% match skill
     → Zone 1 (quá dễ) → chán, PFC scatter → NO flow
     → Zone 3 (quá khó) → cortisol, PFC overwhelmed → NO flow
     → = Csikszentmihalyi "skill-challenge balance" 🟢
     → = H10 P4 (Goldilocks zone) SUSTAINED

  ③ H10 P1-P5 LIÊN TỤC MET:
     → P1: schema pending liên tục (task ongoing, never "xong")
     → P3: VTA delta continuous (micro-novelty mỗi bước)
     → P5: chunks opioid-tagged (compiled under curiosity/safety)
     → = Flow = chuỗi MICRO-OPIOID LIÊN TỤC
     → = Schema-Operations backup: "FLOW STATE = chuỗi micro-rewards
       ĐẶC BIỆT DÀI + ĐỀU"

  ④ PFC FULLY ALLOCATED (no interrupts):
     → Không bị interrupt (phone, người khác, noise)
     → Task complexity tận dụng hết ~4 slots
     → = Clear goals + immediate feedback (Csikszentmihalyi)

  → THIẾU BẤT KỲ → không flow:
     Thiếu expertise → PFC effortful → no smooth
     Thiếu challenge → PFC idle → scatter
     Thiếu opioid tag (P5) → task gây stress → no flow
     Bị interrupt → PFC context switch → flow breaks
```

### §6.2 — Flow reward mechanism

```
🟡 FLOW REWARD = CONTINUOUS MICRO-OPIOID STREAM:

  Normal reward: discrete event → H10 met once → opioid burst → done
  Flow reward: CONTINUOUS stream → H10 met REPEATEDLY → opioid stream

  MECHANISM:
    T₀: task step N → micro-novelty (P3) → VTA micro-delta
    T₁: body-base check → step fits schema (P1) → micro-opioid
    T₂: task step N+1 → new micro-novelty → VTA micro-delta
    T₃: body-base check → fits → micro-opioid
    ...repeat for HOURS...

  → Profile ② (coherence) SUSTAINED over time
  → = "Time flies" = PFC time-track OFF + continuous reward
  → = "Effortless" = Loại B compiled running + micro-opioid lubricating

  KHÁC eureka burst:
    Eureka: SINGLE massive opioid burst (accumulated P1 resolved)
    Flow: CONTINUOUS micro-opioid stream (P1 always partially pending)
    → Eureka = Profile ② PEAK
    → Flow = Profile ② SUSTAINED (lower intensity, longer duration)

  RESEARCH:
    → 🟢 Csikszentmihalyi: "autotelic experience" = intrinsically rewarding
    → 🟢 Opioid system active during flow states (endorphin release)
    → 🟡 Framework contribution: mechanism = H10 continuous met
```

---

## §7 — COHERENCE REWARD: ACC → OPIOID PIPELINE

### §7.1 — Decomposition: 3-4 components in < 1 second

```
🟡 INSIGHT REWARD = NHIỀU COMPONENTS CHỒNG LÊN NHAU:

  T₁ (~0-100ms): ACC detect coherence
    → ACC/insula detect: chunks fit together → "coherent"
    → = DETECTION, chưa phải reward
    → = Feeling-Sources §10: "rightness feeling"
    → = Feeling Gradient §7 position ④ (intuition, pre-verbal)

  T₂ (~100-300ms): Body-base check → opioid release
    → Schema pending (P1) resolved → body-need match → opioid
    → = REWARD THẬT (Step 5 trong 7-step)
    → = Kounios: reward signal ở orbitofrontal ~100ms after insight

  T₃ (~300-500ms): Cortisol drop (conditional)
    → NẾU trước đó có struggle/threat → cortisol DROP → RELIEF
    → NẾU không stress → NO relief component
    → = Eureka model §6.4: Archimedes (opioid + relief) vs
      Einstein (opioid only, no threat)

  T₄ (~500ms+): Multi-chunk cascade → compound opioid
    → Nhiều schemas liên quan fire → mỗi cái add opioid
    → = "Hàng loạt chunks liên kết" (Einstein case, 03-Reward §4.5.5)
    → = Compound: mỗi linked chunk = thêm 1 micro-reward

  PFC observe TẤT CẢ = 1 event → gọi "eureka!"
  Thực ra = 3-4 signals CHỒNG trong < 1 giây

  ⚠️ TIMING = hypothesis — exact ms chưa verified
  🟢 NHƯNG: Kounios ~100ms insight-to-reward = consistent
```

### §7.2 — Coherence vs Sensory: parallel comparison

```
🟡 SO SÁNH 2 PROFILES:

  ┌────────────────────┬────────────────────┬────────────────────────┐
  │ Dimension          │ ① Sensory          │ ② Coherence            │
  ├────────────────────┼────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ Input source       │ Sensory-Driven     │ Pattern-Driven         │
  │ Body location      │ Specific (miệng,   │ Diffuse ("đầu",       │
  │                    │   tai, mũi, da)    │   "ngực", "toàn thân")│
  │ ACC involvement    │ Low                │ HIGH (coherence core)  │
  │ Temporal profile   │ During stimulus    │ Burst → glow           │
  │ Replay fidelity    │ 20-60%             │ Higher (re-derive)     │
  │ Compulsive recheck │ No                 │ Yes (Wiles behavior)   │
  │ Certainty feeling  │ No                 │ Yes (Poincaré)         │
  │ Language           │ "ngon", "hay"      │ "đẹp", "elegant"      │
  │ Duration per event │ Minutes            │ Seconds → hours glow   │
  │ P1 requirement     │ Body-need (hunger) │ Schema-need (gap)      │
  │ P2 requirement     │ Basic receptors    │ Expert chunks library  │
  │ Motor response     │ Savoring, stillness│ Urgency to externalize │
  └────────────────────┴────────────────────┴────────────────────────┘

  MOTOR RESPONSE ĐẶC BIỆT:
    → Sensory reward → SAVORING: slow down, enjoy, linger
    → Coherence reward → URGENCY: Archimedes chạy, Hamilton khắc cầu,
      Wiles đi lại kiểm tra, Tesla vẽ xuống cát
    → = Pattern-driven insight tạo MOTOR URGENCY khác hẳn sensory
    → §7.3 drill sâu (v0.4 R4)
```

### §7.3 — Motor Urgency = Compound 3 Components (v0.4 new: R4 drill)

```
⭐⭐ R4 DRILL — MOTOR URGENCY REFINED:

  v0.2 hypothesis: "insight = fragile → urgency to externalize"
  v0.4 drill: Fragility hypothesis ĐÚNG nhưng CHƯA ĐỦ.
  Motor urgency = COMPOUND 3 COMPONENTS chồng lên nhau:


  ❶ FRAGILITY URGENCY (content-specific — preserve new pattern):

    Insight = NEW pattern connection, chưa compiled:
    → New links in working memory / short-term potentiation
    → Hebbian: new firing needs REPETITION to wire permanently
    → First-time insight = NOT YET strengthened by LTP
    → Working memory ~4 items (🟢 Cowan 2001) → interruption = LOST
    → Emotional peak CAN compile partially (Chunk.md §2 mechanism ②)
    → But FULL compile needs more (repetition, sleep consolidation)
    → = PARTIALLY compiled + NOT FULLY = fragile

    Motor response = EXTERNALIZE specific content:
    → Hamilton carved equations WITH A KNIFE on Broome Bridge
    → Tesla drew rotating magnetic field diagrams IN SAND
    → = External record = backup OUTSIDE brain
    → = Also adds modality (visual/motor) → strengthens compile
    → = Externalization BOTH preserves AND compiles

    🟢 Evidence — Gauss:
    → "Unable to say what was the conducting thread"
    → Result COMPILED (emotional peak → LTP), process LOST
    → = Process = unconscious Pattern-Driven → never in PFC → never compiled
    → = This IS fragility: content partially saved, process gone

    🟢 Evidence — McClintock:
    → "WITHOUT BEING ABLE TO KNOW what I was integrating, I understood"
    → Same pattern: result available, process opaque
    → = Process fragility = FEATURE of Pattern-Driven insight


  ❷ AROUSAL OVERFLOW (content-general — extreme reward → motor):

    Extreme dopamine + opioid + relief → body CAN'T be still:
    → Similar to: extreme joy → jumping, dancing
    → Heisenberg: could not sleep → climbed rock at dawn
    → Einstein: heart palpitations for DAYS
    → = Physiological arousal, NOT content-specific

    This component SHARED with any extreme reward,
    BUT stronger in insight due to COMPOUND:
    → Opioid (coherence confirmed) + Relief (④ years of P1)
      + Dopamine (massive VTA delta after long habituation)
    → = 3 reward signals STACK → arousal EXTREME


  ❸ VERIFICATION URGENCY (content-specific — confirm reality):

    "Is the pattern I found ACTUALLY coherent?"
    → ACC: reward signal fired BUT also UNCERTAINTY signal
    → Coherence CAN BE WRONG (false insight exists)
    → Body NOT YET fully confident gap is truly filled

    🟢 Evidence — Wiles:
    → "I'd keep coming back to my desk looking to see if it was still there"
    → For 20 minutes → compulsive RECHECK
    → NOT preservation (it's written down)
    → = VERIFICATION: "was I RIGHT?"

    🟢 Evidence — Poincaré:
    → "I FELT A PERFECT CERTAINTY" → BUT later verified anyway
    → Body felt certain, PFC demanded verification
    → = ACC certainty + PFC caution = compound

    Unique to coherence:
    → Sensory reward: CANNOT be wrong (taste = taste, no error possible)
    → Coherence reward: CAN be wrong (false insight, flawed proof)
    → = Verification drive = exclusively Profile ②


  ❶+❷+❸ FIRE SIMULTANEOUSLY → PFC observes as 1 "urgency" feeling.
  Each component individually INSUFFICIENT to explain full pattern.
  COMPOUND = why motor urgency feels SO distinctive.
```

```
⭐ SAVORING vs URGENCY — 3-COMPONENT COMPARISON:

  ┌────────────────────┬────────────────────┬────────────────────────┐
  │ Component          │ ① Sensory          │ ② Coherence            │
  ├────────────────────┼────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ ❶ Fragility        │ NO — stimulus      │ YES — pattern in       │
  │                    │ EXTERNAL, persists │ working memory, decays │
  │                    │ (food still there) │ (insight can be lost)  │
  ├────────────────────┼────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ ❷ Arousal          │ MODERATE — lower   │ HIGH — compound:       │
  │                    │ P1 pending (mins)  │ years P1 + massive δ   │
  │                    │                    │ + opioid + relief      │
  ├────────────────────┼────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ ❸ Verification     │ NO — sensory is    │ YES — coherence CAN    │
  │                    │ DIRECT, no error   │ be WRONG (false insight│
  │                    │ possible           │ exists, ACC uncertain) │
  ├────────────────────┼────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ Content to         │ NO — what to write │ YES — equations,       │
  │ externalize?       │ about food taste?  │ diagrams, proofs       │
  ├────────────────────┼────────────────────┼────────────────────────┤
  │ Motor response     │ SAVORING:          │ URGENCY:               │
  │                    │ slow, enjoy, linger│ externalize, recheck   │
  └────────────────────┴────────────────────┴────────────────────────┘


  TYPE A/B CONNECTION (v0.4 integration):

  Type B rewards: NO motor urgency
    → Touch → relax, melt into it
    → Exercise → continue, sustain
    → Warmth → linger, be still
    → = Hardware signal CANNOT be "wrong" → no verification
    → = Hardware pathway persists → no fragility

  Type A sensory: LOW motor urgency
    → Food, music → stimulus external + persistent
    → Fragility: NO. Verification: NO.
    → Only arousal (mild) → subtle motor (tapping foot to music)

  Type A coherence: HIGH motor urgency
    → Insight → stimulus INTERNAL + TRANSIENT + CAN BE WRONG
    → All 3 components active → COMPOUND urgency
    → = Profile ② SPECIFIC behavioral marker

  → Motor urgency = EXCLUSIVELY Type A + Pattern-Driven + Coherence
  → = Can distinguish Profile ② from ALL others by motor response alone


  FLOW vs EUREKA — URGENCY GRADIENT:

    Eureka: 1 massive insight → HIGH fragility + HIGH arousal + HIGH verification
      → INTENSE urgency (Hamilton carving, Archimedes running)

    Flow: many small insights → EACH low fragility + continuous arousal + low verification
      → SUSTAINED mild motor engagement (not urgency)
      → = "Effortless doing" ≠ "urgent externalization"
      → = Csikszentmihalyi: flow = smooth, not agitated

    → Motor urgency ∝ insight MAGNITUDE × insight NOVELTY
    → Large single insight = high urgency (eureka pattern)
    → Continuous small insights = low urgency (flow pattern)
    → = 2 modes of SAME coherence reward, different temporal profile


  🔴 TESTABLE PREDICTIONS:

    P-R4a: Insight motor urgency → CONTENT-SPECIFIC (write equations, draw)
           Pure arousal → CONTENT-GENERAL (pace, jump, can't sleep)
           → Distinguishable by: does motor activity contain information?

    P-R4b: Insight urgency DECREASES with recheck count
           (each verification → more compiled → less fragile → less urgent)
           → Wiles: 20 minutes recheck → eventually calms

    P-R4c: Flow motor response ≠ eureka motor response
           Flow = sustained smooth engagement
           Eureka = burst externalization + recheck
           → Same Profile ② but different temporal mode

    P-R4d: Expert reviewing OWN proof → less urgency than first discovery
           (already compiled, verified → fragility + verification both LOW)
           → Second reading of Wiles = calm, not urgent
```

## §8 — DEVELOPMENTAL PATH: CHILDHOOD P5 → ADULT REWARD CAPACITY

### §8.1 — Research foundation

```
🟢 CHILDHOOD COMPILE CONTEXT → ADULT REWARD + FLOW CAPACITY:

  Ryan & Deci (Self-Determination Theory, 2000, 2020):
    → Intrinsic motivation = foundation for flow
    → UNDERMINED by: controlling feedback, external pressure,
      performance-contingent rewards
    → PRESERVED by: autonomy-supportive environments
    → Children's intrinsic motivation typically DECLINES through adolescence

  Dietrich 2004:
    → Flow prerequisite: skills in IMPLICIT system
    → = Extensive practice transferred from explicit (PFC) to implicit
    → = Framework's Loại B compiled expertise

  Oudeyer et al. 2016 (computational models):
    → "Learning progress ITSELF generates motivation"
    → = Positive feedback loop: learn → opioid → want more → learn more
    → Early DISRUPTION of loop → impair self-reinforcing cycle

  Csikszentmihalyi:
    → "Autotelic personality": curiosity, persistence, low egotism,
      strong intrinsic motivation → more readily access flow
    → Partly CULTIVATED through early experiences
```

### §8.2 — Framework mapping

```
🟡 COMPILE CONTEXT → REWARD CAPACITY → FLOW CAPACITY:

  DEVELOPMENTAL CHAIN:

    Childhood P5 context:
      ┌──────────────────────┬──────────────────────┐
      │ Curiosity/Safety     │ Threat/Pressure       │
      │ (autonomy-supportive)│ (controlling)         │
      ├──────────────────────┼──────────────────────┤
      │ Opioid-tagged chunks │ Cortisol-tagged chunks│
      │ Approach direction   │ Avoidance direction   │
      │ Micro-opioid per step│ Relief-only at end    │
      │ "Thích học"          │ "Phải học"            │
      └──────────┬───────────┴──────────┬───────────┘
                 ↓                      ↓
    Adolescence:
      ┌──────────────────────┬──────────────────────┐
      │ Intrinsic motivation │ Extrinsic only        │
      │ PRESERVED → seek more│ DECLINING → avoid     │
      │ Deliberate practice  │ Forced practice       │
      │ → Loại B deep compile│ → Loại B BUT stressed │
      └──────────┬───────────┴──────────┬───────────┘
                 ↓                      ↓
    Adult:
      ┌──────────────────────┬──────────────────────┐
      │ Expert + opioid tag  │ Expert + cortisol tag │
      │ → FLOW accessible    │ → BURNOUT pattern     │
      │ Profile ② coherence  │ Profile ④ relief only │
      │ "Giỏi VÀ thích"     │ "Giỏi MÀ không thích"│
      │ Sustainable decades  │ Unsustainable → quit  │
      └──────────────────────┴──────────────────────┘

  → = "Talent" = early opioid-tagged exposure + hardware fit + years
  → = NOT random "talent gene" — NHƯNG hardware SEED vẫn có vai trò
    (DRD4, COMT, NE sensitivity → initial response to domain)
  → = Childhood environment × hardware → adult reward profile

  CROSS-REF:
    → Ryan & Deci SDT 🟢 = P5 mechanism expressed in psychology language
    → Oudeyer's learning loop = H10 micro-reward chain
    → Compile-Taxonomy §3 (4 pathways) = NGUỒN GỐC compile context
    → Education/Mechanism.md — pedagogy implications
```

## §8b — ABSTRACT ACTIVITY × BODY-BASE (v0.2 new)

### §8b.1 — Câu hỏi cốt lõi

```
⭐ "EINSTEIN GIẢI E=mc² → BODY-BASE ĐƯỢC FEED GÌ?"

  Physics equations không cho cơ thể ăn no, không làm da mát.
  Giải Sudoku, chứng minh định lý, vẽ tranh — không feed body-base trực tiếp.
  VẬY TẠI SAO body-base cho reward?

  Framework ĐÃ có answer (Gap-Direction §10):
  → 2 con đường serve body-base
  → Chain length gradient
  → "Feature, not bug" — evolution KEPT mechanism general
```

### §8b.2 — 2 con đường serve body-base (Gap-Direction §10.3)

```
🟡 CON ĐƯỜNG 1 — TRỰC TIẾP (internal state improve):

  Inconsistency trong world model → body "unsafe" → cortisol
  → ACC detect: "pattern không khớp" (KHÔNG phân biệt domain)
  → Resolve inconsistency → coherent → cortisol drop + reward signal
  → = Body-base state THẬT SỰ improve:
    ✅ Cortisol giảm (inconsistency resolved)
    ✅ Reward signal (coherence = "safe")
    ✅ Sleep cải thiện (less pending → less cortisol holding)
  → = Einstein feel better NGAY KHI derive E=mc², trước khi anyone knows
  → = Body KHÔNG cần hiểu content. Body chỉ cần "pattern khớp = tốt."

  Evolutionary basis (🟡):
  → ACC wired: detect inconsistency → danger (predator hành xử bất nhất)
  → Mechanism DOMAIN-GENERAL: ACC KHÔNG phân biệt [con mồi đi lạ] vs
    [Newton ≠ Maxwell]
  → = Extended application, NOT malfunction
  → = Hand evolved for grasping → ALSO used for writing, playing piano
  → 🟢 Bush, Luu, Posner 2000: ACC fires on conflict/error (general)


🟡 CON ĐƯỜNG 2 — GIÁN TIẾP (external outcome):

  Abstract work → expertise → recognition → status → resources
  → Einstein: E=mc² → fame → academic position → resources → body-base
  → = NHƯNG đây là CONSEQUENCE, không phải REASON body reward fires
  → Body reward fires VÌ con đường 1 (gap fill)
  → Con đường 2 = bonus, thường arrives LATER
```

### §8b.3 — Chain length gradient

```
🟡 TỪ TRỰC TIẾP → COMPILED COUPLING:

  ① TRỰC TIẾP (1 node):
     Ăn ngon → taste receptors → reward signal
     Ngồi bóng mát → thermoreceptors → relief signal
     = Body-input TRỰC TIẾP. Chó cũng có. Tier 1 evolutionary.

  ② PREVIEW (1-2 nodes):
     Tưởng tượng ăn ngon → body simulate → mini-reward (~20-60% fidelity)
     Tưởng tượng mua xe → preview body state → excitement
     = Pattern-Driven (BFM §2.3 ⓑ). PFC hold → body simulate.

  ③ COMPILED COUPLING (decades):
     Einstein tuổi trẻ: tò mò → Goldilocks → micro-reward
     → 1000x micro-reward → physics chunks COMPILED SÂU vào body
     → Physics inconsistency → Chunk-Gap detect → body dissonance THẬT
     → Resolve → body reward THẬT
     → Body KHÔNG hiểu E=mc². Nhưng body ĐÃ COMPILE:
       "physics coherence = good" qua decades of micro-rewards
     → = "Ảo thật" — virtual becomes real through compile

  ④ COLLECTIVE TRUST (1-2 nodes individual + long collective):
     Học sinh trust bố mẹ/collective → compile [học → tốt] (1-2 nodes)
     Chain dài [học → đại học → việc → lương] → NẰM Ở COLLECTIVE
     = Compile-Taxonomy §3: 4 pathways (Hardware Fit / Trust Install /
       Social Default / Threat Avoidance)
     = Collective-Body.md §1: "chain dài sống ở Cấp 2"
```

### §8b.4 — Multiple Discovery: collective gap → individual drive

```
🟢🟡 COLLECTIVE GAP TẠO CONVERGENCE POINTS:

  HIỆN TƯỢNG "MULTIPLE DISCOVERY" (Merton 1961, 🟢):

    Newton & Leibniz → Calculus (~1680s, ĐỘC LẬP)
    Darwin & Wallace → Evolution (1858, ĐỘC LẬP)
    Edison & Swan → Light bulb (~1879, ĐỘC LẬP)
    Bell & Gray → Telephone (1876, NỘP PATENT CÙNG NGÀY!)
    Hilbert & Einstein → General relativity (Nov 1915, CÙNG TUẦN!)
    Mendeleev & Meyer → Periodic table (1869, ĐỘC LẬP)

  Merton: simultaneous independent discovery = NORM, NOT exception.

  FRAMEWORK GIẢI THÍCH:
    ① Collective knowledge tích lũy (Tier 3 cultural chunks)
    ② Similar chunks → ACC detect similar inconsistency → shared gap direction
    ③ Multiple individuals independently detect + pursue
       (those with hardware fit + domain depth → cảm thấy "bứt rứt")
    ④ Timing ≈ simultaneous — vì cùng starting chunks + cùng gap + cùng tools

  → "Chưa biết = không có gap" (Gap-Direction §3):
    10,000 năm trước KHÔNG AI nghĩ tới thuyết tương đối
    → Collective CHƯA CÓ chunks [Newton] + [Maxwell]
    → Không có chunks xung quanh → không có bờ → KHÔNG CÓ GAP
    → Gap chỉ xuất hiện KHI collective tích lũy ĐỦ chunks


  DIVERSITY = SPECIALIZATION (🟡):
    → DRD4, COMT, NE variants → mỗi cá nhân KHÁC hardware
    → Compiled chunks khác → gap directions KHÁC
    → Mỗi người jump vào domain KHÁC
    → = Natural specialization WITHOUT central planning
    → Nếu 8 tỉ body-base cùng chỉ biết "ăn + bóng mát"
      → no specialization → no collective progress


  SỰ KIỆN HƯỚNG vs TIMING NGẪU NHIÊN:
    → HƯỚNG rõ: gap direction guide attention (Einstein Phase 0→3)
    → TIMING ngẫu nhiên: Background-Pattern + spreading activation
      = WHEN insight arrives = stochastic
    → Poincaré stepping onto omnibus, Kekule dozing, Penrose crossing street
    → PFC confabulate "tôi nghĩ tự do"
    → Body truth: gap direction + hardware fit ĐANG guide
```

### §8b.5 — Cases: reward cho cái "không ăn được"

```
🟡 CÁC VÍ DỤ "BODY-BASE KHÔNG ĂN ĐƯỢC" NHƯNG VẪN REWARD:

  ĐI TỪ THIỆN (Gap-Direction §10.5):
    → SPM fire → body SIMULATE recipient's need → body FEEL need
    → Cho đi → need resolved → SPM signal RELAX → reward
    → + Self-schema shift: "tôi = generous" → compile → reward
    → + Connection pathway ④: giving = reward (Connection.md §8)
    → Multiple reward channels OVERRIDE resource loss
    → "Mất tiền" ở PFC level. Body-base NET POSITIVE.

  BIẾU TRƯỞNG LÀNG:
    → Obligation compiled: "biếu = maintain access" (Obligation.md §1)
    → Con đường 2: status → resource access node → body-base indirectly
    → Threat avoidance: không biếu → risk exclusion → L0 threat
    → PFC sees cost. Body sees: relationship maintained = NET POSITIVE.

  THƯƠNG GIA CON ĐƯỜNG TƠ LỤA:
    → Compiled history: 100 lần [mua → chở → bán → lời]
    → Lúc MUA: body đã preview [bán → lời] → mini-reward
    → Chain cá nhân: chỉ 1-2 nodes [mua → sẽ bán được → tốt]
    → Trust past self → compile short → body reward ngay khi mua

  NGHỆ SĨ "STARVING ARTIST":
    → Con đường 1: mỗi creative step = mini gap fill → reward
    → Con đường 2: uncertain (fame IF successful)
    → Con đường 1 đủ strong → persist DÙ con đường 2 fail
    → = "Starving artist" = con đường 1 reward > resource loss

  GIẢI SUDOKU:
    → Con đường 1 thuần túy: mỗi ô fill = micro-reward
    → Con đường 2: gần như ZERO (no status, no resources)
    → = Abstract gap fill serve body-base TRỰC TIẾP
      without external outcome

  → TẤT CẢ cases: FRAMEWORK PRINCIPLE GIỮA VỮNG:
    "Mọi reward BUỘC phải serve body-base.
    Nhưng 'serve body-base' RỘNG hơn 'cho ăn'."
```

```
    → v0.3 suggested split Profile ① into ①a/①b → REJECTED

  GAP R14 ✅ DRILLED: Alliesthesia × Type B
    → v0.3 prediction "B less affected" = ĐÚNG but imprecise
    → v0.4 finding: 3 TYPES state dependence (not 1):
      ❶ Sensor-level (hardware/physics): Type B territory, cannot override
      ❷ Evaluation-level (classical alliesthesia/P1): Type A territory, partial override
      ❸ Gate-level (A modulates B): A×B interaction, contextual
    → Cabanac 1971 conflated ❶ and ❷ into one concept
    → Temperature = sensor-level MASQUERADING as evaluation-level
    → Framework refines: "B not affected by evaluation-level alliesthesia,
      B HAS sensor-level state dependence, B EXPERIENCE affected by A gate"
    → 3 types → 3 intervention strategies
    → 4 testable predictions (P-R14a through P-R14d)

  GAP R4 ✅ DRILLED: Motor urgency insight vs savoring sensory
    → Fragility hypothesis ĐÚNG nhưng CHƯA ĐỦ
    → Motor urgency = COMPOUND 3 components:
      ❶ Fragility urgency (content-specific: preserve before decay)
      ❷ Arousal overflow (content-general: extreme reward → motor)
      ❸ Verification urgency (content-specific: confirm reality)
    → Sensory lacks all 3 (external, persistent, cannot be wrong) → savoring
    → Exclusively Type A + Pattern-Driven + Coherence (Profile ②)
    → Flow vs eureka: urgency ∝ magnitude × novelty
    → Gauss + McClintock = process fragility evidence
    → 4 testable predictions (P-R4a through P-R4d)
    → REMAINING: no further drill needed, predictions await testing

  GAP R13 ✅ DRILLED: Type A/B boundary
    → 6 edge cases analyzed: spicy, social touch, dance, massage, sex, ASMR
    → Key insight: Input pathway ≠ Reward pathway
    → A Gates B mechanism formalized (3-step + evolutionary logic)
    → Boundary = spectrum (A/B ratio varies by modality + context)
    → NOT discrete categories — continuous dimension
    → REMAINING: R18 ✅ DRILLED (§3.13), R20 ✅ DRILLED (§3.11)

  GAP R19 ✅ DRILLED: Neonate sweet taste — A or B?
    → Sweet taste in neonates = Type A₀ (hardware-installed opioid evaluation)
    → NOT Type B: naltrexone BLOCKS sweet calming (Blass 1994) → opioid pathway
    → Type B = non-opioid (Loseth 2019: naltrexone no effect on touch) → sweet ≠ B
    → A₀ = simplest possible evaluation: binary taste receptor match → opioid
    → Evolution PRE-INSTALLED A₀ vì infant MUST evaluate food (life or death)
    → Type A refined: Complexity Gradient A₀→A₃
      A₀ (hardware binary) → A₁ (basic compiled) → A₂ (complex compiled) → A₃ (expert abstract)
    → A₀ PERSISTS in adult: layers A₁-A₃ BUILD ON TOP, not replace
    → Development: neonate 5% A₀ + 95% B → A₀ enriched gradually → A₁ → A₂ → A₃
    → Key distinction: A₀ = has evaluation (binary) + opioid. B = NO evaluation + non-opioid.
    → 4 testable predictions (P-R19a through P-R19d)
    → REMAINING: umami as possible A₀ (🔴 hypothesis)

  GAP R20 ✅ DRILLED: B habituation rate vs A
    → A habituates via VTA (central, uniform) — 🟢 Schultz 1997
    → B habituates via RECEPTOR ADAPTATION (peripheral, modality-specific)
    → B likely bypasses VTA → NO central habituation
    → CT dynamic touch: SLOW adaptation (designed for sustained contact)
    → Temperature: FAST adaptation (thermal physics)
    → Exercise eCB: SLOW adaptation (metabolic)
    → KHÔNG CÓ "B habituation rate" chung — each modality different
    → Comfort objects: B persists (no VTA), A-gate persists (compiled), novelty=0
    → Hedonic treadmill = primarily Type A phenomenon (VTA habituation)
    → B = "hedonic floor" — resistant to treadmill, democratic
    → 4 testable predictions (P-R20a through P-R20d)

  GAP R17 ✅ DRILLED: Preview fidelity × A/B
    → Preview fidelity = f(cortical proportion of total reward pathway)
    → Follows A₀→A₃ gradient: B ~5-15% < A₀ ~15-25% < A₁ ~25-40% < A₂ ~40-60% < A₃ ~60-80%
    → v0.4 "A ~40-60% vs B ~10-30%" = đúng hướng, A not monolithic
    → Core: preview activates CORTICAL, CANNOT activate PERIPHERAL
    → "Nhớ chocolate rõ hơn massage" = cortical proportion difference
    → Expert preview > novice preview (richer compiled chunks)
    → Wanting from preview (Berridge) → A more vulnerable to craving
    → B = "in the moment" reward, resistant to preview-driven seeking
    → "Apparent B preview" = actually A-component preview of B experience
    → 4 testable predictions (P-R17a through P-R17d)

  GAP R18 ✅ DRILLED: A Gates B — integration locus
    → NOT single anatomical location — GRADIENT PROCESS
    → = Posterior-to-anterior insula gradient (🟢 Craig 2002, 2013)
    → 5-step process:
      ❶ Posterior insula: B signal arrives (raw, ~0-50ms)
      ❷ A evaluation fires in parallel (cortical, ~50-200ms)
      ❸ Anterior insula: B + A integrate = EXPERIENCE (~100-300ms)
      ❹ ACC: conflict check — flags B/A mismatch (~200-400ms)
      ❺ OFC/vmPFC: value assignment (~300-500ms)
    → 4 outcomes mapped: amplify (friend), suppress (stranger), raw (infant), mixed (attracted stranger)
    → Insula maturation across lifespan MIRRORS A/B development gradient
    → Stranger anxiety (~8 months) ≈ anterior insula maturation
    → Framework scope note: neural mapping informative but BELOW framework abstraction
    → 4 testable predictions (P-R18a through P-R18d)

  GAP R5 ✅ DRILLED: Temporal profiles — precision
    → Onset latency = f(evaluation complexity), follows A₀→A₃ gradient:
      B ~20-100ms < A₀ ~100-300ms < A₁ ~200ms-1s < A₂ ~500ms-2s < A₃ ~1-5s
    → "First feel" = B or A₀. A₁-A₃ layers BUILD with delay.
    → Decay = f(mechanism type): B = receptor adaptation (modality-specific),
      A = VTA habituation + consolidation
    → A₃ afterglow EXCEPTIONALLY LONG = 4 overlapping curves:
      ❶ Opioid consolidation glow (hours-days)
      ❷ Relief compound from cortisol drop (days-weeks)
      ❸ Background processing cascade → micro-insights (hours-days)
      ❹ Verification loop → recheck → opioid pulses (minutes-hours)
    → Temporal Stack Model: experience = sum of overlapping profiles.
      Richness = number of active layers × overlap quality.
    → Duration = f(source_type × A/B × compound_layers × pending)
    → 4 testable predictions (P-R5a through P-R5d)

  GAP R7 ✅ DRILLED: Compound profiles — interaction model
    → NOT purely additive, multiplicative, or synergistic.
    → CONDITIONAL INTERACTION MODEL — depends on 4 variables:
      ① Substrate overlap: same (A+A) → SUBADDITIVE (ceiling).
         Different (A+B, B+B) → ADDITIVE to SUPERADDITIVE.
      ② A gate direction: positive → AMPLIFIES B. Negative → SUPPRESSES B.
         Absent → B raw. Conflicted → non-linear.
      ③ Relief presence: cortisol drop = SYSTEM-STATE MULTIPLIER (not additive).
         relief_factor = f(pending_duration × cortisol_drop).
      ④ Temporal overlap: simultaneous peak = maximum compound.
         Sequential = building. Asynchronous = phased.
    → BFM §4 additive model → REFINED to conditional model.
    → 6 edge cases (§3.7) re-analyzed — all fit conditional model.
    → R5↔R7 bridge: temporal overlap = 4th variable.
    → 4 testable predictions (P-R7a through P-R7d)

  GAP R15 ✅ DRILLED: System reconsolidation — individual vs system-level
    → CẢ HAI — system-level = EMERGENT PROPERTY
    → Individual reconsolidation: per-chunk, hierarchy pulls back → limited
    → System reconsolidation: hierarchy FLAT → topology can shift → lasting
    → 3-step mechanism: Destabilize → Reorganize → Consolidate
    → MIRROR of trauma compilation: same power, opposite direction
    → Compilation direction = f(set & setting → approach vs avoidance)
    → 4 conditions: sufficient destabilization + safe context +
      guided recompilation + consolidation
    → Goldilocks applies to destabilization degree (H10 P4)
    → Chunk dynamics run uncoordinated: Shift + Miss + Gap simultaneously
    → Anchor-Schema temporarily loosened → new anchor formation window
    → 4 testable predictions (P-R15a through P-R15d)

  GAP R16 ✅ DRILLED: Strategy A→B transition mechanism
    → A→B ≠ intensity threshold → ESCAPE POSSIBILITY ASSESSMENT
    → 3 variables: ① escape possibility ② compiled A outcome history
      ③ age at first trauma (developmental window)
    → Childhood (0-3): A physically impossible → B = ONLY option = FOUNDATION
    → Caregiver trauma = TRIPLE IMPOSSIBILITY:
      can't fight + can't flee + can't lose attachment
    → Body's "impossible solution": dissociate pain, maintain approach behavior
    → = Disorganized attachment (🟢 Main & Hesse 1990)
    → A and B = PARALLEL OPTIONS (same neurochemistry, different PFC config)
    → 4 hardware factors: HPA sensitivity + PFC-amygdala connectivity +
      vagal tone + epigenetic calibration
    → B→A reversion: possible but never complete (expand repertoire)
    → R15↔R16 bridge: system reconsolidation can address B at foundation level
    → 4 testable predictions (P-R16a through P-R16d)

  GAP R2 ✅ DRILLED: PFC sub-region × function × mode mapping
    → 3D mapping: 24 functions × 6 sub-regions × 2 taxonomies (many-to-many)
    → dlPFC = HUB serving 15/24 functions → bottleneck
    → ACC = 8/24 quality controller, vmPFC = 6/24 emotional bridge
    → OFC = 5/24 value computer, mPFC = 5/24 self+social, vlPFC = 3/24 inhibition

    → Config ⑥ × ⑭ Modify Chunks = system reconsolidation mechanism

      R2↔R5 (onset = sub-region pipeline), R2↔R7 (A Gate B = pipeline)
    → 4 testable predictions (P-R2a through P-R2d)

    → CONFIRMED: 🟢 Zeki 2014 — mOFC activation shared across math/art/music beauty
    → Beauty = H10 P4 operating on ANY domain's chunks (not separate faculty)
    → Same mechanism (ACC → mOFC → opioid), different input pathways

    → P2 = BEAUTY GATE: no chunks = no beauty experience
    → Accessibility gradient: visual(A₁) > music(A₁-A₂) > literary(A₂) > math(A₃)
    → "Subliminal selection by beauty" (Poincaré) = H10 in background processing
    → ② cross-domain priming: music ② warms ACC → physics insight ↑
    → 8 historical figures analyzed: all show cross-domain ② hobbies

      Hardware(ceiling) × Childhood(direction) × Exposure(where) × Balance(dominance)

  GAP R6 ✅ DRILLED: Developmental data — childhood P5 → adult reward capacity
    → 6 converging evidence lines:
      🟢 Ryan & Deci SDT (autonomy-supportive → preserved intrinsic motivation)
      🟢 Harter 1981, 1992 (intrinsic orientation → academic persistence years later)
      🟢 Lepper, Greene & Nisbitt 1973 (overjustification = P5 tag overwrite)
      🟢 Mueller & Dweck 1998 (praise type → P5 tag direction)
      🟢 Sroufe et al. 2005 (Minnesota 30+ years: attachment → competence)
      🟡 Oudeyer et al. 2016 (learning progress = H10 micro-reward chain)
    → 4-Pathway × P5 Tag Model (Compile-Taxonomy §3 integration):
      ① HW Fit → approach tag → ② coherence natural, flow accessible
      ② Trust Install → moderate approach → depends on collective chain
      ③ Social Default → weak/neutral tag → ④ relief dominant
      ④ Threat Avoidance → avoidance tag → ④ relief ONLY, burnout trajectory
    → 4 Sensitive Periods (NOT critical — reconsolidation still possible):
      Window 1 (0-3): Foundation, B dominant, attachment = P5 FOUNDATION tag
      Window 2 (3-7): Exploration, approach/avoidance tags compile en masse
      Window 3 (7-12): Deepening, school threat vs novelty DIVERGES
      Window 4 (12-18): Identity, P5 tags consolidate into Anchor-Schema
    → Compound Tag Accumulation Model:
      NET tag = Σ(approach) - Σ(avoidance) × f(peak_weight)
      Asymmetry: negative peak > positive peak per event (evolutionary)
      Bidirectional snowball: approach→seek→compile→more approach
        AND avoidance→avoid→no compile→tag stays
    → Overjustification = P5 Tag Overwrite (Lepper 1973 in framework terms)
    → Cross-refs: Compile-Taxonomy §3, Child-Dev-Mechanism §2-§3, §3.8
    → 4 testable predictions (P-R6a through P-R6d)

  GAP R8 ✅ DRILLED: Individual differences — hardware × reward profile sensitivity
    → 5-Axis Model for Individual Reward Profile
      (generalizing R3's 4-factor model to ALL 5 profiles):
      ① Hardware Architecture (genetic: COMT, DRD4, MAO-A, NE, μ-opioid)
      ② Childhood Compilation (P5 tags, attachment — very hard to change)
      ③ Domain Exposure (where reward expresses — changeable via education)
      ④ Channel Balance (how dominant one profile becomes — partially changeable)
      ⑤ Current State (cortisol, sleep, social context — most malleable)
    → 4 Receptor Systems × 5 Profiles mapping:
      COMT: HIGH on ② (clear speed → insight duration), LOW on ① sensory
      DRD4 (Hyp D): HIGH on ② (chunk threshold → "AHA" vs "ồ"), LOW on ①
      MAO-A: HIGH on ③ social (mood stability) and ④ relief
      NE α2/α1: HIGH on ② (PFC stability → flow access) and ④ relief
      μ-Opioid: HIGHEST on ① sensory, HIGH on ② and ③
    → Type B = "democratic reward" — LESS affected by hardware variation
      (non-opioid, non-PFC dependent → hardware ceiling less constraining)
    → COMT × Reward Pattern (extending PFC-Hardware from cognition to reward):
      Val/Val: MANY shallow insights, SHORT afterglow, cross-domain NATURAL, flow HARDER
      Met/Met: FEWER DEEPER insights, LONG afterglow, cross-domain HARDER, flow EASIER
      "Bored because draft clears" vs "stuck because draft won't clear"
    → COMT × DRD4 Interaction (4 combos):
      Val/Val + 7R = "Thrill seeker" (need novel BIG experiences)
      Met/Met + 4R = "Obsessive expert" (satisfy within single domain)
      Val/Val + 4R = "Social butterfly" (many small rewards, none deep)
      Met/Met + 7R = "Frustrated genius or true genius" (BIMODAL)
    → COMT × Childhood Compilation (4 combos):
      Met/Met + approach = DEEP FLOW expert (best case)
      Met/Met + avoidance = RIGID ANXIETY (worst combination)
      Val/Val + approach = CREATIVE EXPLORER
      Val/Val + avoidance = SCATTERED ANXIETY
    → 4 Departure Patterns from §3.8 average:
      ① Precocious A (child prodigy), ② Extended B (athletes),
      ③ Arrested A (most common education failure), ④ Reversed A/B (burnout)
    → 3-Variable Shorthand: A/B Ratio × Dominant Profile × Breadth
    → Cross-refs: PFC-Hardware.md §1-§6, §3.8, §3.19 4-factor model
    → 4 testable predictions (P-R8a through P-R8d)

  ═══════════════════════════════════════
  RESOLVED in v0.3
  ═══════════════════════════════════════

  GAP R9 ✅ RESOLVED: Touch reward pathway
    → = Type B Direct State Confirm (CT afferents → posterior insula)
    → Non-opioid = NOT contradiction — different TYPE of reward signal
    → Connection: body-oriented therapy for trauma (bypass PFC)

  GAP R10 ✅ RESOLVED: Endocannabinoid × opioid relationship
    → = Multi-role: Amplifier in Type A (dependent on opioid)
      + Primary in Type B exercise (independent of opioid)
    → Cùng molecule, khác circuit, khác function
    → Consistent with Neurochemical Multi-Role Principle

  GAP R11 ✅ DRILLED: Psychedelic ego dissolution
    → = DMN DISINTEGRATION (not suppression) → schema destabilization
    → REBUS = "compiled schemas lose constraint power"
    → PFC mode ⑥ Disintegrated. Drive modes break down.
    → Chunk dynamics run WILD (uncoordinated)
    → Therapeutic: system reconsolidation window
    → REMAINING: R15 (system reconsolidation mechanism)

  GAP R12 ✅ DRILLED: Dissociation
    → = PFC HYPERACTIVATION (mode ⑤) — OPPOSITE of threat
    → = Drive Mode 6 (Override) weaponized by body automatically
    → 2 defense strategies: Active (A→④) vs Passive (B→⑤)
    → PFC Control Spectrum: Overcontrol ↔ Balanced ↔ Undercontrol
    → REMAINING: R16 (A→B transition mechanism)
```

## §11 — HONEST ASSESSMENT (v1.2 updated)

```
⭐ ĐÁNH GIÁ TRUNG THỰC (v1.2 updated):

  🟢 STRONG (research-backed):
    → Opioid = primary reward signal cho Type A evaluative (food, music,
      sex, insight) — Berridge, NAcc studies, Mallik 2017, Tik 2020
    → Touch = Type B Direct State (Loseth 2019: naltrexone no effect)
    → CT afferents → posterior insula (Löken 2009) = interoceptive pathway
    → Exercise euphoria = endocannabinoid, NOT opioid (Fuss 2015, Siebers 2021)
    → eCB in NAcc hotspot dependent on opioid (Stacey 2018) — multi-role
    → DLPFC deactivates during flow (Limb & Braun 2008)
    → PFC judgment + amygdala off during limerence (Bartels & Zeki)
    → Psychedelic = DMN disintegration (Carhart-Harris 2012, Tagliazucchi 2016)
    → REBUS: compiled schemas temporarily relaxed (Carhart-Harris & Friston 2019)
    → Dissociation = PFC hyperactivation, amygdala suppressed (Lanius 2010)
    → 2 trauma subtypes: re-experiencing vs dissociative (Lanius 2010)
    → Intrinsic motivation undermined by pressure (Ryan & Deci)
    → Multiple Discovery = norm (Merton 1961)
    → Neural reuse principle (Anderson 2010) supports multi-role
    → Stranger touch aversion despite CT pleasantness (social gating, multiple studies)
    → Neonate touch comfort = hardware-level (attachment research 🟢)
    → Neonate sweet → opioid calming (Blass & Hoffmeyer 1991) (v0.5)
    → Naltrexone reduces sweet calming in neonates (Blass 1994) (v0.5)
    → Gustofacial reflexes subcortical (Steiner 1973, anencephalic data) (v0.5)
    → Decorticated rats still show sweet hedonic reactions (Berridge 2003) (v0.5)
    → Visual/motor imagery uses same cortex (Kosslyn 1994, Jeannerod 1995)
    → Working memory ~4 items capacity (Cowan 2001)
    → Motor urgency in expert insight accounts (multiple independent sources)
    → Craig 2002, 2013: posterior-to-anterior insula interoceptive gradient (v0.6)
    → Botvinick et al. 2004: ACC conflict monitoring (v0.6)
    → Singer et al. 2004: anterior insula in empathy for pain (v0.6)
    → Brickman & Campbell 1971: hedonic adaptation/treadmill (v0.6)
    → Thermal adaptation: well-established sensory physiology (v0.6)
    → McGaugh 2000: memory consolidation timescales (v0.7)
    → Walker 2017: sleep-dependent consolidation (v0.7)
    → Collins & Loftus 1975: spreading activation (v0.7)
    → Peciña & Berridge 2005: hedonic hotspot ~1mm³ finite capacity (v0.7)
    → Nader et al. 2000: individual memory reconsolidation (v0.8)
    → Main & Hesse 1990: disorganized attachment (v0.8)
    → Van der Kolk 2014: body-oriented therapy for trauma (v0.8)
    → Yehuda 2016: transgenerational cortisol calibration (v0.8)
    → Goldman-Rakic 1995: dlPFC working memory (v0.9)
    → Fuster 1973: dlPFC sustained activity (v0.9)

    → Ishizu & Zeki 2011: visual beauty → mOFC activation (v1.0)
    → Blood & Zatorre 2001: musical chills → ventral striatum + mOFC (v1.0)
    → O'Doherty et al. 2003: facial beauty → OFC activation (v1.0)
    → Poincaré 1908: Science and Method — "same nature" claim (v1.0)
    → Sroufe et al. 2005: Minnesota Longitudinal Study 30+ years
      (attachment → competence/relationships across lifespan) (v1.2)
    → Harter 1981, 1992: intrinsic orientation predicts academic persistence
      years later (longitudinal, childhood → adolescent) (v1.2)
    → Lepper, Greene & Nisbitt 1973: overjustification effect
      (external reward → intrinsic motivation decrease) (v1.2)
    → Mueller & Dweck 1998: praise type → achievement motivation direction
      ("smart" → performance avoid, "effort" → mastery approach) (v1.2)
```
